Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da kosiron ɨmalni yalɨwit. Aŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ da kɨŋ kɨndap kɨlɨŋ mandaŋ paŋobɨŋ kosiron yalɨwit
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni da obɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gen on yaŋaki Parisi amɨn dakon but yokwi toŋ gak uŋun dɨ nandɨsal, bo dɨma?”
Ji butji sigɨn pakyaŋsi dɨma nandaŋ pɨsoŋ, ma? Nak bret 5 kabɨ baŋ amɨn 5 tausen do yobo naŋakwa dɨwarɨ yɨk morapmɨ sɨmɨlba tugawit ji uŋun do si ɨŋtoŋ?
“Nak pɨŋek gen dɨma yoyɨgɨm tam, yokwini dakon gen kɨnda dɨma tosok. Mani nak pɨŋek gen kɨlɨ yoyɨgɨm, do amɨn kɨnda da ‘nak dɨma nandaŋek suŋ agɨm’ yaŋ yogogɨ mɨni.
ae Saimon (uŋun kalɨp Selot da kabɨkon egɨpgut), ae Judas Iskariot. (Judas uŋun da don Yesu uwal da kɨsiron yɨpgut.)
Yaŋ nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn kɨla amɨni dɨ gat ae emat amɨni dɨ gat tɨmɨkban tɨmtɨm yaŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨkon pɨgɨwit. Pɨgakwa amɨn da emat amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat ae emat amɨni gat pɨndagek Pol saŋbeŋek dɨma aŋakgwit.
Mani nak asi pini asat. Yaŋdo, ji geno do nandaba bamɨ dɨma asak kaŋ, pi asat uŋun kaŋek nandaŋ gadat ani. Aŋek yaŋsi nandani, Dat uŋun nagon egɨsak ae nak Daron egɨsat.”
Dat da Monji but dasi galak taŋ ɨmɨŋek yo morap kɨlani asak do uŋun da kɨsiron yopgut.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn on bɨsapmon ekwaŋ uŋun amɨn yokwisi gɨn. Piŋkop dakon pi naŋ asat yaŋ nandak do wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda kok do yoŋ. Mani kɨnda dɨma kokdaŋ. Kombɨ amɨn Jona dakon tɨlak naŋgɨn kokdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn kɨsi yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda nak nol do nandɨsak kaŋ, iyɨ dakon galaktok manji yomɨŋek tɨlak kɨndapni gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ guramɨgek nak noljak.
Mani Yesu Jerusalem kɨkdɨsak yaŋ nandawit, do uŋun kokupmon amɨn da Yesu abɨdok do dɨma galak tawit.
Yaŋ yaŋakwan uŋudon gɨn pup gen yaŋban kosit bamot agɨt. Yaŋban nandaŋek Pita Yesu da gen yagɨt uŋun do nandagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak dakon man kosit kapbɨ wasɨp yaŋaki pup da kosit bamot gen yosak.” Gen uŋun do nandaŋek burɨ yokwi taŋban kunam madepsi takgɨt.
Amɨn yoyɨki kaŋ yaŋ gayɨkdaŋ, nak Piŋkop gawak ɨm do aŋek Jerusalem kɨŋ altaŋek gɨldat 12 kabɨ egɨpgum.
Yaŋ yaŋba burɨ yokwi taŋban yaŋba kɨk aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Apmiap amɨn ekwaŋ nido wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda kok do yoŋ? Nak asisi dayɨsat, wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda dɨma koni, dɨmasi.”
Wɨgɨ pakbi ɨdapmon kɨŋakwa tepmɨsi mɨrɨm madepsi da abɨŋ pakbi tamalɨgakwan boron pɨgɨwit. Yaŋ aŋakwan Yesu dɨpmɨn pagakwan
Iyɨŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Ji takis gapman da dayɨsak uŋun da arɨpmon gɨn tɨmɨtni. Ae saŋbeŋek dɨ gat dɨma tɨmɨtni.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon bulmakau wup kɨnda kokup kɨdatni wasawit. Wasaŋek paret aŋek kɨsit da yo wasawit do kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋakwa Piŋkop da manji yomɨŋek gɨk kanek gɨldatyo gawak yomni do bɨkbɨk yomgut. Kombɨ amɨn da papiakon gen tosok uŋun da tɨlagon yo yokwi awit. Gen uŋun yaŋ tosok: ‘Israel amɨn ji mɨktɨm kɨbɨrɨ tɨmon bɨlak 40 egek bulmakau ae sipsip dapmaŋek mukwa sowit, uŋun nak do awit? Uŋun dɨmasi.
“Gak Sunduk dakon monji. Gak aŋpak tagɨsi morap toŋ uŋun dakon uwalni. Top gen yogok mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ gat ae aŋpak yokwi morap uŋun gagon tugosok. Gak da Amɨn Tagɨ dakon aŋpak kɨlegɨsi paŋ upbal asal. Yokwi morap asal uŋun dɨma yopbi, ma?”
Sadyusi amɨn da Yesu aŋkewal do iyɨŋba gen tagɨsi yaŋakwan kobogɨ iyɨk do dɨma nandawit. Parisi amɨn da uŋun nandaŋek Yesukon opgwit.
Stiwen yaŋ yaŋek ŋwakbeŋ aŋek yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, yokwini dakon kobogɨ dɨma yobi.” Stiwen yaŋ yaŋek kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋ aŋakwa Juda amɨn da amɨn bamot do nandaba yokwi tok aŋ yomgwit. Yaŋ nandaŋek maket tamokon pɨdok amɨn dɨ egɨpgwit uŋun tɨmɨkba uŋun gat amɨn morapmɨ paŋmuwuk burɨ sugaŋba upbalap madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek amɨn kɨnda mani Jeson uŋun da yutnon kɨŋ Pol gat Sailas gat wɨsɨŋ tɨmɨk amɨn morap da ɨŋamon pabɨgɨ yopneŋ yaŋ yaŋek kɨwit.
“Uŋun Moses dagɨn Israel amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Piŋkop da nak aŋalon aŋ nepgut yaŋ gɨn ji kabɨkon naŋ kombɨ amɨn kɨnda don aŋalon aŋ damjak.’
Kalɨp Moses da yaŋ yagɨt: ‘Amɨn Tagɨsi Piŋkop da don ji kabɨkon amɨn kɨnda aŋnoman aban kombɨ amɨn nak yombem egɨpjak. Uŋun amɨn da gen morap dayɨsak uŋun pakyaŋsi nandani.
“Nayɨŋban kobogɨ yaŋ yagɨm, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ, arɨpmɨ dɨmasi dapmaŋ nokeŋ. Nak bɨsap kɨndakon jap kɨnda Juda amɨn da gen tebanon dɨma noknogɨ kɨnda dɨmasi nagɨm.’
Mani butnikon gelɨ tagɨ dɨma yɨpban kɨgɨt, do bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok akdak. Jɨgɨ mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ altaŋ ɨmni ae Piŋkop dakon gen dakon uwal apni bɨsapmon nandaŋ gadatni yɨpban wɨtdal kɨsak.
Aŋkɨ yɨpmaŋek top amɨn dɨ kokwinɨk yopba sɨtnok aŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ yawit, “On amɨn bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ Telagɨ Yut Madep gat ae gen teban Moses da mandagɨt gat do yaŋba yokwi tok asak.
“Nak yaŋsi dayɨsat, uŋun kalbi amɨn bamorɨ dɨpmɨn pagakwal Piŋkop da kɨnda abɨdaŋek kɨnda yɨpdɨsak.
Uŋun kabɨkon kɨnda mani Maria, kokupni Makdala. Ae Maria ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda Jems gat Josep gat dakon meŋi. Ae Sebedi dakon monjɨ bamot uŋun dakon meŋi kɨsi akgwit.
Parisi amɨn gat ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat da Yesu Sabat bɨsapmon amɨn paŋmɨlɨp aban kaŋek gen yaŋ ɨmneŋ yaŋ do kaŋ egɨpgwit.
“Dat kabɨ, ji kabɨkon da monjɨsi kɨnda da tap kɨlap do dayɨŋban tuŋon amɨn emarɨ toŋ kɨnda tagɨ ɨmni?
Nin kokup pap Miletus uŋudon egek Pol da Epesas paŋmuwukbi dakon kɨla amɨn opni do gen yɨpban kɨgɨt.
Yesukon altaŋek ɨmalni ɨlɨk donki bɨlagɨ da kwenon yopmaŋakwal Yesu pawɨgɨ uŋudon yɨkgɨt.
Yaŋban Pita da uŋun gen nandaŋek Yesu ɨleŋɨkon aŋkɨ tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ! Uŋun yo morap dɨmasi altaŋ gamni!”
Bumjotni dukwan tosok yaŋ nandaŋek but morap aŋek egakwa uŋudon gɨn amɨn bamorɨ kapmatjok altaŋek akbal pɨndakgwit. Uŋun dakon ɨmalni da mal dakon teŋteŋɨ yombem madepsi teŋteŋawit.
Amɨn morap telagɨ pakbi soŋakwa Yesu yo kɨsi sogɨt. Soŋek bɨsit aŋakwan kundu wɨtdal kɨgɨt.
Kɨŋ Sisaria kokup papmon altaŋek uŋudon da Jerusalem wɨgɨ paŋmuwukbi gɨldat tagɨ yaŋ yoyɨŋek Antiok kokup papmon pɨgɨgɨt.
“Yoban bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok egek monji buŋon nani da yo kabɨni kɨsisi tɨmɨk dubagɨsi kɨŋ mɨktɨm kɨndakon paŋkɨ egɨpgut. Paŋkɨ egek aŋpak yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ aŋek moneŋni naŋ mudagɨt.
Ae maket tamokon da tobɨlek obɨŋ yaŋ gɨn kɨsirɨ sugaŋek jap noŋ. Uŋun gɨn dɨma, gen teban morapmɨ yolek kap, kwoba, ɨdapyo kɨsi sugoŋ.
Maria gen uŋun nandaŋek tepmɨsi pɨdaŋ Yesu kok do kɨgɨt.
Wɨli 5 tausen da jap nawit. Ae mɨŋat monjɨyo jap nawit uŋun dɨma manjɨkbi.
Do iyɨ gɨn gen emat aŋek si kɨwit. Mani dɨma kɨŋakwa Pol da mibɨ gen kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Telagɨ Wup da kombɨ amɨn Aisaia aŋtagap aban babɨkji do gen bamɨsi kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt:
Agripa da Pol yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Bɨkbɨk gabo gaga do gen ya.” Iyɨŋban mɨrak yopni do Pol kɨsirɨ aŋenagek iyɨ kutnok do gen yaŋ yagɨt,
Datno nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun dakon galaktok uŋun yaŋ: Nak Datno da amɨn kɨlɨ namgut uŋun kɨnda dɨma yɨpbo pasɨljak. Mibɨ gɨldaron kɨsisi pabo pɨdoni.
Mani koŋ da genji guramɨkgaŋ, uŋun do kɨsɨk kɨsɨk dɨma ani. Ji dakon man Kwen Kokupmon mandabi da toŋ, uŋun do nandaŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ani.”
Yaŋ dayɨgɨt, ‘Amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji yokwi pakpak da kɨsiron yɨpba tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Ae gɨldat kapbɨ egɨ mudaŋek aeni pɨdokdɨsak.’ ”
Dɨwarɨ da kokup dubagɨkon da apgwit, do yabekgo kɨni kaŋ, kosiron jap do aŋek dabɨlɨ upbal taŋba maŋ potdaŋ.”
Gen morap uŋun do kalɨp kombɨ amɨn da papiakon kɨlɨ mandawit uŋun da arɨpmon aŋ mudawit. Yaŋ aŋek bumjotni don tɨlak kɨndapmon naŋ kukwaŋ aŋkɨ kɨmakbi tamokon yɨpgwit.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ pasɨlɨ tosok uŋun ji da tagɨ nandani do Piŋkop da nandɨsak, mani uŋun amɨn do dɨma yolɨsak.
“Nak amɨn pakbisi baŋ telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomɨsat uŋun amɨn but tobɨl bamɨ aŋ dakon tɨlak asak. Mani nak da manjikon abɨsak amɨn uŋun dakon tapmɨm da nak dakon tapmɨm yapmaŋdak. Nak yombem yokwi da kandap gwɨlni tagɨ dɨma abɨdaŋ awɨlɨ. Uŋun amɨn da Telagɨ Wup gat ae kɨndap gat soŋ damdɨsak.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da nak Israel amɨn sipsip kabɨni pasɨlbi uŋun baŋgɨn paŋpulugokeŋ do yabekgɨt.”
Nandani! Dat da yo dam do yaŋ teban tok agɨt uŋun nak da jikon yabetdɨsat. Ji tepmɨ dɨma kɨŋek kokup papmon egakwa Piŋkop dakon tapmɨm Kwen Kokup da jikon pɨkdɨsak.”
Iyɨŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak da ninaŋ abeŋ do nandɨsal?” Iyɨŋban yaŋ yagɨt, “Gak kɨla amɨn madep egɨpbi bɨsapmon on monjɨ bamotno man madep paŋek kɨnda da gak da amɨn tet do ae kɨnda da gwandeŋ tet do yɨtjil do yaŋ dagok aŋyobi do nandɨsat.”
Emat amɨn da Yesu tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋagek ɨmalni tɨmɨkgwit. Tɨmɨgek kokwin 4 kabɨ aŋakwa kaloŋ kaloŋ da ɨmalni kaloŋ kaloŋ tɨmɨkgwit. Ae paba pɨgɨk dubakni kɨsi abɨdawit. Paba pɨgɨkni saŋbekni uŋun mɨni ɨmal dɨwat kaloŋɨ naŋ bupbi kawit.
Ae bret 7 kabɨ baŋ amɨn 4 tausen do yobo naŋakwa dɨwarɨ yɨk morapmɨ sɨmɨlba tugawit ji uŋun do si ɨŋtoŋ?
Kɨlɨ Yesu Tair kokup yɨpmaŋek Saidon kokup kɨŋ yapmaŋek Dekapolis mɨktɨm uŋun kɨsi yapmaŋek Galili Pakbi Ɨdap uŋudon kɨgɨt.
Do pi yopbeŋ bɨsapmon amɨn da but galagon da yaŋ naba yutnikon kɨŋ kɨŋ akeŋ do niaŋ abeŋ uŋun kɨlɨ uŋun nandɨsat.’
Aŋakwa aŋelo da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji dɨma pasolni. Nandani, nak gen tagɨsi kɨnda aŋabɨsat. Uŋun amɨn kɨsi da nandaŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi akdaŋ.
Pol da amɨn kɨmoron da pɨdoni do yaŋban amɨn dɨwarɨ da jɨgɨlak gen yaŋ ɨmgwit. Mani dɨwarɨ da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yo uŋun yosol uŋun do dɨ gat niyɨŋbɨ nandaneŋ do nandamaŋ.”
Nak Sonda kɨnda da butgwan bɨsap bamot gak do nandaŋek jap kelek egɨ egɨ asat. Ae yo morap tɨmɨkdat uŋun kokwinɨkgo 10 kabɨ aŋakwa kabi kɨnda paret do yɨpmaŋ yɨpmaŋ asat.’
Mani Yesu da uŋun jamba but amɨn yaŋ nandaŋ yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido nak aŋkewalgaŋ? Moneŋ tabɨlɨ kɨnda aŋabɨŋ naba koko.”
Meŋi datniyo kaŋ wɨrɨpdagek meŋi da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Monjɨ, gak nido yaŋ aŋaki wusamak? Datgo gat nit gak do nandaba kɨk aŋek wusamak.”
Yaŋakwan Kwen Kokup aŋelo kɨnda da pɨŋ Yesu aŋteban agɨt.
Aŋek Yesu da aŋpulugosak do madepsi yaŋ iyɨwit, “Uŋun amɨn tagɨsi, do geni nandaŋek kɨŋ oman monjɨni aŋpulugoki.
“Nak Juda amɨn kɨnda. Meŋno da Tasas kokup pap Silisia mɨktɨmon tosok uŋudon aŋalagɨt. Mani nak on kokup papmon tagagɨm. Yoyɨŋdetno Gamaliel uŋun da nak babɨknin dakon gen teban morap tagɨsi nayɨŋ dekgɨt. Ji Piŋkop dakon pi but dasi aŋ, nakyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn aŋ kɨmakgɨm.
Aŋakwa pɨndagek Parisi amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Pɨndat, paŋdet kabɨgo Sabat bɨsapmon nido gen teban yapmaŋek pi aŋ?”
Bret Yisni Mɨni Bɨlak wasok wasogɨkon paŋdetni da Yesukon kɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin kɨŋ dukwan Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap paŋkosit aneŋ do nandɨsal?”
Mani ji dɨsi dakon gen monɨŋ monɨŋ ae man ae gen tebanji do yoŋ. Nak uŋuden gen do gen pi ak do dɨma galak tosot. Dɨsi yaŋ paŋmɨlɨp abɨt.”
Aban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Gak emat agak sɨbago yɨgɨkon sɨmɨl. Emat agak sɨba pawɨlgaŋ amɨn uŋun emat agak sɨba da mandaŋ yoba kɨmokgoŋ.
Yaŋ iyɨŋban Konilias gat gen yaŋek yutnon wɨgɨ pɨndakban amɨn morapmɨsi muwukgwit.
Mani Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop dakon papia da gen kɨnda gat yaŋ yosok, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ Piŋkopji dakon tapmɨm kok do aŋek dɨmasi aŋkewaldo.’ ”
Tɨmɨgek maba kɨndap tebanon pɨgek uŋungwan kunam tagek iyoŋ iyoŋ yaŋek egɨpdaŋ.”
Yaŋban koŋ da madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek monjɨ uŋun maban bumjot yombem pagakwan koŋ yɨpmaŋek wɨŋ kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da monjɨ kaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Kuŋwakni.”
Iyɨŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Gɨldat pɨgɨk do aŋakwan ji yaŋ yoŋ, ‘Kwen gami asak, do aŋwa bɨsap tagɨsi.’
Sabat bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgek yoyɨŋdet agɨt. Uŋudon amɨn kɨsirɨ amɨnsi tetni gɨreŋɨkbi kɨnda egɨpgut.
Yaŋ aba pi ami da aeni oman monjɨ kɨnda yabekdak. Uŋun pi monjɨ busuŋɨkon aŋagek yo yokwisi aŋɨmgwit.
Yaŋdo, gɨptɨmgo dakon teŋteŋɨ uŋun pɨlɨn tuk asak yaŋ do kaŋ kɨmokgi.
Mani Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn do pasalek mibɨlni noman dɨma yawit.
Ae jap yet dɨwarɨ da joŋ kelɨ toŋ tɨmgwan mawit. Uŋun joŋ kelɨ toŋ gat kɨsi kwaŋek wutjɨŋba kɨmak mudawit.
Kwa Erot da bɨsap kɨnda aŋ yomɨŋek uŋun bɨsapmon kɨla amɨn madep yɨk ɨmalni paŋek kɨla amɨn madep tamonikon yɨkgɨt. Yɨgek gen madepsi yoyɨgɨt.
Piŋkop da asi Yesu kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdagɨt. Aeni arɨpmɨ dɨmasi kɨmotjak. Piŋkop da uŋun do yaŋ yagɨt: ‘Kalɨp Dewit do yo tagɨsi ae telagɨsi aŋ ɨm do yaŋ teban tok agɨm uŋun yo ji do dabeŋ. Yo morap uŋun yagɨm uŋun da tɨlagon asi altokdaŋ.’
Ae amɨn kɨnda da yɨkni ɨmegek kosit 1 kilomita kɨki do tebaisi gayɨsak kaŋ, yɨk uŋun ɨmegek 2 kilomita kɨki.
Yaŋ nandaŋek kɨŋ obip amɨn kabi kɨnda yapmaŋek kɨŋ aeni obip amɨn kabi kɨnda gat yapmaŋek ain yoma tagɨt uŋudon kɨgɨmal. Uŋudon kɨŋakwal ain yoma uŋun iyɨ wɨtdal kɨŋakwan kokup papmon pɨgɨgɨmal. Pɨgɨ tɨmɨsok dɨ kɨŋek aŋelo uŋun Pita yɨpmaŋ dek kɨgɨt.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji gen emat nido aŋ?”
Uŋun amɨn kabɨ madepgwan da amɨn kɨnda da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, peno iyɨŋbɨ datnit da yo morap yopgut uŋun kokwinɨk dɨwarɨ nak do namjak.”
Yesu da nandaŋ gadatni pɨndagek yagɨt, “Not, dɨwarɨgo yopmaŋ gamɨsat.”
Mata uŋun Yesu obɨsak yaŋ nandaŋek Maria yutnon yɨpmaŋek kosiron kwan Yesu gat domdom agɨmal.
Paŋkewal altaŋ namgwit bɨsapmon ji nak dɨma nepmaŋ dekgwit. Nak gat kɨsi egɨpgumaŋ.
Ae paŋdet uŋun kɨnda mibɨltok kɨmakbi tamokon kɨgɨt uŋun kɨsi wɨgɨgɨt. Wɨgɨ pɨndagek nandaŋ gadat agɨt.
“Kɨŋakwa tɨmɨ dɨ egɨ 9 kilok aŋakwan pi ami kɨŋ makeron amɨn dɨwarɨ ɨsal ekwa pɨndagek
Bɨsap 3 awa egɨ mudaŋakwa mɨŋatni yo morap uŋun noman taŋ uŋun dɨma nandaŋek apgut.
Yaŋban dɨ da Pol da gen yagɨt do nandaba bamɨ agɨt, ae dɨwarɨ da nandaŋ gadat ak do dɨma galak tawit.
Not kabɨ, babɨknin Dewit uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ do asisi dayɨŋ teŋteŋoko. Dewit uŋun kɨmakban kɨlɨsi wayɨkgwit. Bumjotni dakon tamo abɨsok on kokupmon komaŋ.
Nak yaŋ gayɨsat, mango uŋun Pita. Aŋakwan tɨp uŋun da kwenon paŋmuwukbi kabɨno paŋ- muwuk yopbo Tɨpdom dakon tapmɨm da arɨpmɨ dɨma pabɨŋ yopmaŋakwan toktogɨsi taŋ aŋ aŋ kɨkdɨsak.
Yaŋban amɨn da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Kristo uŋun altaŋek dagok dagogɨ mɨni egɨpdɨsak, Piŋkop dakon gen teban papia da yaŋ yosok. Do gak da Amɨn Dakon Monji aŋenotdaŋ yaŋ nido yosol? Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun namɨn amɨn kɨnda?”
Gen kɨnda dayɨko nandawit uŋun yaŋ ‘Nak depmaŋ kɨkdɨsat. Aŋek aeno tobɨl jikon opdɨsat.’ Ji da nak but dasi galak taŋ namaŋ kaŋ, nak Daron wɨgɨkdɨsat uŋun da kɨsɨk kɨsɨk damdɨsak, nido Dat da nak ŋwapmaŋdak.
Bɨsap kɨndakon peni padɨge 7 kabɨ egɨpgwit. Mibɨltok nani uŋun mɨŋat paŋek monji mɨni egek kɨmakgɨt.
Iyɨŋba nandaŋek amɨn bamot pawɨgɨ dam teban yutnon yut monɨŋ kɨnda yutgwansi tagɨt uŋudon yopgut. Yopmaŋek dɨma abɨgɨnjil yaŋ do kandapni kɨndap kwuk baŋ paŋteban agɨt.
Aŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdet, gen yosol ae yoyɨŋdet asal uŋun kɨlegɨsi asal yaŋ nandaŋ gadamaŋ. Amɨn mani toŋ ae mani mɨni uŋun kɨsi gen bamɨsikon da Piŋkop dakon aŋpak yoyɨŋ dekdal.
Uŋun kokupmon amɨn da nin do aŋpak tagɨsi aŋnimgwit. Sɨkak maŋek kokup mɨrɨmɨsi agɨt do kɨndap paŋ soŋek uŋudon kɨndap alɨneŋ do niyɨwit.
Nak si kɨmokgeŋ da arɨpmon suŋ kɨnda agɨm kaŋ, tagɨ nɨkba kɨmokgeŋ. Mani top yaŋek gen pikon nepgwit kaŋ, amɨn kɨnda da nak Juda amɨn da kɨsiron dɨmasi nepjak. Rom dakon kɨla amɨn madep Sisa dagɨn geno nandɨsak do nandɨsat.”
“Paŋpulugokji, Gen Bamɨ Dakon Wup, Daron egɨsak. Nak da jikon yabekgo pɨkdɨsak. Uŋun da Daron da pɨŋek mibɨlno do yaŋ teŋteŋok akdɨsak.
Aŋakwa amɨn dɨ da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Meŋgo padɨk padɨkgoyo yomakon agek gak gandak do yoŋ.”
Ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da yaŋ mudaŋ ɨmgwit da ɨdon apgut. Abɨŋ amɨn mango yaŋek bɨsit aŋ amɨn uŋun tɨmɨk dam tebanon yop do apgut.”
Yaŋbal nandaŋ gadat amɨn dɨ Parisi da kabɨkon nani uŋun da pɨdaŋ agek yaŋ yawit, “Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨkon nani uŋun gɨptɨmni mandaŋek Moses dakon gen teban guramɨtni do yoyɨni.”
Mani tap wakga nɨman madep kɨnda tap binap tagɨt uŋudon wukwan abɨdagɨt. Tap wakga dakon tomno nɨmanon tebaisi tegaŋek tagɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan tap da tap wakga dakon buŋɨ tɨdaŋ tuwɨlgɨt.
“Amɨn kɨnda da amɨn tagɨ bamorɨ dakon oman arɨpmɨ dɨma asak. Yaŋ kaŋ, kɨnda naŋgɨn galak taŋ ɨmɨŋek kɨnda do nandaban yokwi taŋ ɨmdɨsak. Ae kɨnda dakon gen guramɨgek kɨnda manji ɨmdɨsak. Ji Piŋkop gat ae moneŋ gat kɨsi dakon oman monjɨni arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ.”
Moneŋni naŋ mudaŋakwan uŋun mɨktɨm amɨn da jap do madepsi aŋek dɨwarɨ da kɨmakgwit. Aŋakwa monji uŋun wadak wadak madepsi agɨt.
Amɨn morap uŋun moneŋni morapmɨ taŋ yomaŋakwa dɨwarɨ gɨn paret ɨdapmon yopmaŋ. Mani on mɨŋat wadak wadaksi aŋek moneŋni kɨsi yopmaŋdak. Kɨlɨ jap yumaŋ nosak moneŋni dɨ dɨma taŋ ɨmaŋ.”
Nak sipsip kabɨno nandaŋ yomɨsat. Uŋun tekno nandaŋek nolgaŋ.
Uŋun bɨsapmon gɨn Sol da Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn sigɨn dapba kɨmotni do yaŋek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨnon kɨgɨt.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Rom dakon kɨla amɨn madep Sisa Ogastus da gen teban kɨnda yɨpgut. Pi monjɨni kɨŋ amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun mani mandani do gen teban yɨpgut.
Mani gak yo kaloŋɨ kɨnda dogɨn nandaki kaŋ tagɨ. Maria uŋun dogɨn nandɨsak, do tagɨ dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk ɨbeŋ.”
Yaŋ teban tok awit amɨn uŋun 40 yapgut.
“Asisi dayɨsat, nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namjak amɨn da nak da pi asat uŋun akdɨsak. Nak Daron wɨgɨkdɨsat, do nak da pi agɨm si yapmaŋek madepsi akdɨsak.
Uŋun do aŋek Piŋkop da nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsikon da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak da kombɨ amɨno gat ae yabekbi kabɨno gat uŋun amɨn kabɨkon yabetdɨsat. Yabekgo dɨwarɨ dapba kɨmotdaŋ, ae dɨwarɨ yo yokwisi aŋyomdaŋ.’
Egek don Sirakus yɨpmaŋ degek Regium kokupmon kɨŋ altagɨmaŋ. Uŋudon pakgɨmaŋ da wɨsa dagokdo mɨrɨm saut tet da apgut do nin Regium yɨpmaŋ dekgɨmaŋ. Yɨpmaŋ degek gɨldat kɨnda do nin Puteoli kokupmon kɨŋ altagɨmaŋ.
Kɨŋ Jodan Pakbi pudaŋek aeni Jon da kalɨp amɨn telagɨ pakbi soŋ ɨmgut uŋun kokupmon paŋkɨ egɨpgut.
Israel amɨn dakon Piŋkop da babɨknin iyɨ do manjɨŋek Isip mɨktɨmon gɨsam yomaŋakwan amɨn morapmɨsi ɨreŋ tawit. Don Piŋkop da iyɨ da tapmɨmon Isip baŋ tɨmɨk paŋopgut.
Gen uŋun mɨktɨmon pɨŋ egɨpgut. Mɨktɨm gat ae yo morap mɨktɨmon toŋ uŋun iyɨ wasagɨt, mani mɨktɨmon ekwan mɨktɨm amɨn da niaŋen amɨn kɨnda yaŋ dɨma kaŋba pɨsagɨt.
Uŋun monjɨ wɨli aŋalaŋban mɨŋat amɨn kabɨni dɨwarɨni wɨrɨrɨgek iyɨ do tɨmɨtdɨsak, do mani Yesu yaŋ iyɨki.”
Amɨn Piŋkop do pasolgoŋ uŋun amɨn bupmɨ nandaŋ yomɨsak. Abɨsok ae don mɨŋat amɨn morapyo yaŋ gɨnsi bupmɨ nandaŋ yomɨŋ aŋaŋ kɨkdɨsak.
Do kɨŋ uŋun mɨktɨm dakon amɨn kɨndakon pi kɨnda abɨdagɨt. Aban amɨn tagɨni da yabekban bɨt damnikon kɨŋ bɨt jap yomgut.
Nak naga naŋ joŋɨgek naga do yaŋkwok asat, ae Dat nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋunyo kɨsi nak naŋ joŋɨgek yaŋkwok asak.”
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni amɨn kabɨ madep yopmaŋ degek boron wɨkwa paŋdetni gat kɨsi kɨwit. Ae bot dɨwarɨ gat kɨsi kɨwit.
Paŋmuwukbi dukwan dukwan waseŋ kɨwit uŋun agek amɨnon Gen Bin Tagɨsi yoyɨŋ teŋteŋawit.
Gɨldat pɨgakwan pɨlɨndo sot amɨn gat koŋni toŋ amɨn gat kɨsisi Yesukon paŋpaŋ apgwit.
Jerusalem kɨŋ altaŋba paŋmuwukbi gat ae kɨla amɨni gat ae yabekbi kabɨ gat da gɨldat tagɨ yaŋ yoyɨwit. Yaŋ yoyɨŋba Piŋkop da paŋpulugaŋakwan yo morap agɨmal uŋun dakon geni yoyɨgɨmal.
Gak nipbɨ kɨmakbi tamokon dɨma tokeŋ. Telagɨ amɨngo dakon gɨptɨm aŋkutnaŋaki dɨma mɨktosak.
Aŋakwa amɨn kaŋ agakwa kɨla amɨn da yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ yawit, “Amɨn dɨwarɨ paŋpulugagɨt, do uŋun asi Kristo, Piŋkop da pini asak do manjɨgɨt amɨn kaŋ, iyɨ tagɨ aŋpulugosak.”
Mani Yesu da mɨŋat monjɨyo iyɨkon apni do yoyɨŋek paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji mɨŋat monjɨyo yopba nagon apgut. Dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk yomni. Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun amɨn mɨŋat monjɨyo da tɨlagon ekwaŋ uŋuden amɨn dakon.
“Kosit yolɨk amɨn, ji dabɨlji mɨni da ekwaŋ. Awa! Ji yaŋ yoŋ: ‘Amɨn kɨnda da Piŋkop dakon Telagɨ Yut Madep do yaŋek geni yaŋ aŋteban aŋek ae don tagɨ kɨrɨŋɨtjak. Mani amɨn kɨnda da telagɨ yut dakon gol do yaŋek geni yaŋ aŋteban asak kaŋ, tagɨ dɨma kɨrɨŋɨtjak.’
Kaŋakwan Kwen Kokup wɨtdal kɨŋakwan yo kɨnda ɨmal madep yombem kɨnda da pɨgɨt. Uŋun kodɨgɨ 4 kabɨkon da yɨpba mɨktɨmon pɨgɨt.
Juda amɨn nandaŋakwa nak amɨn kɨnda gat gen emat Telagɨ Yut Madepmon dɨma agɨmak. Bo ae muwut muwut yutnikon bo kokup papmon amɨn paŋmuwugek upbalap ani do butni dɨma sugagɨm.
Yesu paŋdetni gat Galili mɨktɨmon muwugek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji amɨn da uwal da kɨsiron yɨpba
Yaŋ dɨma aŋek yut gwak maŋek yo dɨwarɨ do wadaŋek yut dɨma aŋ mudosok kaŋ, amɨn morap koni uŋun kɨsi jɨgɨlak yaŋek yanjaŋ ɨmdaŋ.
Kɨlɨ don Josep Arimatea kokupmon nani da kɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjotni Pailat da nandaŋ ɨban aŋkɨsak do iyɨgɨt. (Josep uŋun Yesu dakon paŋdetni kɨnda. Mani Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn do pasalek Yesu do nandaŋ gadatni si aŋkɨsɨbɨgɨt.) Pailat da nandaŋ ɨban Josep da kɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjotni aŋkɨgɨt.
Yesu Betani kokupmon amɨn kɨnda mani Saimon uŋun da yutnon yɨkgɨt. (Saimon uŋun kalɨp wuda tebani toŋ egɨpgut.) Yesu jap noknok tamokon yɨgakwan mɨŋat kɨnda pakbi kɨbaŋɨ toŋ tagɨsi kɨnamɨ kɨnda abɨdaŋek wɨgɨgɨt. Awɨŋ gapmɨ jokgalek Yesu da busuŋon tagalgɨt. (Uŋun pakbi dakon yumaŋ nogɨ madepsi ae tɨbɨrɨ uŋun tɨpnaŋ wasaŋbi.)
Mani Amɨn Dakon Monji Piŋkop Tapmɨm Ami da amɨn tet do kɨlɨ uŋun yɨtdɨsak.”
Juda amɨn morapmɨ Yesu Betani kokupmon egɨsak yaŋ nandaŋek uŋudon apgwit. Yesu kok do gɨn dɨma, Lasarus kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdagɨt uŋunyo kɨsi kok do apgwit.
Yaŋ kaŋek tap wakga kɨŋ tɨpmon tɨdaŋban wagɨl tuwɨl kɨsak yaŋdo si pasalgwit, do tap wakga da buŋɨkon kɨrat madep tap wakga abɨdaŋban akgaŋ 4 kabɨ yopba pɨgɨwit. Yaŋ aŋek wɨsa tepmɨ dagosak do bɨsit pi awit.
Ji dɨsi dakon kɨla aŋek paŋmuwukbi morap dakon kɨla kɨsi ani. Paŋmuwukbi kabɨ uŋun Piŋkop da Monji dakon yawi naŋ yumaŋ nagɨt. Uŋun sipsip kabɨni ji da kɨla ani do Telagɨ Wup da ji manjɨŋ depgut.
Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalon pɨgɨ amɨn moneŋ ɨlɨt pi awit uŋun wasaŋek yolakwan abɨgɨwit.
Kapaneam kokupmon ekwan kombɨ amɨn Aisaia da gen kɨnda yagɨt uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ:
Yaŋ aŋek dɨma apdɨsak yaŋ nandaŋakwan amɨn tagɨni da but pɨsogɨ mɨni apdɨsak.
Ae jap yet dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm nelagɨ toŋ uŋudon maŋ kwawit. Dɨwarɨ bamɨ 100, ae dɨwarɨ bamɨ 60, ae dɨwarɨ bamɨ 30 tawit.”
Amɨn Tagɨ da uŋun bɨsap dɨma aŋpɨsɨp asak tam mɨŋat amɨn morap kɨsi kɨmak mudonom. Mani mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ iyɨ do kɨlɨ manjɨgɨt uŋun do bupmɨ nandaŋek bɨsap aŋpɨsɨp asak.
Uŋun nak dakon yo. Naga dakon galaktok yolek moneŋno tagɨ kokwinɨk dabeŋ. Nak amɨn do yo tagɨsi aŋapbo gak nido nandaba yokwi tok asal?’ ”
Yo pasɨlɨ toŋ ae yo wɨtjɨŋbi da toŋ uŋun kɨsi teŋteŋɨkon tokdaŋ.
Kɨmagakwan ae kɨnda da pagɨt. Peni padɨgeyo 7 kabɨ kɨsi da paŋek monjɨ mɨni egek kɨmakgwit.
Piŋkop da man madep ɨmgut da iyɨ da amɨnsi tet do yɨkdak. Dat da Telagɨ Wup Monji do ɨbeŋ yaŋ kɨlɨ yaŋ teban tagɨt. Do Monji do ɨban uŋun da tagalban yo abɨsok noman tosok uŋun ji kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋ.
Kɨŋ altaŋakwa Yesu boron da ɨleŋɨkon obɨŋek amɨn morapmɨsi pɨndagek sipsip kɨla amɨni mɨni yombem da egɨpgwit, do bupmɨsi nandaŋ yomgut. Yaŋ nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn wasaŋek Piŋkop gen morapmɨ yoyɨgɨt.
Uŋun Juda amɨn da Sabat bɨsap dakon yo paŋtagap ak bɨsap, ae kɨmakbi tamo uŋun kapmatjok tagɨt, do amɨn bamot Yesu dakon bumjotni aŋkɨ uŋungwan yɨpgumal.
Mani nak da gulusuŋ kɨnda si kɨmotjak da arɨpmon dɨma agɨt kagɨm. Ae iyɨ Sisa da geni nandɨsak do yagɨt, do nak da yaŋ mudaŋ ɨbo Sisakon kɨkdɨsak.
Juda amɨn dakon Ɨmal Yut Kabeŋ Bɨlak uŋun dakon bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan
Paŋdetni da tɨlak gen uŋun yagɨt dakon mibɨlɨ do iyɨwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon mɨŋat amɨn morap Amɨn Tagɨ da paŋpulugosak do bɨsit iyaŋ uŋun amɨn kabɨ iyɨ do paŋkutnosak.’ ”
Mani Elaija kɨlɨ apgut, aban amɨn da dɨma kaŋba pɨsagɨt, do galaktokni yolek yo yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ aŋ ɨmgwit. Ae Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋunyo kɨsi yo yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ yaŋ gɨn aŋɨmdaŋ.”
“Mɨktɨmon amɨn ekwaŋ, awa! Amɨn dɨwarɨ da yokwikon depdaŋ. Mani yokwi ani do yabetdaŋ amɨn, awa!
Wɨŋakwan Pestus da yaŋ yagɨt, “Kɨla amɨn madep Agripa, gat ae amɨn morap on muwamaŋ ji on amɨn do koni. Juda mɨŋat amɨn morapyo Jerusalem ekwaŋ ae ɨdon ekwaŋ kɨsi da on amɨn gen yaŋ ɨmgwit. Aŋek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek uŋun amɨn dɨmasi egɨpjak, nak da si aŋakgo kɨmotjak do nayɨwit.
Aŋakwan Amɨn Tagɨ da yaŋ iyɨgɨt: ‘Moses, kandap gwɨlgo ɨlɨk yopmaŋ. Mɨktɨm tɨm uŋun bamaŋ akdal uŋun telagɨ mɨktɨm.
Mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yosok, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ dakon kosit aŋdɨmdɨm ani, kositni pasɨŋ aŋmɨlɨp ani.’ ”
Nak da naga gen dulumji paŋtagap aŋek nandak nandak tagɨsi damdɨsat. Dabo amɨn gen yaŋ damni uŋun da gen yoni uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma pabɨŋ depni. Do ji dɨsi kutnok do aŋek ni gen baŋ paŋtobɨl yomneŋ yaŋ do nandaba kɨk dɨma ani.
Yaŋ mudaŋakwan Yesu naŋgɨn kawit. Yo ɨleŋon altaŋba pɨndakgwit uŋun iyɨ dogɨn nandaba tawit. Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn dɨ dɨma yoyɨwit.
Uŋun amɨn kapbɨ dakon gen dɨma nandɨsak kaŋ, kɨŋ paŋmuwukbi kabɨkon mibɨlni yoyɨni. Aŋek paŋmuwukbi kabɨ dakon gen dɨma nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn yokwisi asak. Uŋun amɨn do Piŋkop dɨma nandaŋ ɨmaŋ amɨn ae takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn yaŋ nandaŋ ɨmni.
Yesu mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep gen yoyɨŋakwan meŋi padɨk padɨkni paŋabɨŋ yomakon agek Yesu gat yaŋ nandat ak do yawit.
Altaŋek Pega kokupmon Piŋkop gen yoyɨŋek Atalia kokup papmon pɨgɨgɨmal.
“Ji amɨn dakon teŋteŋɨ yombem da ekwaŋ. Kokup madep kɨnda ɨleŋon taŋban yo kɨnda da arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋyoŋgam asak.
Aŋek Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak dakon geni yoyɨŋ teŋteŋaŋek Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu Kristo do yoyɨŋ dekgɨt. Gen yaŋ teŋteŋok do dɨma pasalgɨt. Ae amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ sop dɨma aŋ ɨmgut.
Uŋudeŋ gɨn yo morap dayɨt uŋun da altaŋakwa Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Akdɨsak dakon bɨsap kɨlɨ kwaŋ tosok yaŋsi nandani.
“Mani amɨn kɨsisi dɨma op do yawit. Kɨnda da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak pi kɨnda kaluk yumɨt uŋun kɨŋ kokeŋ. Do nandaŋ namɨŋaki dɨma opbeŋ.’
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yagɨt, “Ji amɨn dakon aŋpak dɨma kokwinɨtni. Yaŋ ani kaŋ, Piŋkop da jiyo kɨsi kokwin akdɨsak.
Yɨpba taŋakwan don Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn da abɨŋ muwuk Pol aŋgwasɨŋek akgwit. Yaŋ aŋakwa pɨdaŋban kokup papmon aeni pɨgɨwit. Pɨgɨ pakgwit da wɨsa dagokdo Banabas gat uŋun kokup pap yɨpmaŋek Debe kokup pap kɨgɨmal.
Mani kalɨp Piŋkop da kombɨ amɨn kɨsi da gen kagakon da Kristo tepmɨ pasak do yagɨt. Do ji da Yesu aŋakba gen uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt.
“Amɨn kɨnda nak nol do nandɨsak kaŋ, meŋi datni, ae mɨŋatni gwakniyo gat, ae peni samɨni padɨgeyo gat, ae iyɨ dakon egɨp egɨpni gat kɨsi do uwal dɨma aŋyomjak kaŋ, uŋuden amɨn nak dakon paŋdetno arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpjak.
Yaŋ yawit, “On Yesu, Josep dakon monji gɨn, ma? Meŋi ae datni uŋun nandaŋ yomamaŋ. ‘Nak Kwen Kokup da pɨgɨm’ yaŋ niaŋon da yosok?”
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak uŋun amɨn kabɨ dogɨn dɨma pɨgɨm. Do nin kokup taŋ aŋaŋ kwaŋ uŋudon kɨŋek Piŋkop gen yoyɨkeŋ. Nak pi uŋun ak do pɨgɨm.”
Gen pɨlɨn kaga dayɨsat, uŋun gɨldat kalba yaŋ teŋteŋoni. Gen pɨsɨk mɨrakjikon dayɨsat uŋun yut kwenon da agek yaŋ teŋteŋaŋ yomni.
Ji pigaga kɨnda pi dɨma awiron jap bamɨ pani do nak da yabekgɨm. Amɨn da pi madepsi awiron ji da pini dakon bamɨ paŋ.”
“Nandani, yo jɨgɨsi morap uŋun dɨma altaŋakwa mibɨltok dayɨsat.
Gak tapmɨmgo yolɨŋaki sot amɨn kɨlek toni. Ae tɨlak tapmɨmɨ toŋ ae wasok masɨ masɨmɨ uŋun telagɨ oman amɨngo Yesu uŋun da manon aki.”
Mani uwal da kɨsiron nepjak amɨn nak gat kɨsi tamokon oni yɨkgamak.
Wɨsa dagokdo Juda amɨn muwugek Pol aŋakba kɨmotjak do wagɨl yaŋ aŋteban awit. Aŋek yawit, “Jap pakbiyo dɨma aŋek Pol aŋatno kɨmagakwan don noneŋ. Yaŋ dɨma aneŋ kaŋ, Piŋkop da nin tagɨ nindapjak.”
Yesu dakon padɨk padɨkni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak on kokup yɨpmaŋek Judia Provinskon kɨŋek wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ aŋaki paŋdetgoni da koni.
Yesu uŋun Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon burɨ kɨnda paret yopgwit uŋudon egek amɨn yoyɨŋ degek gen uŋun yagɨt. Mani bɨsapni dɨma agɨt, do amɨn kɨnda da dɨma abɨdagɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban Sunduk da Yesu iyɨŋ aŋaŋ ɨleŋ dubagɨsi kɨndakon wɨgek uŋudon gɨn on mɨktɨmon mɨktɨm madep madep morap kɨsi yolɨŋban pɨndakgɨt.
Yaŋdo, ji kaŋ kɨmotni. Bɨlak kapbɨ da butgwan nak kunamon da ji kaloŋ kaloŋ kɨsi dayɨŋ dekgɨm. Uŋun do dɨma ɨŋtoni.
Paŋdetni 10 kabɨ gen uŋun nandaŋek amɨn bamot uŋun do butjap nandawit.
Ae Juda amɨn da si aŋakba kɨmotjak do pasɨlɨkon da gen yaŋ aŋteban awit uŋun nandaŋek tepmɨsi yabekgo gagon obɨsak. Ae gen yaŋ ɨmaŋ amɨn uŋun kɨsi gagon obɨŋek mibɨlɨ nido gen yaŋ ɨmaŋ uŋun gak da ɨŋamon yaŋ teŋteŋoni do yoyɨsat.”
Maria Makdala kokupmon nani gat ae Maria Josep dakon meŋi gat da kaŋakwal Yesu dakon bumjotni yɨpgut.
Yaŋban Saimon Pita da boron wɨgek tap kɨlap yɨk ɨlɨkban ɨleŋɨkon wɨgɨgɨt. Yɨgon tap kɨlap madep madep 153 yaŋ da pɨgɨ tugawit, mani yɨk uŋun dɨma dagagɨt.
Yaŋsop aŋyomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨŋ dekgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ mandabi: ‘Nak dakon yut uŋun amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun da abɨŋ bɨsit aŋnamni do tosak.’ Mani ji da kulabɨk aba ‘kabo noknok dakon pasɨlɨ tamo asak.’ ”
Yaŋba gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda mani Yesu yaŋ iyaŋ uŋun da mɨktɨm baŋ neŋak wasaŋek dabɨlnokon wɨrɨrɨgek yaŋ nayɨk, ‘Gak kɨŋ Silom Pakbi Ɨdapmon pakbi soki.’ Yaŋ nayɨŋban kɨŋ pakbi soŋek dabɨlno kɨlek taŋban yo pɨndat.”
Ji kombɨ amɨn dakon babɨ kabɨni ekwaŋ. Piŋkop da babɨkji gat saŋbek saŋbek agɨt do yo morap yom do yagɨt uŋun ji da tɨmɨtni. Piŋkop da Abraham yaŋ iyɨgɨt: ‘Nak da gak dakon babɨgo yabegek amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun gɨsamɨkgo tagɨsi egɨpni.’
Yesu burɨ da bupmɨsi nandaŋek paŋdet kabɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Pigaga jap bamɨ madepsi taŋ pektaŋ, mani pi monjɨ bamɨ pakpak amɨn morapmɨ dɨma.
Yaŋ egek gen bamɨ nandaŋ pɨsaŋba uŋun da pulugaŋ depdɨsak.”
Yaŋban amɨn uŋun kɨŋ Yesu da yo agɨt uŋun dakon gen bin Dekapolis mɨktɨm uŋudon amɨn yoyɨŋban nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Niniwe amɨn Jona da Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋban but tobɨl awit. Mani ji da binapmon amɨn kɨnda egɨsak uŋun da Jona yapmaŋ mudosok, mani ji but tobɨl dɨma aŋ. Do gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon Niniwe amɨn da pɨdaŋ agek abɨsok ekwaŋ amɨn kabɨ dakon aŋpak yokwi uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋokdaŋ.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Niaŋ nandaŋ? Jikon da kɨnda dakon sipsipni kɨnda Sabat bɨsapmon gapmagwan mosak kaŋ, yum kaŋakwa uŋungwan di egɨpjak? Dɨmasi, aŋpulugaŋek abɨdaŋ ɨlɨkba wɨkdɨsak.
Nak gen kaloŋɨ kɨnda gɨn gen papmon da yaŋ yagɨm, ‘Piŋkop da amɨn kɨmakbi aeni paban pɨdokdaŋ uŋun nandaŋ teban tosot. Yaŋ nandɨsat do ji da nak gen pikon nepmaŋ.’ ”
“Yaŋban amɨn tagɨni da yagɨt, ‘Kokup pap 5 kabɨ kɨla aki do man madep gamɨsat.’
Aŋakwan emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn da Yesu ɨŋamɨkon kɨmakban kaŋek yagɨt, “On amɨn asisi Piŋkop dakon Monji egɨpgut.”
Wɨgɨkwan gawak ɨmɨŋek tobɨl kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi nandaŋek Jerusalem kɨwit.
“Yo on pɨndakgaŋ uŋun bɨsap kɨnda apdɨsak uŋun bɨsapmon uŋun dakon tɨp notni kwenon dɨma taŋ taŋ akdaŋ. Tuwɨlba kɨsisi maŋ mudokdaŋ.”
Wɨkwan amɨn Yesu gat yɨkgwit uŋun da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Meŋgo padɨk padɨkgo yomakon da gak do yoŋ.”
“Nandaba kɨk aŋek jap pakbiyo dukon baŋ noneŋ, bo ɨmal dukon baŋ paneŋ yaŋ dɨma nandani.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, yokwi pakpak kɨnda da but tobɨl asak kaŋ, Kwen Kokupmon kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi yaŋ gɨn akdaŋ. Amɨn 99 uŋun kɨlegɨ do but tobɨl agagɨ mɨni do uŋun dakon kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madep dɨma ani. Mani yokwi pakpak kɨnda but tobɨl asak uŋun dakon kɨsɨk kɨsɨk uŋun madepsi noman tosok.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gulusuŋ yat kaŋ, uŋun do nayɨ. Ae gen kɨlegɨ yat kaŋ, nido nɨkdal?”
Yaŋ nandaŋakwan Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, nak gen kɨnda gayɨko.” Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, kɨlɨ nayɨ.”
Amɨn da Yesu uŋun kɨla amɨn madepnin egɨ nimjak do aŋteban aneŋ yaŋ nandaŋakwa Yesu da butni pɨndak mudagɨt, do yopmaŋek iyɨ gɨn tobɨl ɨleŋon wɨgɨgɨt.
Jap bamɨ pakpak amɨn uŋun tomni tɨmɨkdak. Jap bamɨ paŋmuwukdak uŋun egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do paŋmuwukdak. Yaŋdo, jap kwaot kwaot amɨn gat ae jap bamɨ pakpak amɨn gat kɨsi da kɨsɨk kɨsɨk tagɨ anjil.
Do kɨla amɨnji dɨ yopba nak gat pɨgɨno gulusuŋ kɨnda agɨt kaŋ, uŋun amɨn da gen yaŋ ɨmni.”
Yaŋ yaŋek yawit, “Telagɨ bɨsap madepmon dɨma abɨdoneŋ. Yaŋ aneŋ kaŋ, mɨŋat amɨnyokon pɨdok pɨdok noman tokdɨsak.”
Uwal da abɨŋ amɨn dɨwarɨ emat agak sɨbabaŋ dapba kɨmotdaŋ. Ae dɨwarɨ mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ paŋkɨ yopba oman amɨni do egɨpdaŋ. Aŋakwa Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ da Jerusalem bamaŋ ɨktagɨldaŋ. Uŋun amɨn da Jerusalem kɨlani aŋakwa Piŋkop da bɨsap yɨpgut uŋun mudosak.”
Kɨmakbi da pɨdoni bɨsapmon mɨŋat eyo agak dɨma tokdɨsak. Aŋelo Kwen Kokup ɨsal ekwaŋ uŋun da tɨlagon egɨpdaŋ.
Yaŋ iyɨŋek amɨn kapmatjok akgwit uŋun yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Gol moneŋ tabɨl uŋun gwayeŋ amɨn moneŋ tabɨlni 10 kabɨ taŋ ɨmaŋ uŋun do ɨmni.’
Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Gak kɨki. Monjɨgo egɨpdɨsak.” Yaŋban kɨla amɨn Yesu da gen yagɨt uŋun do nandaban bamɨ aban tobɨl kɨgɨt.
Gɨldat kɨnda do Jon da Yesu iyɨkon opban kaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Kabɨt, on Piŋkop dakon Sipsip Monɨŋni. Uŋun mɨktɨm amɨn dakon dɨwarɨni wɨrɨrɨkdak.
Amɨn bamot uŋun manjɨŋek bɨsit yaŋ awit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak amɨn morap dakon but kɨsi pɨndak mudosol. Uŋun bamoron da namɨn dasi Judas dakon tamo abɨdaŋek yabekbi pi asak uŋun amɨn nolɨki. Bupmɨsi, Judas uŋun tamoni yɨpmaŋek kɨmak tamo iyɨ do yaŋ mudaŋbikon kɨgɨt.”
Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da kosiron ɨmalni kukwaŋ yalɨwit. Aŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ da kɨŋ kɨndap kɨlɨŋ mandaŋ paŋobɨŋ kosiron yalɨwit.
Nak dɨma mandaŋ nal, mani yutgokon si wɨron da wasaŋek mɨŋat on da kandapno mandaŋ nak da sigɨn mandaŋ nosok.
Amɨn morap Piŋkop bɨsit iyaŋ uŋun yo tɨmɨkgaŋ, ae yo wɨsaŋ amɨn uŋun bamɨ koŋ, ae yoma domon tɨdoŋ amɨn uŋun wɨtdal yomɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋakwa Yesu da donki kɨnda kaŋ uŋun da kwenon yɨkgɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda tosok uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt.
Ae Nikodemus kalɨp Yesu kalbi kɨŋ kagɨt uŋunyo kɨsi uŋun bɨsapmon gɨn apgut. Uŋun yo kɨbaŋɨ toŋ tagɨsi dɨ tɨmɨk paŋapgut. Uŋun kɨndap bamorɨ dakon gawoŋɨ baŋ ɨktagɨlek wasawit. Yo kɨbaŋɨ tagɨsi uŋun dakon jɨgɨni uŋun 30 kilo da arɨp.
Uŋun da kwenon Josep da datni Jekop ae yawi dɨwatni 75 kabɨ yaŋ kɨsisi morap apni do gen yɨpban kɨgɨt.
Aŋek Mata da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak ɨdon egɨpgul tam, olapno dɨma kɨmakgɨt.
Gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Telagɨ Yut Madepmon muwukgwit. Ae notni da yutnon muwuk muwuk aŋek but galagon da not paŋpulugok dakon kɨsɨk kɨsɨk aŋek jap nawit.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Kapaneam kokupmon kɨŋ altaŋakwa Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn da Pitakon kɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdetgo Telagɨ Yut Madep do takis yopmaŋdak bo dɨma?”
Amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni egɨpgut da sɨŋtagɨt uŋun iyɨŋ aŋaŋ Parisi amɨnon kɨwit.
“Ji yɨk monɨŋjikon gol bo silwa moneŋ bo kopa moneŋ dɨma sɨmɨlek agɨpni.
Pɨdot pɨdot bɨsap madepmon mɨŋat wɨliyo agak dɨma tokdɨsak. Aŋelo Kwen Kokup ɨsal ekwaŋ uŋun da tɨlagon egɨpdaŋ.
Kɨŋ egɨ don wain sop pakpak bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan oman monjɨ kɨnda yabekban wain bamɨ tɨmɨk paŋopjak do kɨgɨt. Mani pi kɨla awit amɨn da oman monjɨ obɨsi aŋagek bamɨ dɨ dɨma ɨmɨŋek yolba kɨgɨt.
Bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu Genesaret Pakbi Ɨdap ɨleŋɨkon agek Piŋkop dakon gen yaŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da abɨŋ uŋun da kapmatsisok aŋgwasɨŋek nandawit.
Uŋun do nak yaŋsi dayɨsat, ji uŋun amɨn kabɨ do yo yokwi kɨnda dɨma aŋ yomni. Ɨsal yopba kɨni. Amɨn da nandak nandagon yo uŋun aŋ kaŋ, bamɨ dɨma asak.
Yaŋban Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep tɨmtɨm yaŋek apba pɨndagek koŋ tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Koŋ, gen kaga ae mɨrak sopsop amɨn, gak monjɨ on yɨpmaŋdet! Wagɨl kɨŋek buŋon on monjɨgwan dɨmasi pɨgɨki!”
Aŋek Telagɨ Wup da amɨn kɨsi morap burɨkon pɨgɨ tugagɨt. Aŋek Wup da paŋpulugaŋban wasaŋek gen mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ yawit.
“Jon, monjɨno, gak don Piŋkop Wɨkwisi dakon kombɨ amɨn kɨnda yaŋ gayɨkdaŋ. Gak Amɨn Tagɨ mibɨltaŋ ɨmɨŋek kositni yuldɨsal.
Gɨldat kɨnda do amɨn kabɨ madep Yapyap Bɨlak kok do apgwit uŋun da Yesu Jerusalem kokup papmon abɨsak yaŋ nandawit.
Kɨsisi waŋga kɨŋ mudaŋakwa sipsip kɨla amɨn da mibɨltaŋ yoban tegɨ nandaŋ ɨmaŋ, do buŋon yol aŋaŋ kwaŋ.
Paŋdetni da namɨn dasi mibɨltok amɨnin egɨsak yaŋ do gen emat awit.
Jap yet kwaŋek bamɨ tok do aŋakwa joŋ yokwi kɨsi kwaŋ wɨwit.
Yaŋ aba ji nak nolgaŋ do aŋek amɨn kɨsi morap da ji do butjap nandakdaŋ. Mani tebai agek egɨ wɨgakwa bɨsap madepmon wɨgɨsak amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨtdɨsak.”
Uŋun aŋelo da yaŋ egɨpdaŋ, do ae kɨnda gat arɨpmɨ dɨma kɨmotni. Uŋun kɨmoron da pɨdokdaŋ, do Piŋkop dakon mɨŋat monjɨyo egɨpdaŋ.
Koŋni toŋ amɨn kɨnda Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon yɨkgɨt. Uŋun da madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda da nak dakon gen guramɨtjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn dɨmasi kɨmotjak.”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban Pita da pɨdaŋ pɨgɨ amɨn uŋun yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn wɨsaŋ uŋun nak mani. Ji mibɨlɨ nido abeŋ?”
Yoyɨŋban paŋdetni da gen uŋun iyɨ gɨn yaŋ nandaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Kɨmoron da pɨdot pɨdot uŋun yo kɨnda nido nandaŋek yosok.”
Gen yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek Juda amɨn da iyɨ gɨn yaŋ yawit, “ ‘Nak kɨkeŋon arɨpmɨ dɨma apni’ yaŋ uŋun nido yosok? Iyɨ naŋ aŋagek kɨmot do yosok?”
Kanekni kapbɨ aŋakwan waŋga abɨgɨ yɨpmaŋakwa kɨla amɨn madep Pero dakon gwi da kaŋ abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ iyɨ dakon monji naŋ yaŋ upmakgɨt.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban bret tɨmɨ 5 bali baŋ wasaŋbi naŋ dɨwarɨkgwit uŋun yɨk madep 12 kabɨ sɨmɨlba tugawit.
Mani Yesu uŋun mɨŋat kabɨ tobɨl pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jerusalem dakon gwani, ji nak do kunam dɨma tatni. Dɨsi gat ae mɨŋat monjɨyosi gat do tatni.
Mani kalbi kosit agɨpjak kaŋ, teŋteŋɨ mɨni do aŋek kesal aŋatjak.”
Salmon uŋun Boas dakon datni. (Meŋi uŋun Reap.) Boas uŋun Obet dakon datni. (Meŋi uŋun Rut.) Obet uŋun Jesi dakon datni.
Ji bɨsit ani bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda da yokwi aŋ damgut kaŋ, yokwini yopmaŋ ɨbi. Yaŋ ani kaŋ, Kwen Kokup Datji da yokwisi yaŋ gɨn yopdɨsak.”
Antiok paŋmuwukbi kabɨkon kombɨ amɨn ae yoyɨŋdet amɨn kɨsi egɨpgwit. Uŋun dakon mani yaŋ: Banabas, ae Simeon mani kɨnda Naija yaŋ iyɨwit. Ae Lusias Sairini kokupmon nani, ae Manain uŋun monɨŋɨsogon da Erot gat kaloŋɨ egɨpgumal, ae Sol.
Yesu paŋdetni 12 kabɨ yoyɨŋ dek mudaŋek uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Galili mɨktɨm dakon kokup pap tawit uŋudon agek Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋ dekgɨt.
Yaŋ aba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji Parisi gat ae Sadyusi amɨn gat uŋun dakon yis do pakyaŋsi kaŋ kɨmotni.”
Parisi amɨn da uŋun amɨn yabekba apgwit.
Yabekbi kabɨ da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ aŋakwa amɨn morapmɨ uŋudon kɨŋ gadaŋakwa mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat dabɨni gat da pɨndagek nandaba yokwi tok aŋ yomgwit. Uŋun amɨn uŋun Sadyusi da kabɨkon nani.
Mani Gen Bamɨsi Dakon Wup uŋun da abɨŋ ji paŋpulugaŋban gen bamɨ morap nandaba pɨsokdaŋ. Uŋun iyɨ dakon gen baŋ dɨma dayɨkdɨsak, gen nandɨsak uŋun baŋgɨn dayɨkdɨsak. Aŋek yo don altokdaŋ uŋun do dayɨkdɨsak.
Erot da Yesu dakon mibɨlɨ nandak do gen morapmɨ iyɨgɨt, mani gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma yagɨt.
Gen uŋun yaŋakwan gɨn amɨn morapmɨ da nandaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit.
Gɨldat kɨnda do mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda do egɨpgwit uŋun sigɨn egɨpgwit. Egek yaŋ nandawit, apma bot kaloŋɨ kɨnda gɨn tagɨt, mani Yesu uŋun boron paŋdetni gat dɨma wɨgɨwit. Paŋdetni dagɨn wɨgek kɨwit.
Ae amɨn kɨnda da wain kalugɨ tɨbɨrɨ meme gɨp baŋ wasaŋbi kalɨpmɨ kɨndakon kolesak kaŋ uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Yaŋ asak kaŋ, wain da pukwa paptaŋ meme gɨp kɨrɨŋɨgakwa wain maŋ mudokdaŋ. Ae meme gɨpyo kɨsi yokwi tokdɨsak.
Yesu tɨmɨsok dɨ kɨŋek ae amɨn bamorɨ gat pɨndakgɨt, kɨnda uŋun Jems, Sebedi dakon monji, ae padɨge Jon. Uŋun bamot gat datni gat boron yɨgek tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨkni bɨsawɨk paŋmɨlɨp aŋyo aŋakwal pɨndakgɨt. Pɨndagek yaŋ yoban
Ji nak nolgaŋ do aŋek yokwi aŋdamdaŋ, nido Dat nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun dɨma nandaŋ ɨmaŋ.
Amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut uŋun mani Ananias. Mɨŋatni dakon mani uŋun Sapaira. Ananias uŋun mɨktɨm tɨmni kɨnda amɨn do yomɨŋek moneŋ tɨmɨkgɨt.
Nak egɨp egɨpno paregek aeno abɨdokdɨsat, yaŋ do Dat da nak do but dasi galak taŋ namɨsak.
Aŋakwa sakwabat yoni mɨni kɨnda da abɨŋ moneŋ gɨmani tabɨlɨ bamorɨ monɨŋɨsisok paret yopyop tamokon yopgut.
Muwugakwa Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut dakon kɨla amɨn kɨnda mani Jairus, uŋun da abɨŋ Yesu kaŋek burɨkon kɨŋek gawak ɨmgut.
Jon iyɨ teŋteŋɨ dɨma. Uŋun da teŋteŋɨ dakon but pɨso gen gɨn yagɨt.
Amɨn nak dakon gen nandaŋek burɨkon yɨpmaŋdak uŋun amɨn Piŋkop da saŋbeŋek nandak nandak tagɨ madepsi ɨmdɨsak. Mani amɨn nak dakon gen nandaŋek burɨkon dɨma yɨpmaŋdak uŋun amɨn nak dakon gen dɨwarɨ nandagɨt uŋun pasɨl ɨmdɨsak.
Uŋun da kalɨp Juda amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kaloŋ kɨnda dagɨn amɨn morap kɨsi do aŋek kɨmotjak kaŋ, uŋun tagɨ.”
(Amɨn jap nawit uŋun 4 tausen yaŋ da nawit.) Yaŋ aŋek Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep yabekban kɨŋakwa,
Yesu dakon bumjotni dɨma taŋban kaŋek tobɨl abɨŋ yaŋ niyɨmal, ‘Nin kɨŋ dɨpmɨn yombem kɨnda kaŋapno aŋelo da yaŋ niyeŋ “Uŋun kalugɨ egɨsak.” ’
Yaŋban mɨŋat da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, bamɨ yosol, mani pɨŋan tewɨgɨ da tamokon da jap jɨmjɨm moŋ uŋun tagɨ noŋ.”
Aŋek yaŋ teban tok kɨnda aŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yo nido nayɨki, tagɨ gabeŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek aeni gawagek mɨktɨmon kɨlda mandagɨt.
Mani amɨn morapmɨ, do yutnon awɨgɨk do aŋtɨdok awit. Do yut kwenon wɨgɨ yut tuwɨlek amɨn uŋun wayɨgon pagakwan napmon da abɨdaŋakwa amɨn morap da binapmon pɨgek Yesu da buronsi pɨgɨgɨt.
Yapyap Bɨlak kwaŋ taŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ kokup dukwan dukwan da Jerusalem apgwit. Abɨŋ aŋpakni yolek iyɨ Piŋkop da dabɨlon kɨlek taŋek bɨsap madepmon kɨlegɨsi egɨpni yaŋ do pini awit.
Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn bamorɨ uŋun amɨn kɨndakon gomani toŋ. Kɨnda dakon gomani uŋun moneŋ 500 danari, ae kɨnda dakon gomani uŋun moneŋ 50 danari.
Bɨsap kɨndakon gɨldat tobɨl do 3 kilok burɨ pɨsaŋakwan dɨpmɨn yombem kɨnda kagɨt. Kaŋakwan Piŋkop dakon aŋelo kɨnda yutnon wɨgɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Konilias!”
(Pilip si aŋkewalek kok do yaŋ iyɨgɨt. Yesu uŋun yaŋ akeŋ yaŋ uŋun iyɨ kɨlɨ nandagɨt.)
Uŋun amɨn kabɨ da aŋsolat aŋek, ɨlɨp sul ɨmɨŋek, baljaŋek aŋakba kɨmotjak. Gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Yaŋ aŋek Amɨn Tagɨ da nayɨgɨt, uŋun da tɨlagon uŋun moneŋ baŋ mɨktɨm kwoba wasawit mɨktɨm tɨm kɨnda yumaŋ nawit.”
Uŋun mɨŋat monjɨyo da yaŋ, yumaŋ gwayek tamokon yɨgek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yoŋ: ‘Nin kasɨsɨŋ kɨlɨ pɨsomaŋ, mani ji kap ak do dɨma nandayɨŋ. Nin bupmɨ kap yamaŋ, mani ji bupmɨ nandaŋek kunam tat do dɨma nandayɨŋ.’ ”
Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun yaŋ gɨn kɨlɨ agɨt. Amɨn da oman aŋɨmni do dɨma pɨgɨt. Iyɨ mɨŋat amɨn morap paŋpulugokdo, ae iyɨ dakon gɨptɨmnaŋ paregek yumaŋ naŋ yop do pɨgɨt.”
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni burɨ yokwi taŋba kaloŋ kaloŋ yaŋ yawit, “Nak dɨma, ma?”
Ji datji Sunduk uŋun dakon monjini egek galaktokni yol do tagɨsi nandaŋ. Kalɨpsi wasok wasogɨkon amɨn dapdap kɨnda egɨpgut. Gen bamɨ uŋun iyɨkon dɨma tosok, do gen bamɨ uŋun dɨma yoldak. Uŋun top gen dakon datni egɨsak, do iyɨ dakon gen yaŋek top yosok.
Aŋakwa bot uŋun paŋkɨ ɨleŋɨkon agakwan Yesu pɨŋ ɨleŋɨkon wɨŋek amɨn kabɨ madepsi pɨndak bupmɨ nandaŋek sot amɨn paŋmɨlɨp agɨt.
Ae uŋun amɨn da tuŋon amɨn emarɨ toŋ abɨdokdaŋ, ae pakbi emarɨ toŋ naŋba uŋun da dɨma paŋupbal akdaŋ. Uŋun amɨn da sot amɨn kɨsirɨ kwenikon wɨtjɨŋba sotni mudokdaŋ.”
Wɨsa dagaŋakwan tap wakga dakon pi monjɨ da mɨktɨm uŋun kaŋek ni mɨktɨmon abɨmaŋ uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt. Mani tap wakga da paŋkɨ atjak tamo nɨmani toŋ tagɨsi kɨnda kawit. Yaŋ kaŋek nin uŋudon paŋkɨ atneŋ kaŋ tagɨsi yaŋ nandawit.
Yaŋ yaŋek wigaron pɨgakwan oman mɨŋat kɨnda Pita kaŋek amɨn uŋudon akgwit yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On amɨn uŋun Yesu Nasaret amɨn gat kɨsi egɨpgwit.”
Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madepmon wɨgek paret yopyop tamo da kapmatjok yɨkgɨt. Yɨgek pɨndagakwan amɨn morapmɨ da paret yopgwit. Moneŋ morapmɨ taŋ yomgwit amɨn uŋun da moneŋ madep yopgwit.
Kosiron kɨŋek pakbi kɨndakon altaŋek amɨn madep uŋun da Pilip yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Kosol, pakbi oni. Mibɨlɨ nido telagɨ pakbi dɨma sokeŋ?”
Uŋun kɨsi tagɨ dɨma abɨŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsini? On amɨn mɨktɨm ŋwakŋwarɨkon nani dagɨn abɨk.”
Amɨn Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak dakon gen nandaŋek butni dɨma pɨsoŋ uŋun jap yet kosiron mawit uŋuden. Yokwi Ami da abɨŋ gen tagɨ butnikon toŋ uŋun gwayeŋ paŋkɨsak.
Yoba tɨmɨgek amɨn kɨsisi jap arɨpmɨsi nawit.
“Yaŋ nayɨŋban yagɨm, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ gak namɨn?’ “Yaŋ yoko Amɨn Tagɨ da yagɨt, ‘Nak Yesu. Nak naŋ aŋupbal ak do pi asal.
Mɨktɨm dakon bɨsap mudosak bɨsapmon yaŋ gɨn altokdɨsak. Aŋelo kabɨ da abɨŋ amɨn yokwi amɨn kɨlegɨ da bɨkbɨgon ekwaŋ uŋun tɨmɨtdaŋ.
“Amɨn abɨsok ekwaŋ uŋun nandaŋ kokwini tagɨ dɨma. Uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ tɨmɨsok dɨ dayɨko nandabɨt. Uŋun mɨŋat monjɨyo da yaŋ, yumaŋ gwayek tamokon yɨgek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yoŋ,
Aŋakwan amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, Piŋkop da amɨn kaloŋɨsok dɨ baŋgɨn yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨtjak bo niaŋ?” Yaŋban Yesu da yoyɨgɨt,
Yesu Matyu da yutnon yɨgek jap naŋek takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn morapmɨ ae yokwi pakpak amɨn morapmɨ da apba Yesu gat paŋdetni gat kɨsi yɨgek jap nawit.
“Nak Klodias Lisias da papia on gapman dakon mibɨltok amɨn madep Peliks do mandɨsat. Gɨldat tagɨsi.
Juda amɨn ae Grik amɨn morap Epesas egɨpgwit uŋun yo altagɨt dakon geni nandaŋek madepsi pasalgwit. Yaŋ aŋek Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu dakon man do nandaba wukwisi agɨt.
yaŋ iyɨwit, “Kristo gak namɨn da gɨkdak? Kombɨ gen ya!”
Yesu da aeni tɨlak gen kɨnda gat yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun yis yombem. Mɨŋat kɨnda da plaua ɨdap madep kɨnda gat ɨktagɨldak. Yaŋ aŋakwan plaua uŋun kɨsisi paptaŋ madep tawit.”
Gɨldat kabi dɨ egɨ mudaŋek kɨla amɨn madep Agripa gat sami Benaisi gat Pestus kok do Sisaria kokupmon opgumal. Obɨŋek but galak gen iyɨŋek pi tamo on abɨdagɨl uŋun do nandando tagɨsi asak yaŋ iyɨgɨmal.
Yaŋ iyɨŋek kɨnda da emat agak sɨbanaŋ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon oman monjɨ aŋagek mɨrakni amɨn tet nani mandaban dagaŋ kɨgɨt.
Aŋakwan paŋdetni pakbi wayɨgek 5 bo 6 kilomita da tɨlak kɨŋek kaŋakwa Yesu pakbi ɨdap kwenon bamaŋ bamaŋ bot da kapmatjok opban kaŋek pasalgwit.
Yesu yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji tɨp madep aba kwan.” Yaŋ yaŋban Mata uŋun amɨn kɨmakgɨt dakon sami da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, abɨsok taŋban gɨldat 4 kabɨ asak, do yaŋ aneŋ kaŋ, kɨbaŋ madepsi akdɨsak.”
Abɨŋ nandaba amɨn bamot da Yesu kɨmoron da pɨdagɨt ae amɨn kɨmakbi yaŋ gɨn pɨdokdaŋ uŋun do yoyɨŋ teŋteŋagɨmal. Yaŋ aŋakwal amɨn bamot do nandaba yokwi tok awit.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban ae kokup ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨndakon kɨwit.
Obɨŋ gen teban dakon mibɨlɨ nandak nandak amɨni kɨnda da Yesu aŋkewalek yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
“Iyɨŋban yo kɨla agak pi amɨni uŋun iyɨ yaŋ nandagɨt, ‘Amɨn tagɨno da pikon noldak, do niaŋ abeŋ? Amɨn kɨnda dakon oman monjɨni egek mɨktɨmni pudaŋ ɨbeŋ dakon tapmɨmno mɨni. Ae amɨn moneŋ do bɨsit yoyɨk do mayagɨ nandɨsat.
Yaŋgɨn Sunduk da Sunduk yoljak kaŋ, Sunduk da iyɨ waseŋ kɨ kabi bamorɨ aŋek yo morap kɨla agak dakon tapmɨm pasɨl ɨmdɨsak.
Telagɨ Wup da iyɨ amɨn egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni yomɨsak. Amɨn da iyɨ egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni arɨpmɨ dɨma tɨmɨtni. Gen dayɨsat uŋun da Wup egɨp egɨp damɨsak uŋun jikon aŋabɨsak.
Yaŋdo, ji dɨsi do kɨla tagɨsi ani. “Notgo kɨnda yokwi aban kaŋ, tebai iyɨŋbɨ egɨp egɨpni aŋmɨlɨp asak. Ae but tobɨl aban kaŋ, yokwini yɨpmaŋ ɨbi.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek paŋdetni mibɨltaŋ yomɨŋek Betani kokupmon kɨwit. Kɨŋ uŋudon kɨsirɨ paŋenagek gɨsam yomgut.
Mɨŋat amɨn kabɨno Isip amɨn da yo yokwi morapmɨ aŋ yomɨŋakwa kɨlɨ pɨndat. Ae kunam wuwɨkni kɨlɨ nandat do aŋek Isip da kɨsiron baŋ tɨmɨt do pɨsat. Moses kɨlɨ apbɨ yabekgo Isip mɨktɨmon kɨki.’
Aŋakwa Yesu abɨŋ Ɨleŋ Olip dakon kosit obandom naŋ pukwaŋ uŋun aŋkapmat aŋakwan paŋdet kabɨni madepsi da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ morap aban pɨndakgwit uŋun do nandaŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiwit.
Aŋakwa jap yet dɨwarɨ joŋ kelɨ toŋ tɨmgwan mawit. Uŋun joŋ kelɨ toŋ gat kɨsi kwaŋek wutjɨŋba kɨbɨdawit.
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “On ekwamaŋon amɨn dɨma ekwaŋ, do jap dukon baŋ paŋabɨŋ on mɨŋat amɨn madep yomneŋ?”
Yaŋba Yesu da kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok teŋteŋɨ ji gat egɨpjak. Pɨlɨn tuk tepmɨ apban kosit dɨma kokdaŋ, do abɨsok teŋteŋɨ taŋakwan gɨn teŋteŋɨkon agɨpni. Amɨn pɨlɨn tukgwan akwaŋ uŋun dukwan kwaŋ uŋun dɨma nandaŋ.
Yaŋ aŋek naga do yaŋsi yokeŋ, “Nak bɨlak morapmɨ tagɨsi egɨ aŋaŋ kɨkeŋ dakon yo morapno arɨpmɨsi. Do yaworɨsi egek jap pakbiyo madepsi aŋek bɨsap morapmɨ kɨsɨk kɨsɨk aŋek egɨpbeŋ.” ’
Aŋkɨ yɨpba kalbi Amɨn Tagɨ da Pol da kapmatjok agek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak pasol pasol dɨma aki. Si teban taŋek egɨpbi. Nak dakon gen Jerusalem yaŋ teŋteŋagɨl uŋun Rom mɨktɨmon yaŋ gɨn yaŋ teŋteŋoki.”
Mani uŋun gen mandagɨt uŋun do nandaba bamɨ dɨma asak, do nikon da nak dakon gen do nandaba bamɨ asak?”
Aŋek yoyɨgɨt, “Ji bumjotni dukwan yɨpgwit?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, abɨŋek ka.”
“Noa da bɨsapmon amɨn egɨpgwit uŋudeŋ gɨn Amɨn Dakon Monji apjak bɨsapmon yaŋ gɨn aŋ egɨpdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da gen morapmɨ yaŋ ɨmgwit.
Yut kɨndakon wɨgɨni bɨsapmon, uŋun yutnon amɨn ‘Amɨn Tagɨ dakon but yawot jikon tosak’ yaŋ yoyɨni.
Jon da gen yaŋ yaŋban Erodias da Jon do nandaban yokwi taŋban aŋakba kɨmotjak do si nandagɨt. Mani arɨpmɨ dɨma,
Yaŋ agɨt do amɨn da ɨmal dakni paŋobɨŋ Pol da kwenon wɨtjɨŋek paŋkɨ sot amɨn do yoba tɨmɨkgwit. Tɨmɨgakwa sotni mudaŋakwa koŋni wɨŋ abɨgɨwit.
Ji on amɨn do nandaba kɨk dɨma ani. On amɨn kosit yolɨk amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni yombem. Dabɨlɨ mɨni kɨnda da notni kɨnda kosit yolɨsak kaŋ, kɨsi bamot gapmakon mokdamal.”
“Kɨsitgo da yokwi aki do gayɨŋban kaŋ, kɨsitgo mandaŋ dagoki. Gwɨnɨmbɨl egek Tɨpdomon kɨndap tebanon pɨgɨki yaŋ do kɨsitgo mandaŋ dagaŋek tagapmɨ egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do amɨn aki.
Iyɨ dakon oman monjɨni Israel paŋpulugaŋek yaŋ teban tok gen Abraham gat ae babɨkni gat do yoyɨgɨt uŋun dɨma ɨŋtagɨt. Yaŋ teban tok geni aŋteban aŋek uŋun yawi dɨwatni dagok dagogɨ mɨni bupmɨ nandaŋ yomɨŋ aŋaŋ kɨsak.”
Aeni don paŋdetni 11 kabɨ muwuk yɨgek jap naŋakwa altaŋ yomgut. Altaŋ yomɨŋek gen tebaisi yaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji amɨn da ‘pɨdak da egɨsak’ yaŋ dayɨŋba nido nandaba bamɨ dɨma ak? Nandaŋ gadatji mɨni?”
Yaŋ nandaŋek pɨdaŋ datnikon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan datni dubagɨkon da monji kaŋ bupmɨ nandaŋ tɨmtɨm yaŋek kɨŋ monji bedaŋek mandaŋ nagɨt.
Dat gat nit kaloŋɨ ekwamak.”
Amɨn Tagɨ da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨni yo tagɨsi aŋyomdɨsak dakon bɨsap kɨlɨ abɨsak uŋun dakon yaŋ teŋteŋok akeŋ do yabekgɨt.”
Kɨŋakwan uŋudon gɨn 25 tausen danari tɨmɨkgɨt amɨn uŋun yomɨŋ gwayek aŋakwan 25 tausen danari kɨnda gat noman tagɨt.
Pol Debe kokup pap kɨŋek uŋudon da Lista kokup pap kɨŋ altagɨt. Uŋun kokupmon Yesu dakon paŋdetni kɨnda egɨpgut mani Timoti. Meŋi uŋun Juda mɨŋat kɨnda. Uŋun mɨŋat Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgut. Mani datni uŋun Grik amɨn kɨnda.
Yesu da amɨn morapmɨ aŋgwasɨŋek akba pɨndagek paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nin pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda do kɨno.”
Mani Yesu uŋun amɨn ɨgayɨŋ ɨmgut uŋun kok do sigɨn wɨsɨgɨt.
Gɨldat 7 kabɨ palɨ mudaŋakwan Juda amɨn dɨ Esia mɨktɨmon da apgwit uŋun da Pol Telagɨ Yut Madepmon kawit. Kaŋek mɨŋat amɨn morap muwukgwit dakon but sugaŋek Pol abɨdawit.
Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Nak naga pɨdot pɨdot ae egɨp egɨp ami. Amɨn kɨnda nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨŋek kɨmotjak kaŋ, kalugɨ sigɨn egɨpdɨsak.
Ae kandapgo da yokwi aki do gayɨŋban kaŋ, kandapgo mandaŋ dagoki. Gwɨnɨmbɨl egek Tɨpdomon kɨndap tebanon pɨgɨki yaŋ do kandapgo mandaŋ dagaŋek tagapmɨ egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do amɨn aki.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Parisi amɨn da abɨŋ Yesu aŋkewal do aŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda abɨ kaŋek nin da gandano Piŋkop da gak yabekban pɨl da pini asal yaŋ gandaneŋ.”
Mani amɨn kɨnda da Telagɨ Wup abɨŋ yɨp do manji gen kɨnda yosak kaŋ, Piŋkop da dɨwarɨni dɨma wɨrɨrɨtjak. Uŋun dɨmasisi, uŋun dɨwarɨni mudok mudogɨ mɨni taŋ wɨgɨkdɨsak.”
(Juda amɨn ae amɨn dɨwarɨ Juda amɨn kabɨkon saŋbeŋbi kɨsi). Dɨwarɨ nin Krit amɨn, ae dɨwarɨ Arebia amɨn. Nin kɨsi morap da nandaŋapno uŋun amɨn kabɨ da nin da genon da Piŋkop dakon wasokni masɨ masɨmɨ uŋun do yaŋba nandamaŋ.”
Uŋun da kwenon Yesu yomakon pɨgek kɨŋ kaŋban takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt yut kabeŋon takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn kɨnda yɨkban kagɨt. Uŋun mani Liwai. Yesu da Liwai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Abɨŋ nak nol.”
Mibɨlni yaŋ teŋteŋaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gwano, nandaŋ gadatgo da gak aŋkɨlek ak. Uŋun do butgo yaworɨ taŋakwan kɨki. Sotgo kɨlɨ pasɨlak.”
Yaŋ yaŋek kɨsit bamotni ae gekgekniyo yolɨŋban paŋdetni Amɨn Tagɨni kaŋek but galak madepsi nandawit.
Mani mɨŋat uŋun bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ jɨgɨ namɨsak, do yumsi aŋpulugokeŋ. Bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ yaŋ gɨn apjak kaŋ, tagɨsi dɨma nandakdɨsat.’ ”
Yesu pɨdaŋ kɨk do aŋakwan amɨn kɨnda tɨmtɨm yaŋek abɨŋ gawak ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet gɨman, niaŋsi aŋek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokeŋ?”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo jɨgɨ dakon bɨsap mudaŋakwan, ‘Gɨldat dabɨl pɨlɨn tuk akdɨsak, ae kanek dɨma teŋteŋokdɨsak. Ae gɨk kundu yɨpmaŋek mokdaŋ. Aŋakwa kwen kundukon yo tebai toŋ uŋun da kwakwalɨtdaŋ.’
Naga pi teban yaŋ aŋek dayɨŋ dolɨgɨm. Jiyo yaŋ gɨn aŋek teban tokni mɨni amɨn uŋun paŋpulugoni. Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu iyɨ gen kɨnda yagɨt uŋun dɨma ɨŋtoneŋ. Gen uŋun yaŋ: ‘Yo ɨmɨsak amɨn dakon kɨsɨk kɨsɨkni wukwi, aŋakwan ɨban abɨdosok amɨn dakon kɨsɨk kɨsɨkni pɨŋbi.’ ”
“Sebulan mɨktɨm, ae Naptali mɨktɨm, Jodan Pakbi usugap tet do Galili mɨktɨmon tomal. Uŋun mɨktɨm bamot kosit tapmon pɨkwaŋ mɨktɨmon tomal. Galili mɨktɨmon Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨkon nani morapmɨ ekwaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋek Piŋkop da papiakon gen toŋ uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ nandaba pɨsoni do paŋpulugagɨt.
Mɨŋat amɨn jap naŋba arɨpmɨ aŋakwa jap dɨwat tawit uŋun paŋdetni da yɨk madepsi 7 yaŋ sɨmɨlba tugawit.
Uŋun da kwenon Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Judia mɨktɨmon kɨwit. Paŋkɨ paŋdetni gat egek amɨn telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomgut.
Yaŋ yaŋek Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda nak nol do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn iyɨ dakon galaktok morapni kɨsi yopmaŋ mudaŋek tɨlak kɨndapni guramɨgek nak noljak.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, Jon dakon monji, gak kɨsɨk kɨsɨk tagɨ abi. Gen yal uŋun mɨktɨm amɨn kɨnda da dɨma golɨgɨt. Kwen Kokup Dat da iyɨ golɨgɨt.
Ji teban taŋek bɨsit aŋek egɨpni. Yaŋ aŋek egɨpni kaŋ, paŋkewalon arɨpmɨ dɨma moni. But da nak nol do galak tosok mani gɨp dakon teban tokni mɨni.”
Uŋun amɨn sakwabat paŋkewalek yutni tɨmɨkgaŋ. Ae amɨn da pɨndatni yaŋ do bɨsit dubagɨsi aŋ. Uŋuden amɨn gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon kobogɨ do yo jɨgɨsi pakdaŋ.”
Gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak yo kaloŋɨsi kɨnda gɨn dɨma asal. Yo morapgo kɨsi yumaŋ naŋ mudaŋek, uŋun dakon moneŋɨ yoni mɨni amɨn do yobi. Yaŋ aŋaki yogo tagɨsi Kwen Kokupmon taŋ gamdɨsak. Yaŋ aŋek abɨŋ nak nol.”
Ae dɨ da yawit, “Elaija da noman tak.” Ae dɨ da “Kombɨ amɨn kalɨpsi egɨpgwit uŋun kɨnda da kɨmoron da pɨdak” yaŋ yawit.
Amɨn kabɨ uŋun kɨŋ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae kɨla amɨn kabɨ yaŋ yoyɨwit, “Nin jap dɨma naŋek Pol aŋatno kɨmagakwan don noneŋ do wagɨl yaŋ aŋteban amaŋ. Yaŋ dɨma aneŋ kaŋ, Piŋkop da nin tagɨ nindapjak.
Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn morapmɨ nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namaŋ uŋun nandaŋ gadatni yopba wɨtdal kɨŋakwa notni do nandaba yokwi tok aŋek uwal da kɨsiron yopmaŋ yopmaŋ akdaŋ.
Yesu gen uŋun yaŋ mudaŋek Galili mɨktɨm yɨpmaŋek Jodan Pakbi terɨ kɨnda Judia mɨktɨmon kɨgɨt.
Paŋdetni kɨnda Yesu da but dasi galak taŋ ɨmgut uŋun Yesu da ɨleŋɨkon yɨkgɨt.
Yaŋ aŋakwa notni da pɨndak nandaŋyo aŋek Sol Sisaria kokupmon aŋkɨ yabekba Tasas kokupmon kɨgɨt.
Mani datni da oman monjɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Monjɨno kɨmoron da yaŋ abɨsak. Pasɨlbikon naŋ aŋalon amaŋ. Do ji tepmɨ kɨŋ paba pɨgɨk dubagɨ tagɨsi kɨnda aŋabɨŋ paŋ ɨmni. Ae kɨsirɨkon sɨp tagɨsi kɨnda yɨpmaŋ ɨmɨŋek kandap gwɨl kɨsi paŋ ɨmni. Ae bulmakau monjɨ nelagɨ toŋ kɨnda naŋ aŋapba aŋak soŋ naŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ano.’ Datni da yaŋ yaŋakwan jap noknok aŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk awit.
Ae Erot yo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn nandaŋek aeni yɨpban ninon tobɨl abɨsak. Aŋatno kɨmotjak da tɨlak yokwi kɨnda dɨma agɨt kosot.
Uŋun dakon gen bini Jerusalem kwan paŋmuwukbi da nandaŋek Banabas yabekba Antiok kɨgɨt.
Sabat dakon tagaptok bɨsap Neŋgo pɨlɨndo Josep Arimatea kokupmon nani da apgut. Uŋun gen kokwin amɨn kabɨ dakon kɨla amɨn egɨpgut. Amɨn morapmɨ da nandaba wukwan ɨmgwit. Ae uŋun Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Akdɨsak uŋun do jomjom aŋek egɨpgut. Josep uŋun pasol pasolɨ mɨni Pailaron kɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjotni abɨdok do iyɨgɨt.
Aŋkɨ yɨpban Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egakwan gɨldat 40 ae pɨlɨn 40 mudagɨt, do jap do agɨt.
Aŋakwan Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn da geni uŋun nandaŋ wurɨpdagek yaŋ yawit, “On amɨn papia yut dɨma wɨgek nandak nandak madep dukon pagɨt?”
Yesu da gen uŋun yoyɨŋban paŋdetni dɨwarɨ tobɨl kɨŋek Yesu saŋbeŋek dɨma yolgwit.
Aŋakwa emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn gat ae emat amɨn Yesu do kaŋ egɨpgwit amɨn uŋun wudɨp ae yo morap altawit uŋun pɨndagek si pasalgwit. Pasalek yaŋsi yawit, “On amɨn asisi Piŋkop dakon Monji egɨpgut.”
Gɨldat kaloŋɨ do moneŋ 1 danari tɨmɨtni do yoyɨŋban but kaloŋ aba wain pinikon yabekban kɨwit.
Yaŋ nandaŋek oman monjɨ notni dapmaŋek pakbi teban naŋek but upbal aŋ amɨn gat muwugek jap pakbiyo aŋ.
Yaŋban Nataniel da iyɨgɨt, “Yo tagɨ kɨnda Nasaret kokupmon tagɨ dɨma altogɨ nandɨsat.” Yaŋban Pilip da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Abɨŋek ka.”
Yaŋdo, ji but tobɨl aŋek Piŋkopmon gadaŋba yokwisi mudoni.
Yaŋban yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Barabas naŋ yɨpbɨ kɨsak.” Barabas uŋun kabo noknok, ae amɨn dapmaŋek yoni gwayaŋ amɨn kɨnda.
Aba Yesu uŋun mɨŋat da kapmatjok paŋkɨ agek gɨptɨmni kɨndapmɨ sogɨt uŋun pasɨl ɨmjak do tebai yagɨt. Yaŋban sotni pasɨl ɨmɨŋakwan uŋudon gɨn pɨdaŋek japni paŋkosit agɨt.
do Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji Amɨn Dakon Monji aŋenagek nak Uŋun Amɨn yaŋ nandaŋ namdaŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak naga da nandak nandagon yo dɨma asat yaŋ nandakdaŋ. Dat da nayɨŋ dekgɨt uŋun baŋgɨn yosot yaŋ nandakdaŋ.
Aban paŋdet kabɨni da uŋun da manon but tobɨl dakon gen gat, ae dɨwarɨ wɨrɨrɨt dakon gen gat yoyɨŋ teŋteŋaŋba amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun da nandakdaŋ. Pi uŋun Jerusalem kokup papmon da wasaŋek akdaŋ.
Yaŋakwa amɨn madep uŋun da bɨkbɨgon Parisi amɨn dɨ akgwit uŋun da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdet, paŋdetgoni kɨrɨŋɨk yom.”
Kulup madep dɨma altaŋakwan jap pakbiyo aŋek mɨŋat pakpak awit. Yaŋ aŋek egakwa Noa tap wakgakon wɨgɨgɨt.
Aŋakwa Parisi amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Pɨndat, amɨn Sabat bɨsapmon nido gen teban yapmaŋek pi aŋ?”
Pol yaŋ yaŋban kɨla amɨn madep, ae gapman dakon mibɨltok amɨn madep, ae Benaisi, ae amɨn dɨwarɨ amɨn madep gat yɨkgwit uŋun kɨsi pɨdaŋ akgwit.
Yaŋ aŋek uŋun da kwenon jap naŋek aeni tapmɨm pagɨt. Sol gɨldat kabi dɨ Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn gat Damaskus egɨpgwit.
mani nak uŋudon dɨma egapbo kɨmakgɨt do tagɨ nandɨsat. Nido nak ji dakon nandaŋ gadat paŋteban ak do nandɨsat. Kɨlɨ uŋudon kɨno.”
Pi aban yokwinin madepsi taŋ nimaŋ yaŋ pɨndatdaŋ. Yokwini dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun nak dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ namaŋ.
Uŋun yo morap altaŋakwa amɨn kɨmakba yopmaŋgaŋ tamo wɨtdal kɨŋakwa Piŋkop dakon amɨn morapmɨ kalɨp kɨmakba yopbi uŋun pɨdawit.
Kwen busuŋɨkon mibɨlɨ nido aŋakgwit uŋun dakon but pɨso yaŋ mandawit, ON YESU, JUDA AMƗN DAKON KƗLA AMƗN MADEPNI
Kɨŋakwan mɨŋat kɨnda uŋungwan agɨpgɨt. Uŋun dagaŋ mok aŋek yawini maŋakwa bɨlak 12 yaŋ agɨt, mani amɨn kɨnda da arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋkɨlek agagɨ.
“Ason Kwen Kokup Piŋkop aŋkɨsino. Mɨktɨmon amɨn galak taŋ yomɨsak uŋun kabɨkon but yawot tosak.”
Uŋun wit dakon sɨbɨt sɨbɨt wɨrɨrɨt kɨndap kɨrɨŋni kɨsitnikon taŋakwan apdɨsak. Abɨŋek bamɨ kokwinɨk tamonikon yopmaŋek sɨbɨt sɨbɨt wɨrɨrɨk maban kɨndap kɨmot kɨmorɨ mɨni uŋudon sokdaŋ.”
Yaŋ aban Yesu da tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Emat agak sɨba yɨgɨkon sɨmɨl! Dat da tepmɨ pakeŋ do nandɨsak uŋun dɨma pakeŋ yaŋ nandɨsal, ma?”
“Yoni mɨni amɨn egek kɨmakban aŋelo da abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ yɨpba Abraham gat egɨpgumal. Egakwal yoni morapmɨ amɨn uŋun yo kɨsi kɨmakban wayɨkgwit.
Paŋdetni gen uŋun nandaŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, yum dɨpmɨn pokdok kaŋ, sotni dagaŋ kɨŋakwan kɨlek tosak.”
Uŋun do Piŋkop da mɨŋat wɨli kɨlɨ paŋmuwukgɨt, do amɨn da dɨma paŋwasekdo.”
“Peni da padɨge si aŋakba kɨmotjak do gen pikon yɨpdɨsak. Ae dat da monjɨ gwayoni yaŋ gɨn akdɨsak. Aŋakwa monjɨ gwayoni da meŋi datniyo do uwal aŋek si dapba kɨmotni do amɨn yoyɨkdaŋ.
“Uŋun do aŋek ji kaŋ kɨmotni. Ji yut dakon ami ni bɨsapmon apjak uŋun dɨma nandaŋ. Apjak bɨsap uŋun pɨlɨndo bo kalbi binap bo pup da gen yosok bɨsapmon bo wɨsa dagokdo uŋun ji dɨma nandaŋ.
Yoyɨŋakwan Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ Yesu gen yokwi kɨnda yaŋban kaŋek gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋ nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gen tebanin da amɨn kɨnda mɨŋatni tagɨ kwɨnɨtjak do yosok bo dɨma?”
Yesu yaŋ yaŋakwan obip amɨn kɨnda da mogɨm kulbak aŋagek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon geni kobogɨ gen tagɨ naŋ iyɨsat yaŋ nandɨsal ma?”
Mani gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon Tair gat Saidon kokupmon amɨn gat da kobogɨ do jɨgɨ tagapmɨ paŋakwa ji da kobogɨ do jɨgɨ madepsi pakdaŋ.
Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Gak ni gen teban do yosol?” Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn dɨma dapba kɨmotni, mɨŋat eyo kɨlɨ abi ji yumabi dɨma ani, yo kabo dɨma noni, top gen yaŋek amɨn notji yum dogɨn gen pikon dɨma yopni,
Aŋakwan Josep uŋun Maria monjɨ kwapni kɨnda awɨlak yaŋ nandaŋek yɨpmaŋ det do nandagɨt. Mani eni amɨn kɨlegɨ do amɨn morap da ɨŋamon Maria mayagɨ ɨm do dɨma nandagɨt. Yaŋ do aŋek pasɨlɨkon da kɨrɨŋɨk ɨm do nandagɨt.
Agapno wɨsa dagaŋban Saidon kokupmon paŋkɨ akgɨmaŋ. Uŋudon Julius da Pol do nandaban tagɨ agɨt do yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak kwi notgoni da yo nido wadasal uŋun tagɨ aŋpulugoni.”
Bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu paŋdetni gat bot kɨndakon wɨgek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda do kɨno.” Yaŋ yaŋban kɨwit.
Obɨŋ jap noknok tamokon jap naŋ yɨgek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, jikon da kɨnda da nak uwalno da kɨsiron nepdɨsak. Uŋun amɨn nin gat yɨgek jap nomaŋ.”
“Kɨŋakwa mukwa sogok amɨn kɨnda uŋun kosit naŋgɨn pɨgɨgɨt. Pɨgɨ amɨn uŋun kaŋek aŋpekwolek kosit ɨleŋ naŋ yapmaŋ kɨgɨt.
Uŋun amɨn nandaban amɨn morapmɨ obɨŋ yapmaŋ kɨŋakwa nandaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nibaŋ aŋ?”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yagɨt, “Uŋun do aŋek yaŋ dayɨsat, ji egɨp egɨpji do nandaba kɨk aŋek jap pakbiyo ni baŋ noneŋ yaŋ dɨma nandani. Ae gɨptɨmji do nandaŋek ɨmal dukon baŋ paneŋ, yaŋ nandaŋek nandaba kɨk dɨma ani. Egɨp egɨpji da jap yapmaŋdak, ae gɨptɨmji da ɨmal yapmaŋdak.
yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Abɨgɨt. Mɨŋatjok uŋun dɨma kuŋwak, uŋun yum dɨpmɨn pokdok.” Yesu da yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek jɨkgo yanjaŋ ɨmgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek amɨn uŋun pɨdaŋ yutnikon kɨgɨt.
Galili kɨk do Samaria Provins binap naŋ kɨgɨt.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, ji on akgaŋ kabɨkon da dɨ dɨma kɨmagek Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni kokdaŋ.”
Tɨmɨkba pakgɨmaŋ da wɨsa dagokdo Pol nin gat kɨsi Jems kok do kɨgɨmaŋ. Kɨŋ altaŋek paŋmuwukbi dakon kɨla amɨn kɨsi morap uŋudon gɨn Jems gat ekwa pɨndakgɨmaŋ.
Aba Tɨpdomon tepmɨ madepsi nandaŋek egɨpgut. Egek sɨŋtaŋban wɨkwanek Abraham dubagɨsikon Lasarus gat kapmat kapmat yɨgakwal pɨndakgɨt.
Mandaŋ dagaŋ ɨdapmon yɨpmaŋ aŋabɨŋ mɨŋatjok uŋun do ɨban aŋkɨ meŋi do ɨmgut.
Jon pini aban mudok do aŋakwan yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Ji nak do namɨn yaŋ nandaŋ? Nak ji da jomjom aŋ ɨmaŋ amɨn dɨma. Mani nandani, amɨn wukwisi kɨnda nak da buŋon noldak. Nak uŋun amɨn dakon pɨŋbisi egɨsat do uŋun dakon kandap gwɨl napni nak da arɨpmɨ dɨma wɨtdalɨ.’
Amɨn uŋun da gen uŋun manjɨŋek Pilip yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Kombɨ amɨn uŋun namɨn do yosok, iyɨ do yosok bo amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda do yosok? Nayɨŋbɨ nandako.”
Amɨn kɨsi morap da dɨma kawit. Piŋkop da man bini yaŋ teŋteŋok ani do kokwinɨkgɨt kabɨ ninon gɨn altagɨt. Kɨmoron da pɨdaŋban nin uŋun gat jap pakbiyo agɨmaŋ.
Amɨn Kɨla Agakgo yɨpbɨ ninon apjak. Gak dakon gen guramɨt Kwen Kokup tosok, mɨktɨmon ninon yaŋ gɨn tosak.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yoni morapmɨ amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut, uŋun bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkni kɨldani toŋ tagɨsi ae ɨmalni gami baŋ paŋek yoni arɨpmɨsi taŋ ɨmɨŋakwa yaworɨsi egɨpgut.
Pɨgɨ gɨldat kapbɨ egakwan dabɨlɨ dɨma pɨsagɨt. Ae jap pakbiyo dɨma agɨt.
Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: Kristo uŋun kɨla amɨn madep Dewit dakon yawi dɨwat kabɨkon da altosak. Uŋun kalɨp Dewit da egɨpgut kokup Betlehem uŋudon altokdɨsak.”
Nak Jerusalem wɨgɨgɨm bɨsapmon Juda amɨn dakon mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨni gat, ae kɨla amɨni gat da uŋun amɨn gen yaŋ ɨmgwit. Yaŋ ɨmɨŋek suŋ agɨt dakon kobogɨ nak da yaŋ dagok aŋapbo kobogɨ yokwi abɨdosak do yawit.
Aŋtɨdok agɨt do Sakius uŋun tɨmtɨm yaŋek mibɨltaŋ kɨŋ pik kɨndap kɨndakon wɨgɨgɨt. Yesu uŋun onaŋ abɨsak do tagɨ kokeŋ yaŋon da nandaŋek wɨgɨgɨt.
“Do yaŋ dayɨsat, nak da kombɨ amɨn ae nandak nandak amɨn ae yoyɨŋdet amɨn yabekgo jikon apdaŋ. Apba ji da uŋun amɨn dɨwarɨ yolba pasal kokupmɨ kokupmɨ kɨkdaŋ. Aŋakwa dɨwarɨ tɨmɨgek dapba kɨmotdaŋ, ae dɨwarɨ tɨlak kɨndapmon dapdaŋ, ae dɨwarɨ muwut muwut yutjikon nap kɨrɨŋbaŋ baljokdaŋ.
Aŋek uŋun do nandaŋ kokwin aŋek egɨpgwit. Amɨn Tagɨ dakon tapmɨm taŋ ɨmgut, do yaŋ yawit, “Uŋun monjɨ tagaŋek niaŋ amɨn kɨnda egɨpdɨsak?”
“Ji Abraham, Aisak, Jekop, ae kombɨ amɨn kɨsisi Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak kokupmon ekwa pɨndatdaŋ. Mani ji maba waŋga kɨŋ mudokdaŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon ji kunam tagek iyoŋ iyoŋ yaŋ tɨdaŋek egɨpdaŋ.
Yo uŋun kosirɨ kapbɨ altaŋ namɨŋek uŋudon gɨn aeni Kwen Kokup wɨgɨgɨt.
Aŋakwan amɨn kabi kɨnda da amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi kɨnda wamaŋ aŋaŋ opgwit. Uŋun wayɨgon yɨpba pagakwan aŋaŋ Yesu da akgɨron awɨgɨk do awit.
Kundu gat mɨktɨm gat pasɨldamal, mani nak dakon gen uŋun dɨmasi pasɨldɨsak.”
Yoyɨŋ dek mudaŋek Saimon yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Tɨmɨsok dɨ gat kɨŋek pakbi ɨlarɨkon kɨŋek tap kɨlap sɨmɨl do yɨk yopba pɨgɨni.”
Nandaki. Don bɨsap kɨnda noman tokdɨsak. Uŋun bɨsapmon uwalgo da gak aŋgwasɨŋek mɨktɨm paŋabɨŋ dam madepgokon yopba tugaŋ wɨgɨkdaŋ. Aŋakwa terɨ terɨ da abɨŋ paŋdagat akdaŋ.
Pɨndagek yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Abraham dat, bupmɨ nandaŋ nam. Lasarus iyɨŋbɨ uŋun da pakbi jɨmjɨmjok dɨ kɨsirɨkon yopmaŋ paŋabɨŋ melnokon yopban tɨmɨsok dɨ yawotjak. Nak on kɨndapmon egek tepmɨ madepsi nandɨsat!’
Amɨn kɨnda mɨktɨm dakon yo morap paŋek egɨ kɨmotjak bɨsapmon iyɨ pasɨljak kaŋ, uŋun yo morap da arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋpulugokdaŋ.
Yesu dubagɨkon akban kaŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek Yesu da buron kɨŋ gawak ɨmgut.
“Amɨn butdasi galak taŋ damaŋ baŋgɨn butdasi galak taŋ yomni kaŋ, ji amɨn tagɨ dɨma. Yokwi pakpak amɨn uŋun kɨsi amɨn butdasi galak taŋ yomaŋ baŋ butdasi galak taŋ yomaŋ.
Ae gak dakon gen yaŋ teŋteŋok amɨngo Stiwen aŋakba kɨmakgɨt bɨsapmon nak kapmatjok agek tɨp baŋ aŋakgwit amɨn dakon ɨmal dubakni ɨlɨk yopmaŋ naba kɨla agɨm. Aŋek pɨndagapbo Stiwen aŋakba kɨmakban nandako tagɨsi agɨt.’
Aŋek yaŋ yoŋ, ‘Nin kalɨpsi babɨknin da bɨsapmon egɨpgumaŋ tam, nin paŋpulugaŋek kombɨ amɨn dɨma dapnom.’
Amɨn Tagɨ dakon aŋelo kɨnda da Pilip yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak mɨktɨm kɨbɨrɨ tɨmon kosit kɨnda Jerusalem da Gasa kwaŋ uŋudon pɨgɨki.”
Yaŋ yaŋban Sunduk da Yesu iyɨŋ aŋaŋ Jerusalem kokup papmon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ Telagɨ Yut Madep da kwenon awɨgɨ yɨpmaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda yaŋ tosok: ‘Uŋun da aŋeloni yoyɨŋban kɨlago tagɨsi ani. Ae kandapgo tɨpmon dɨma gɨtni yaŋ do aŋelo da gak kɨsit da kendak abɨŋ gepni.’ Gen yaŋ tosok, do gak asi Piŋkop dakon Monji kaŋ, gak amon mibɨlɨkon paŋ ma.”
Yesu gen on Pita kosit niaŋon da kɨmagek Piŋkop man madep ɨmjak uŋun do yagɨt. Yaŋ yaŋek iyɨgɨt, “Nak nolgi.”
Yaŋ aŋakwan kombɨ amɨn Aisaia da kalɨpsigwan gen mandagɨt uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ: “Iyɨ sotnin mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ iyɨ do tɨmɨgakwan kɨlek tagɨmaŋ.”
“Datno da yo morap kɨlɨ namgut. Dat uŋun dagɨn Monjɨ nandaŋ ɨmɨsak. Aŋek Monjɨ gat ae amɨn morap Monjɨ da Dat dakon mibɨlɨ yolɨsak, uŋun amɨn dagɨn Datno nandaŋ ɨmaŋ.”
“Pi monjɨni uŋun gen aŋaŋ uŋun amɨn kabɨkon aŋkɨwit, mani geni nandak do kuragɨ nandaŋek iyɨ da galak togon kɨŋ kɨŋ awit. Kɨnda uŋun pigagani kɨgɨt, ae kɨnda moneŋ ɨlɨt pinikon kɨgɨt.
Yaŋ aŋek mibɨltok Anaskon aŋkɨwit. Anas uŋun Kaiapas dakon yopmi. Uŋun bɨlagon Kaiapas da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn egɨpgut.
Mani nak da yaŋ dayɨsat, ji uwalji do but dasi galak taŋ yomni. Aŋek yokwi aŋdamaŋ amɨn do bɨsit ani.
Dewit uŋun Jesi dakon monji. Jesi uŋun Obet dakon monji. Obet uŋun Boas dakon monji. Boas uŋun Salmon dakon monji. Salmon uŋun Nason dakon monji.
Mani ji ninaŋ kok do kɨwit? Kombɨ amɨn kɨnda kok do kɨwit? Uŋun bamɨ, nak asisi dayɨsat, Jon da kombɨ amɨn dɨwarɨ yapmaŋ mudosok.
Yaŋ aŋek Yesu Saimon Pitakon opban yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak nak dakon kandap sugokdɨsal, ma?”
Yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn da gadat gadat tebaisi aŋakwa namɨn da ɨgayɨŋ namɨsak yaŋ nido yosol?”
Banabas uŋun Jon mani kɨnda Mak uŋun kɨsi abɨdaŋbal agɨpni do nandagɨt.
Iyɨŋban Amɨn Tagɨ da iyɨgɨt, “Gak kosit kɨnda mani Kosit Kɨlegɨ yaŋ yoŋ uŋudon kɨŋ Judas da yutnon wɨgɨki. Wɨgɨ Tasas amɨn kɨnda mani Sol uŋun do yoyɨki. Uŋun amɨn bɨsit pi aŋek egɨsak.
amɨn kɨsirɨ gɨreŋɨkbi kɨnda ekwan kagɨt. Amɨn yɨkgwit uŋun da Yesu gen teban kɨnda yapmaŋakwan gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋ nandaŋek iyɨwit, “Sabat bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda da notni kɨnda aŋmɨlɨp asak kaŋ, uŋun gen teban yapmaŋdak?”
“Israel dakon Piŋkop da abɨŋ amɨni yokwikon baŋ yumaŋ naŋ nipgut, do Amɨn Tagɨ aŋkɨsino.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Mibɨlɨ yaŋ do nak yaŋ kɨlɨ dayɨgɨm, ‘Amɨn kɨnda Dat da dɨma aŋtagap asak kaŋ, nagon arɨpmɨ dɨma opjak.’ ”
Yaŋ yaŋban iyɨwit, “Gak dakon gen Juda amɨn dɨ da papiakon mandaŋ yɨpba apban dɨma kagɨmaŋ. Ae Juda amɨn kɨnda da Judia mɨktɨm da ɨdon abɨŋek gak do gen yokwi kɨnda dɨma niyɨŋban nandagɨmaŋ.
Juda amɨn da uŋun amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni egɨpgut da sɨŋtagɨt uŋun do nandaba bamɨ dɨma agɨt. Yaŋ nandawit do uŋun amɨn dakon meŋi datniyo apjil do gen yɨpgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban gen kɨnda kalɨp yagɨt uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ: “Amɨn kabɨ uŋun nak do namgul uŋun kɨnda dɨma yɨpbo pasɨlgɨt.”
Nandaba Pol Ibru genon da gen yaŋakwan upbalap dɨma aŋek tayaŋgok egɨpgwit. Yaŋ aŋakwa Pol da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Yaŋ yaŋba yaŋsi yoyɨkdɨsat, ‘Yokwi pakpak amɨn, ji dɨma nandaŋ damɨsat. Nepmaŋ dek kɨŋ mudabɨt!’ ”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, yo aeni kalugɨ mudoni uŋun bɨsap madepmon Amɨn Dakon Monji man madep paŋek kɨla amɨn madep yɨtyɨt tamoni tɨlɨmɨ toŋ uŋudon yɨtdɨsak. Aŋakwan ji nak nolgaŋ amɨn uŋun bɨsapmon kɨla amɨn madep tamo 12 kabɨ uŋudon yɨgek Israel amɨn kabi 12 dakon gen kokwin kɨla agak pi akdaŋ.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Gen kɨnda babɨk da abɨdawit uŋun ji kɨlɨ nandawit. Gen uŋun yaŋ: ‘Amɨn dɨma dapba kɨmotni. Amɨn kɨnda da amɨn kɨnda aŋakban kɨmotjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn gen pikon kɨsak.’
Sonda wɨsa dagokdosi mɨŋat kabɨ uŋun yo kɨbaŋɨ tagɨsi kɨlɨ paŋkosit awit uŋun tɨmɨgek tɨp kɨnamon kɨwit.
Yaŋ aŋek egakwa monji mibɨltogɨ pigaga egɨpgut da yutnon obɨŋ aŋkapmat aŋek nandaban amɨn da kap kɨsɨk kɨsɨkyo awit.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, nak wain ae dɨma naŋek egɨ wɨgɨ Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Agak kokupmon don wain kalugɨ nokeŋ.”
On gen teban bamot da gen teban dɨwarɨ gat ae kombɨ amɨn dakon gen morap kɨsi tɨmɨkgamal.”
Kokup kɨndakon kɨŋakwa not dɨma aŋ daba kaŋ, uŋun kokup dakon kosit madepmon agek yaŋ yoyɨni,
Mɨŋat amɨn morapyo mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun bɨsap madep altaŋban kokdaŋ.
Jon dakon paŋdetni gat ae Parisi amɨn gat uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egɨpgwit. Aŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋun Yesukon kɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit: “Jon dakon paŋdetni gat ae Parisi amɨn dakon paŋdetni gat uŋun Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egakwa gak dakon paŋdetgoni nido jap naŋek ekwaŋ?”
Yoyɨŋban aŋagakwa Pol da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da gɨtdɨsak. Gak yut dakon pompom kɨlegɨ yombem, mani mukgwan nɨp da naŋba nɨtnɨraŋbi. Gak gen teban guramɨkdat yaŋ nandaŋek nak gen pikon nep do abɨl da yɨkdal. Mani gaga gen teban yapmaŋek nɨtni do yoyɨsal.”
Asisi Erot ae Pontias Pailat, ae Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ amɨn, ae Israel amɨn uŋun kɨsi da on kokup papmon telagɨ oman amɨngo Yesu gak da pigo asak do manjɨgɨl, uŋun amɨn abɨŋ yɨp do muwukgwit.
Kɨŋakwal Yesu gat domdom aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Wɨsa dagokdo tagɨsi.” Yaŋ yoyɨŋban kandapmɨ abɨdaŋek gawak ɨmgumal.
(Kalɨp Epesas kokup papmon amɨn kɨnda mani Tropimus uŋun Pol gat Jerusalem kokup papmon ekwal pɨndakgwit, uŋun do aŋek gen uŋun yawit. Uŋun amɨn Pol da abɨdaŋban Telagɨ Yut Madepmon wɨgɨgɨmal yaŋ nandawit.)
Aŋwa Yapyap Bɨlak do nandaŋek jap paŋkosit ak bɨsap, gɨldat binap 12 kilok agɨt. Pailat da Juda amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kabɨt, kɨla amɨn madepji oni.”
Egakwa Amɨn Tagɨ dakon aŋelo kɨnda da altaŋ yomgut. Aban Amɨn Tagɨ dakon teŋteŋɨ da teŋteŋaŋ yoban madepsi pasalgwit.
Nak da ji do aŋek Dat bɨsit iyɨkeŋ yaŋ dɨma dayɨsat. Dɨma. Ji nak do but dasi galak taŋ namaŋ, ae nak Piŋkopmon da apgum yaŋ nandaba bamɨ asak. Yaŋ aŋ, do Dat da iyɨ but dasi galak taŋ damɨsak. Do uŋun bɨsapmon ji nak da manon Dat bɨsit iyɨkdaŋ.
Pailat gen uŋun nandaŋek Yesu yɨpban ɨsal kɨsak do kosit wɨsɨk agɨt. Mani Juda amɨn da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Gak uŋun amɨn yɨpbɨ kɨsak kaŋ, gak Sisa dakon notni dɨma. Amɨn iyɨ do nak kɨla amɨn madep yaŋ yosok uŋun Sisa dakon uwalni.”
Saŋbeŋakwa yabekbi kabɨ da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ morapmɨ aba pɨndakgwit, do mɨŋat amɨnyo da sot amɨn morapmɨ paŋapgwit. Paŋabɨŋ tobaron ae yalɨŋ poron yopba kosit obakon pakgwit. Yaŋ nandaŋek awit: Pita kosit obanaŋ obɨŋ kɨŋakwan gɨldat paŋopmon wupni da sot amɨn dɨ wɨtjɨŋban kɨlek toni yaŋ do yopba pakgwit.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda da ‘Kristo oni!’ bo ‘Asoni!’ yaŋ yaŋban kaŋ, top yosok yaŋ nandani.
Yo morap don noman taŋ mudaŋakwa nandaŋ gadat ani yaŋ do mibɨltok gen on dayɨsat.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun do tɨlak kɨnda ako mibɨlɨ nandani. Amɨn kɨnda kokup dubagɨ kɨndakon kɨk do aŋek pi monjɨni yaŋ yoban opba yo kabɨni kɨla ani do yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “On mɨktɨm amɨni mɨnikon bret morapmɨ dukon baŋ on mɨŋat amɨn morapyo yomno noni?”
“Gak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ amɨn dɨma yoyɨki. Aŋek mukwa sogok amɨnon kɨŋek gɨptɨmgo yolɨki. Aŋek Moses da yagɨt uŋun da tɨlagon paret aŋaki amɨn da asi kɨlek tal yaŋ gandani.”
Nin tap wakga abɨdaŋek kokup pap Sirakus kɨŋ gɨldat kapbɨ uŋudon egɨpgumaŋ.
Yesu gen uŋun yaŋakwan muwut muwut yut dakon kɨla amɨn Jairus da yutnon da amɨn kɨnda apgut. Abɨŋek Jairus yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gwago kɨlɨ kuŋwak, do yoyɨŋdet ɨsal dogɨn dɨma iyɨŋbɨ kɨsak.”
Yum yo bamorɨ dogɨn gen emat awit. Kɨnda uŋun iyɨ Piŋkop aŋpak niaŋsi aŋek gawak ɨmaŋ uŋun do yawit, ae kɨnda uŋun amɨn kɨnda kɨmakgɨt mani Yesu do gen emat awit. Mani Pol da Yesu uŋun pɨdagɨt da egɨsak yaŋ yosok.
iyɨŋba Yesu kɨŋ kɨsitnikon abɨdaŋek ɨlɨkban pɨdagɨt. Yaŋ aban sotni yɨpmaŋakwan jap noni do oman agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋakwan Sebedi dakon monji bamot gat meŋi gat Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋek meŋi da ŋwakbeŋ aŋek Yesu da yo kɨnda aŋ yomjak do iyɨgɨt.
Yaŋ nandat aŋek egakwal amɨn jomjom aŋegek Sekaraia nido bɨsap dubak Telagɨ Yut Madepmon egɨsak yaŋ nandaŋek but morap awit.
mani ɨmalni naŋ kukwaŋek pasal molaŋ molaŋ kɨgɨt.
Judas bret uŋun abɨdaŋakwan Sunduk da burɨkon pɨgɨgɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Yo ak do nandal uŋun tepmɨsi abi.”
Amɨn kɨnda jikon da mibɨltok amɨn egɨp do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn mɨŋat amɨn morap dakon oman amɨni egek mibɨltok amɨn asak.
Mani Piŋkop da iyɨ tapmɨm namɨŋakwan koŋ yoldat kaŋ, Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni jikon kɨlɨ abɨk.
Piŋkop da amɨn kɨnda yabekban apgut, uŋun mani Jon.
“Mani Samaria amɨn kɨnda da uŋun kositnaŋ obɨŋ amɨn uŋun kaŋek bupmɨ nandaŋ ɨmgut.
Moses yaŋ aŋek yaŋ nandagɨt, ‘Piŋkop da nak aŋpulugaŋban Israel amɨn uwal da kɨsiron baŋ tɨmɨtdɨsat yaŋ nandaŋ namdaŋ.’ Mani Israel amɨn Moses do yaŋ dɨma nandawit.
Moses da nak do gen mandagɨt. Geni do nandaba bamɨ asak tam, nakyo kɨsi nandaŋ gadaŋ nabam.
Yaŋban Amɨn Tagɨ da yagɨt, “Oman monjɨ kɨnda nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi ae pi agakni tagɨsi, uŋuden oman monjɨ amɨn tagɨni da oman monjɨni dɨwarɨ kɨlani asak do manjɨsak. Yaŋ aban jap yomyom bɨsapmon japni yomɨŋ yomɨŋ asak.
“Amɨn dɨwarɨ paŋpulugagɨt da nido iyɨ aŋpulugok do aŋtɨdok asak? On Israel amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn madepni ma! Kaŋ tɨlak kɨndapmon da pɨŋban kaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmneŋ.
Yaŋban amɨn kɨsi da geni yaŋ aŋtobɨl ɨmgwit, “Nin gat ae mɨŋat monjɨyonin gat da kɨmotjak dakon kobogɨ tagɨ paneŋ.”
Uŋun da pɨŋ pi aban mɨktɨm amɨn morap aŋpak yokwi gat, ae aŋpak kɨlegɨ gat, ae Piŋkop da amɨn gen pikon yopdɨsak gat dakon mibɨlɨ kɨsi pakyaŋsi nandaba pɨsokdɨsak.
Mani Parisi amɨn gat ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat da japmɨsi nandaŋ ɨmɨŋek iyɨ gɨn yaŋ nandat aŋek Yesu niaŋsi aŋ ɨmno yaŋ yawit.
Yaŋ yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat ae kɨla amɨn dɨwarɨ gat da gen yaŋ ɨmɨŋba gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma yoyɨgɨt.
Yo morap do nak da manon bɨsit yoni, uŋun nak akdɨsat.”
Yesu Judia yɨpmaŋek Galili kɨŋ wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ uŋun aban kosit bamot agɨt.
Yaŋban paŋdetni nandaŋ wɨrɨpdagek yaŋ yawit, “Yaŋ kaŋ namɨn amɨn da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdosak?”
Yaŋ yaŋek monjɨ uŋun aŋakba kɨmakgɨt. Kɨmakban bumjotni pigaga naŋ maba waŋga kɨgɨt.
Judas uŋun yoni mɨni amɨn do nandaba kɨk aŋek dɨma yagɨt. Iyɨ uŋun kabo noknok amɨn kɨnda Yesu gat paŋdetni gat dakon moneŋ kɨnam kɨla agɨt, do bɨsap morapmɨ moneŋ yopgwit uŋun Judas da kabo tɨmɨkgɨt.
Uŋun monjɨ, wup gɨpyo kɨsi tapmɨmɨ toŋsi tagagɨt. Aŋakwan mɨktɨm amɨn dɨma ekwaŋ tɨmon egakwan don noman taŋban Israel amɨn da kawit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Telagɨ Wup da Yesu Sunduk da aŋkewaljak do mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon aŋkɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek yagɨt, “Ji gen uŋun nandaŋ uŋun pakyaŋsi nandani. Ji Piŋkop dakon gen nandaŋek guramɨtni kaŋ, Piŋkop da saŋbeŋek damdɨsak. Mani geni dɨma nandani kaŋ, saŋbeŋek dɨma damdɨsak.
Aŋakwan mɨŋat amɨn morapyo uŋun kaŋ wurɨpdagek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiŋek yawit, “Abɨsok yo ŋwakŋwarɨsi altaŋban komaŋ.”
Kabo noknok bamorɨ Yesu gat kɨsi dapgwit. Kɨnda amɨnsi tetdo, ae kɨnda gwandeŋ tet do tɨlak kɨndapmon dapmaŋ dapmaŋ awit.
Nasaret kokup yɨpmaŋek Kapaneam kokupmon kɨŋ uŋudon egɨpgut. Kapaneam uŋun Galili Pakbi Ɨdap ɨleŋɨkon, Sebulan ae Naptali mɨktɨmon uŋudon tosok.
Kɨŋ Juda amɨn kɨnda kagɨt mani Akwila. Akwila uŋun Pontus mɨktɨmon nani kɨnda. Kɨlɨ yaŋgok mɨŋatni Prisila gat Itali mɨktɨm yɨpmaŋek opgumal. Itali mɨktɨm mibɨlɨ yaŋ do yɨpmaŋek apgumal. Rom dakon kɨla amɨn madep Klodias da Juda amɨn kɨsi morap Rom kokup pap uŋun yɨpmaŋ kɨŋ mudoni do gen tebai yɨpgut. Pol uŋun amɨn wam pɨndat do kɨgɨt.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda da mɨŋat monjɨyo da Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak abɨdoŋ uŋun da tɨlak dɨma abɨdoni kaŋ, uŋungwan arɨpmɨ dɨma pɨgɨkdaŋ.”
Yoyɨŋba Gerasa mɨktɨm dakon mɨŋat amɨn morap kɨsi pasol pasol madepsi nandaŋek Yesu uŋun yopmaŋ dek kɨsak do iyɨwit. Iyɨŋba boron wɨgek yopmaŋ kɨgɨt.
Kɨŋakwa mɨrɨm madepsi aŋakwan pakbi madepsi tamalɨkgɨt.
Nin da bɨkbɨgon peni padɨgeyo 7 kabɨ egɨpgwit. Mibɨltok nani uŋun mɨŋat paŋek monjɨ mɨni egek kɨmakban padɨge da kwabatni pagɨt.
Ae bret abɨdaŋek Piŋkop ya yaŋ iyɨŋek bret uŋun paŋdagaŋ yomɨŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “On nak dakon gɨptɨm tɨmno ji do parekdat. On naŋek nak do nandaŋek egɨpni.”
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da yagɨt, “Nandaŋ gadatji mɨni amɨn, ji aŋpakji yokwisi. Nak bɨsap niaŋ da ji gat egek jɨgɨsi guramɨk dabeŋ? Monjɨgo ɨdon aŋop.”
Yaŋban Agripa da Pol yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok gen nayɨŋbɨ Kristo Dakon Amɨn kɨnda dagokeŋ yaŋ nandɨsal, ma?”
Uŋun da gen teban mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ jɨgɨsi guramɨtni do dayaŋ, mani iyɨ paŋpulugaŋba guramɨtni do kɨsitjok kɨnda dɨmasi yɨpmaŋgaŋ.
Gen uŋun amɨn dagaŋban nin gat egɨpgumaŋ. Egakwan Dat da monji kaloŋɨ yabekban pɨgɨt uŋun dakon tɨlɨmni kagɨmaŋ. Nandaŋ yawot ae aŋpak bamɨsi uŋun amɨnon tugagɨt.
Saimon Pita da emat agak sɨbani ɨlɨk mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon oman monjɨ dakon mɨragɨ amɨn tet nani mandaŋ dagagɨt. Oman monjɨ uŋun dakon mani Malkus.
Nak Juda amɨn ae Grik amɨn but tobɨl aŋek Piŋkopmon kɨŋek Amɨn Tagɨnin Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmni do gen madepsi yaŋ teŋteŋagɨm.
Bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu iyɨ gɨn bɨsit pi agɨt. Uŋun bɨsapmon paŋdetni kɨsi uŋudon egɨpgwit. Egɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kabɨ madep da nak do namɨn yaŋ yoŋ?”
Yaŋban kɨla amɨn da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, monjino dɨma kɨmagakwan tepmɨ pɨki.”
Yaŋ aŋakwa Yesu da paŋdetni tɨmɨkban pakbi ɨdapmon kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Galili amɨn morapmɨsi da yolgwit. Ae uŋun gɨn dɨma, Judia mɨktɨmon da,
Yaŋban gen kobogɨ arɨpmɨ dɨma iyɨgɨ yaŋ kawit.
Aŋakwan tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋagek emat amɨn da satu wasok aŋek ɨmalni kokwinɨk tɨmɨkgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋek datni ni man naŋ yok do nandɨsak yaŋ do kɨsit tɨlak aŋ ɨmgwit.
Dewit uŋun Piŋkop da yutnon wɨgɨ bret Piŋkop do parekbi uŋun tɨmɨkgɨt. Bret uŋun mukwa sogok amɨn dagɨn tagɨ noknogɨ. Mani Dewit da naŋek amɨn kabɨni kɨsi do yomgut.”
Gen yaŋ tosok do amɨn kɨnda kulabɨgɨ aŋnoman aneŋ. Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨnon da wasaŋek Yesu nipmaŋ wɨgɨgɨt, ae amɨn morap nin gat saŋbek saŋbek egapno Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu kɨŋ ap agɨt, uŋun amɨn kɨnda naŋ kulabɨk aneŋ. Uŋun amɨn dasi nin gat pi aŋek Yesu kɨmoron da pɨdagɨt uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋok aneŋ.”
“Yoyɨŋdet, Moses da gen kɨnda yaŋ mandagɨt, ‘Amɨn kɨnda monji mɨni da kɨmagakwan mɨŋatni ɨsal egɨpjak kaŋ, padɨge da paŋakwan yawi dɨwatni dɨma pasɨlni yaŋ do monjɨ paŋalasak.’
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn sotni mɨni uŋun wuda wamagon dɨma kwaŋ. Amɨn sotni toŋ uŋun dagɨn wuda wamagon kwaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak da yo asat uŋun abɨsok dɨma nandabɨ pɨsosok, mani don nandabɨ pɨsokdaŋ.”
Amɨn kɨnda Piŋkop dakon gen guramɨtjak kaŋ, uŋun da geno dakon mibɨlɨ tagɨ nandɨsak. Piŋkop dakon gen naŋ yosot, bo naga da nandak nandagon da yosot uŋun tagɨ kokwinɨtjak.
Aŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak nin gat tɨmɨsok dɨ gat egek don kɨki.” Yaŋ iyɨŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpneŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek mɨŋat amɨnyo yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji kaŋ kɨmotni. Yo mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ tɨmɨt tɨmɨt dakon galagɨ dɨ pabam. Yo kabɨsi uŋun morapmɨsi kaŋ, uŋun da egɨp egɨp bamɨsi arɨpmɨ dɨma damdaŋ.”
“Kɨŋakwa amɨn mɨŋat pak do agɨt uŋun apgut. Apban mɨŋat tagap taŋek egɨpgwit uŋun gat soŋnok ak do yutnon wɨgakwa yoma sopgwit.
Gak da nak yabekbɨ mɨktɨmon pɨgɨm. Yaŋgɨn nak da amɨn kabɨno mɨktɨmon yabekdat.
Uŋun bɨsapmon mɨŋat monjɨ kwapni toŋ, ae mɨŋat monjɨ mum noŋ uŋun bupmɨsi.
Mani ‘Amɨn da yabekgɨt’ yaŋ iyɨneŋ kaŋ, uŋun kɨsi tagɨ dɨma asak, nido amɨn morapmɨ da Jon do kombɨ amɨn bamɨsi kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋ. Do Jon dakon man bin aŋupbal aneŋ kaŋ nindapdaŋ.” Yaŋ do si pasalek
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji Piŋkop dakon gen teban yum pɨndagek dɨsi dakon yaŋ teban tok gen guramɨkgaŋ.
Gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ nak da ɨŋamon telagɨsi ae kɨlegɨsi egɨ aŋaŋ kɨkdaŋ.’
Nak gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ nandako dɨma pɨsagɨt do niaŋon da gen kokwin kɨlegɨ abeŋ yaŋ do aŋtɨdok agɨm. Do Pol yaŋ iyɨgɨm, ‘Gak Jerusalem wɨgɨ nak da ɨŋamon agaki gen on yaŋ gameŋ uŋudon nandakeŋ do tagɨ nandɨsal?’
Yaŋ nandaŋakwa mɨŋat wɨliyo morapmɨ da Amɨn Tagɨ nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmɨŋek paŋmuwukbi kabɨkon saŋbewit.
