Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Pi ami da abɨŋ uŋun amɨn yokwi kobogɨ yo yokwisi aŋyomdɨsak. Aŋek wain pi uŋun amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ da kɨsiron yɨpban uŋun da wain sop pakpak bɨsapmon bamɨ tagɨ paŋ ɨmni.”
Amɨn kɨnda but dasi dɨma galak taŋ namɨsak, uŋun amɨn nak dakon gen dɨma guramɨkdak. Gen on nandaŋ uŋun nak dakon gen dɨma, gen on Dat yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun dakon gen.
On man sɨlɨp uŋun Yesu Kristo dakon babɨkni dakon man sɨlɨp. Yesu uŋun Dewit da kabɨkon nani. Aŋakwan Dewit uŋun Abraham da kabɨkon nani.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn tagɨni da uŋun oman monjɨ iyɨŋban yo morapni kɨla akdɨsak.
Aŋakwa Yesu da gen yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok ji gat egek yabekban pɨgɨm amɨnon tobɨl wɨgɨkeŋ.
Ba-Yesu uŋun gapman dakon mibɨltok amɨn mani Segius Paulus uŋun dakon paŋpulugokni egɨpgut. Segius Paulus uŋun nandak nandakni wukwisi. Sol gat Banabas gat da obɨŋ Piŋkop dakon gen yaŋbal nandɨsak do yaŋ yomgut.
Nandaŋ pɨsoni. Yut kɨnda dakon ami kalbi kabo noknok ni bɨsapmon apdɨsak yaŋ nandagɨt tam, kɨla aŋakwan yutni arɨpmɨ dɨma tuwɨlban.
Yaŋ aban amɨn bamot dabɨlni pɨsaŋban kaŋ nandaŋyo agɨmal. Yaŋ aŋakwal uŋudon gɨn pasɨlakwan ae saŋbeŋek dɨma kagɨmal.
Yaŋban mɨŋat gɨmoŋ uŋun da waŋga kɨŋ meŋi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Ni yo naŋ namjak do iyɨkeŋ?” Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Kɨŋ Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn uŋun dakon busuŋɨ uŋun do iyɨki.”
Nak naga dɨma nandaŋ ɨmgum, mani Israel amɨn kabɨ da uŋun amɨn kaŋ nandaŋyo ani do aŋek telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomɨŋek apgum.”
“Nin Gen Bin Tagɨsi dayamaŋ. Piŋkop da kalɨp babɨknin yaŋ teban tok kɨnda aŋ yomgut uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt. Gwakni kabɨ nin da bɨsapmon Yesu kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdaŋban gen yagɨt uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt. Kap Papia 2 kon gen uŋun yaŋ mandabi: ‘Gak Monjɨno, nak abɨsok gak dakon Datgo asat.’
Gen uŋun yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Babɨknin da mɨktɨm kɨbɨrɨ tɨmon mana nawit. Uŋun dakon gen Piŋkop da papiakon yaŋ mandabi da tosok: ‘Kwen Kokup dakon bret amɨn do yoban nawit.’ Do gak niaŋ abi? Tɨlak tapmɨmɨ toŋ niaŋensi kɨnda naŋ abɨ kaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ gamneŋ?”
Pita uŋun kokup morap kɨsi agek Lida kokupmon kwan Piŋkop dakon amɨn kabɨ gat egɨpgwit.
iyɨ da kokupmon kɨgɨt. Uŋudon Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgɨ amɨn yoyɨŋ degakwan tamtam yaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Nandaŋ kokwin tagɨsi ae wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ agak dakon tapmɨm dukwan baŋ pagɨt?
Yaŋ nandaŋakwa Yesu da yoyɨŋban opba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ dakon kɨla amɨni dakon mibɨlɨ dɨsi nandaŋ. Uŋun iyɨ do nandaba wukwanek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyoni da geni guramɨk kɨmotni do nandaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋek yaŋ teban tok gen kɨnda yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo nido nayɨki, tagɨ gabeŋ. Mɨktɨmno terɨ kɨnda pɨdaŋ gak do tagɨ gabeŋ.”
Iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn monjɨ dakon datni da madepsi yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak nandaŋ gadasat, mani nandaŋ gadatno uŋun madep dɨma, do nak aŋpuluga!”
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋek Galili mɨktɨm da binapgwan kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Yesu paŋdetni yoyɨŋdet ak do nandagɨt, do gen bini amɨn da dɨma nandani do si pasɨlek kɨwit. Aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji don amɨn da kɨsiron yɨpba aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Kɨmak gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Aŋek don monjini gat Josua gat da uŋun ɨmal yut abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ Piŋkop da amɨn kabɨ morapmɨ yolban abɨgɨwit uŋun mɨktɨmon aŋkɨ yɨpgwit. Aŋkɨ yɨpba agakwan wɨgɨ Dewit dakon bɨsap don apgut.
Nak Piŋkop gawak ɨmɨsat. Nak uŋun dakon amɨn. Uŋun dakon aŋelo kɨnda da kalbi abɨŋ nak da kapmatjok agek
Nikodemus, uŋun kalɨp Yesukon kɨgɨt, uŋun kɨla amɨn gat Parisi gat da kabɨkon nani kɨnda. Uŋun da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Mibɨlɨ niaŋon da on nap teban kɨsitnokon yɨpgwit uŋun dayɨk do aŋek yaŋ dabo abeŋ. Israel amɨn da Mesaia apdɨsak yaŋ nandaŋ teban toŋ. Uŋun Mesaia kɨlɨ apgut yaŋsi nandɨsat. Yaŋ do aŋek dam tebanon egɨsat.”
Yaŋba Pailat da iyɨ yaŋ nandagɨt, “Gen yoko dɨma nandaŋek emat madepsi akdaŋ.” Yaŋ nandaŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep da dabɨlon kɨsitni pakbikon sugaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On amɨn kɨmakban nak da dɨwarɨ dɨma pakeŋ, ji da pani.”
Uŋudon gɨn gen yogokni pɨsaŋakwan gen wasaŋek yaŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsigɨt.
Uŋun amɨn Piŋkop da dɨma yabekban apgut tam, yo kɨnda arɨpmɨ dɨma aban.”
Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak aŋpak tagɨ do nido nayɨsal? Amɨn Kaloŋɨ gɨn uŋun tagɨsi. Gak Piŋkop dakon gen teban guramɨgek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨnikon tagɨ kɨki.”
Kɨŋek Silisia ae Pampilia Provins bamot yapmaŋek tap binap mandaŋek kokup pap Maira uŋudon kɨŋ altagɨmaŋ. Maira uŋun Lisia Provinskon tosok.
Yaŋban Yesu da kɨsitni amɨn uŋun kwenikon wɨtjɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Kɨlek toki do nandɨsat, do pasɨl gamni!” Yaŋ yaŋban uŋudon gɨn wuda tebani pasɨl ɨmɨŋakwa kɨlek tagɨt.
Yaŋban uŋun gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, tagɨsi yosol. Uŋun asisi, Piŋkop uŋun kaloŋ dagɨn egɨsak, ae Piŋkop kɨnda dɨma egɨsak.
Yesu da gen saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Abɨsok butno jɨk tosok. Ni gen naŋ yokeŋ? ‘Dat yo jɨgɨ nagon apdɨsak gwayeki’ yaŋ yokeŋ? Dɨma. Yo jɨgɨ nagon apdɨsak uŋun pak do apgum.
Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madepsi yopmaŋek yutnon wɨgakwan paŋdetni da Yesukon kɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Joŋ pigaga kwoŋ dakon tɨlak gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ yaŋbɨ nandano.”
Aŋakwan uŋudon gɨn Parisi amɨn kɨŋek Erot dakon amɨn kabɨ uŋun gat muwugek “Niaŋ aŋek aŋatneŋ?” yaŋ do gen paŋkosit awit.
Kɨla amɨn kɨnda bo Parisi amɨn kɨnda da uŋun amɨn dɨmasi nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgut.
Pakbi ɨdapmon bamaŋ bamaŋ apban kaŋek paŋdetni si pasalgwit. Aŋek “Koŋ kɨnda abɨsak!” yaŋ yaŋek yaŋ tɨdawit.
Amɨn morap Jerusalem egɨpgwit uŋun dakon gen nandaŋek uŋun mɨktɨm tɨm mani Yawi Mɨktɨm yaŋ yawit. Iyɨ da genon da Akeldama yaŋ yawit.
Iyɨŋba Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen uŋun bamɨ yoŋ. Elaija da abɨŋ yo morap paŋkaluk akdɨsak.
Yesu gat paŋdetni kapbɨ gat ɨleŋon da pɨŋ mɨŋat amɨn morapmɨ muwukgwit kabɨkon kɨŋakwa amɨn kɨnda da abɨŋ Yesu da buron gawagek yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Yaŋ aŋek Yesu yut kɨndakon wɨgakwan paŋdetni da iyɨ gɨn egek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nido koŋ uŋun nin da yol do aŋtɨdok amaŋ?”
Judas Yesu uwal da kɨsiron yɨpgut amɨn kaŋban Yesu kɨmotjak do yaŋ dagok aŋakwa mabisi at yaŋ nandagɨt. Aŋek nandak nandakni kulabɨk aŋek silwa moneŋ 30 yaŋ tɨmɨkgɨt uŋun mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat ae kɨla amɨn gat do aeni paŋtobɨl yomgut.
Uŋudon pakgɨmaŋ da wɨsa dagokdo uŋun kokup pap yɨpmaŋek Sisaria kokup papmon kɨŋ altaŋek Pilip da yutnon kɨno uŋun gat egɨpgumaŋ. Pilip uŋun yabekbi kabɨ paŋpulugoni do kalɨp amɨn 7 kabɨ manjɨkbi uŋun kabɨkon nani kɨnda. Uŋun amɨn Gen Bin Tagɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋok amɨn kɨnda.
Ji tuŋon amɨn emarɨ toŋ yombem. Gen tagɨsi niaŋsi aŋek yoni? Yo ni da butjigwan toŋ uŋun gen yogokjikon paŋalon aŋ.
Mɨktɨm saut tetgɨn dakon kɨla amɨn mɨŋat madep uŋun Solomon dakon nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi iyɨŋakwan nandak do mɨktɨm dubagɨsikon da apgut. Mani amɨn kɨnda oni egɨsak, uŋun da Solomon yapmaŋdak, mani geni dɨma nandaŋ. Do gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon uŋun kɨla amɨn mɨŋat madep da pɨdaŋ agek abɨsok ekwaŋ amɨn kabɨ dakon aŋpak yokwi uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋokdɨsak.”
Notno kɨnda kosit dubagɨkon da abɨk da yutnokon ɨsal yɨkdak. Japno mɨni.’
Bo kɨla amɨn madep kɨnda da uwalni gat emat wam do nandɨsak kaŋ, mibɨltok nandaŋ kokwin asak. Iyɨ dakon emat amɨn 10 tausen da uwalni dakon 20 tausen tagɨ yolni bo dɨma, yaŋ do nandak nandak asak.
Yaŋ yaŋban binap gen kɨnda paŋmuwukbi kabɨkon kɨŋ ɨreŋ tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ: “Uŋun paŋdet dɨma kɨmotdɨsak.” Mani Yesu da paŋdet uŋun dɨma kɨmotjak yaŋ dɨma yagɨt. “Egakwan gɨn nak aeno tobɨl apbeŋ do nandakeŋ bo dɨma, uŋun nak dakon yo”, uŋun gɨn yagɨt.
Nak pakbisi baŋ telagɨ pakbi soŋ damɨsat, mani uŋun da Telagɨ Wup soŋ damdɨsak.”
Yerɨ dɨwarɨ da mɨktɨm tɨpmɨ toŋ tɨmon mawit. Uŋun kwenjok tawit, do tepmɨ kwawit, mani tɨp kwenon mɨktɨm morapmɨ dɨma, do gelɨ tagɨ dɨma yopba kɨwit. Do gɨldat da wɨŋ pɨndakban alek tawit.
Mani amɨn morap not aŋ ɨmɨŋek mani nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn, uŋun amɨn Piŋkop dakon monjɨ gwayonisi ani do yagɨt.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋakwa Pol gat Banabas gat da nandabal yokwi taŋban uŋun amɨn gat gen emat madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋakwa paŋmuwukbi da amɨn bamot gat ae nandaŋ gadat amɨn dɨ gat manjɨŋ yopba Jerusalem kɨwit. Kwa yabekbi gat paŋmuwukbi dakon kɨla amɨn gat gen uŋun aŋmɨlɨp ani yaŋ do yabekgwit.
Jap arɨpninon naŋek tap wakga tagap tosak yaŋ do wit maba tap kagagwan pɨgɨwit.
Aŋakwan uŋudon gɨn koŋni toŋ amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Mani muwut muwut yut dakon kɨla amɨn da Sabat bɨsapmon Yesu da amɨn aŋmɨlɨp agɨt uŋun do butjap nandagɨt. Butjap nandaŋek mɨŋat amɨnyo yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Pi agak dakon gɨldat 6 kabɨ toŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon sot amɨn apba tagɨ paŋmɨlɨp ani. Mani Sabat bɨsapmon dɨmasi ani.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn kɨlegɨ kabɨ Datni da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan gɨldat da teŋteŋosok uŋudeŋ teŋteŋaŋek egɨpdaŋ. Nak da gen yosot pakyaŋsi nandani.”
Ae don mɨŋat uŋun kɨsi kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Gak namɨn? Gak da gen kobogɨ niyɨŋbɨ kɨŋ amɨn yabekba abɨmaŋ yoyɨno. Gak gaga do namɨn yaŋ yosol?”
Kɨŋek Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak dakon bɨsap uŋun kwaŋ tosok uŋun dakon gen yaŋ teŋteŋoni.
“Yaŋ iyɨŋban amɨn tagɨ da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Gak pi monjɨno gen guramɨt tagɨsi agɨl. Aŋek pigo dakon kɨla tagɨsi agɨl. Yo monɨŋɨsok gabo kɨla tagɨsi agɨl do yo madep gabo kɨla tagɨ aki. Gak apbɨ kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ando.’
Yaŋban Pita da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Uwal da gɨkba kɨmagaki nakyo kɨsi nɨkba kɨmokgeŋ do ani kaŋ, gak do wasɨp dɨma yokeŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdet kabɨ dɨwarɨ kɨsi yaŋ gɨn yawit.
abɨŋ altaŋek paŋmuwukbi yaŋ yobal apba Piŋkop da paŋpulugaŋakwan yo morap agɨmal uŋun dakon geni yoyɨŋek yaŋ yagɨmal, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ nandaŋ gadat dakon kosit wɨtdal yoban nandaŋ gadat awit.”
Yaŋ dagok aŋek Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ. Yɨpba uŋun da toptopmon da man madep ɨmɨŋek, baljaŋek tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Kɨmagek gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan Piŋkop da kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdokdɨsak.”
Aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: ‘Nak dakon yut uŋun amɨn da abɨŋ bɨsit aŋnamni do tosok.’ Mani ji da kulabɨk aba ‘kabo noknok dakon pasɨlɨ tamo yombem asak.’ ”
Yesu Sonda wɨsa dagokdo kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek mibɨltok Maria Makdala kokupmon nani altaŋ ɨmgut. (Uŋun mɨŋat Yesu da kalɨp koŋ 7 kabɨ burɨgwan egɨpgwit baŋ yol ɨmgut.)
Pɨndagek uŋudon gɨn yaŋ yoban nandaŋek datni Sebedi gat pi amɨni gat boron si yɨgakwa Yesu yolgɨmal.
Amɨn Dakon Monji niaŋon da kɨmotdɨsak do yaŋbi uŋun da tɨlak kɨmotdɨsak. Mani uwal da kɨsiron yɨpjak amɨn, awa!”
Yɨgek mibɨltok kɨsirɨ dɨma sugaŋek jap naŋban Parisi amɨn uŋun da kaŋek dɨma agagɨ asak yaŋ nandagɨt.
Amɨn kɨnda iyɨ dakon gen yosok, uŋun amɨn iyɨ man madep pak do yosok. Mani amɨn kɨnda yabet amɨni man madep pasak do nandɨsak uŋun amɨn topni mɨni, amɨn kɨlegɨsi.
Nak gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan ji gat egek amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgɨm. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak abɨdok do dɨma nandawit? Mani Piŋkop da papiakon nak do gen mandabi uŋun da arɨpmon noman tosak.”
Ae Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Mɨŋat kɨnda da silwa moneŋ tabɨlɨ 10 kabɨ baŋ kaloŋɨ da yutnon maŋ pasɨljak kaŋ uŋun niaŋ asak? Uŋun da lamni koleŋek yutni ɨkdɨgaŋek tebaisi wɨsɨŋek don kosak.
Aŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji da egɨ yo yokwi morapmɨ noman taŋ ɨba tepmɨ pakdɨsak. Ae Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn, ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn uŋun da manji ɨmɨŋek aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Aŋakwa gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan pɨdokdɨsak.”
Piŋkop uŋun amɨn kɨnda da dɨmasi kagɨt. Mani Monjɨsi kaloŋɨ, Datni da kapmatjok egɨsak, uŋun da Piŋkop dakon mibɨlɨ kɨlɨ nolɨgɨt.
Yesu da amɨn uŋun yaŋ ɨban kɨgɨt uŋun yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak jap noknok kɨnda asal kaŋ, notgo, bo ae pego padɨk padɨkgo bo ae yawi dɨwatgo bo ae yoni morapmɨ amɨn dɨbaŋ dɨma yaŋ yobi. Uŋun da kobogɨ do don yaŋ gamdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda Jerusalem yɨpmaŋek Jeriko kokup papmon kɨk do aŋek kosiron pɨgɨgɨt. Pɨgakwan kabo noknok da abɨdaŋ yɨk ɨmalni gwayeŋek aŋakba palɨ kɨmakban yɨpmaŋ kɨwit.
yaŋ yagɨt, “Nin abɨsok Jerusalem kɨŋapno amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn uŋun da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ. Yaŋ aŋek gen pikon yɨpmaŋek kɨmotjak do yaŋ dagok akdaŋ. Yaŋ dagok aŋek Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ.
Tepmɨ abɨŋ dandaban dɨpmɨn potni kaŋ, uŋun tagɨ dɨma.
Gen uŋun nandaŋ mudaŋek Yesu mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋ kɨsak do tebai iyɨwit.
“Not kabɨ, ji nidosi uŋun akdaŋ? Nit amɨn ji yombem gɨn. Nit ji do Gen Bin Tagɨsi dayamak. Ji da kokup kɨdat uŋun yopmaŋek Piŋkop egɨp egɨpmɨ toŋ egɨsak uŋudon gɨn tobɨlni do dayamak. Uŋun Piŋkop da mɨktɨm, kundu ae tap wasaŋek yo morapni kɨsi wasaŋ yopgut.
Pol da yut uŋun egɨpgut uŋun si yumaŋ naŋ naŋ aŋek bɨlak bamorɨ egɨpgut. Egakwan amɨn da yutnikon abɨŋ abɨŋ aŋakwa nandaban tagɨsi agɨt.
Yo yaŋ altaŋakwa yabekbi kabɨ Jerusalem egɨpgwit amɨn da Piŋkop dakon gen Samaria amɨn da kɨlɨ abɨdawit uŋun dakon gen bini nandawit. Nandaŋek Pita gat Jon gat uŋudon kɨnjil do yabekgwit.
“Uŋun pakbi kɨbaŋɨ toŋ tagɨsi amɨnon moneŋ 300 danari da arɨp tɨmɨgek yoni mɨni amɨn do yomnom tam uŋun tagɨsi.”
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen uŋun nandayɨŋ uŋun naga do aŋek dɨma, ji do aŋek altak.
“Yesu kalugɨ egakwan kat.” Yaŋ yaŋban gen uŋun do nandaba bamɨ dɨma agɨt.
Dewit Telagɨ Wup da aŋpulugaŋban iyɨ yaŋ yagɨt: ‘Piŋkop da nak dakon Amɨn Tagɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak abɨŋ nak da amɨnsi tet do yɨkbɨ don uwalgo kandap gɨbaŋgogwan yopbo gengo guramɨtni.” ’
Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon yoma wɨtdal gabeŋ. Gen mɨktɨmon yaŋ aŋteban abi, Kwen Kokupmon Piŋkop da yaŋ gɨn yaŋ aŋteban asak. Ae gen mɨktɨmon yaŋ wɨtdalbi, Kwen Kokup-mon Piŋkop da yaŋ gɨn yaŋ wɨtdaljak.”
Wɨgakwan yo jɨgɨ altaŋ nimdaŋ uŋun dɨma nandawit. Butni dɨma pɨsaŋakwa kulup madep da altaŋek wutjɨŋban pasɨlgwit. Amɨn yaŋ gɨn egakwa Amɨn Dakon Monji apdɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋek yoyɨŋba yutnon wɨŋbal Yesu da manon gen dɨma yonjil ae amɨn dɨma yoyɨŋdetjil do yaŋsop tebaisi aŋ yomgwit.
Yaŋbal yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil kɨŋ kokup papmon pɨgakwal amɨn kɨnda pakbi kwoba kɨnda guramɨk apban jil gat domdom akdaŋ. Uŋun amɨn da yut wɨgɨsagon jil uŋudon yol aŋaŋ wɨgɨnjil.
Bo amɨn da ‘Oni obɨk’, bo ae ‘Asoni obɨk’ yaŋ dɨma yokdaŋ. Nandani, Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni uŋun jikon kɨlɨ abɨk.”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae Parisi amɨn, ji jamba but amɨnsi. Awa! Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan pɨgɨk do aŋ amɨn ji da kosit sopmaŋ yomaŋ. Yaŋ aŋek dɨsiyo kɨsi uŋungwan dɨma pɨkwaŋ.
Nao uŋun Seruk dakon monji. Seruk uŋun Reu dakon monji. Reu uŋun Pelek dakon monji. Pelek uŋun Ebe dakon monji. Ebe uŋun Sela dakon monji.
Aŋakwal Simeon da gɨsam yomɨŋek Monjɨ dakon meŋi Maria yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nandaki, Israel amɨn morapmɨ da on Monjɨ do aŋek maŋ potdaŋ, ae morapmɨ da pɨdokdaŋ. But tobɨl ani do Piŋkop da yabekgɨt, mani yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmdaŋ.
“Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae Parisi amɨn ji jamba but amɨnsi. Awa! Ji kombɨ amɨn ae amɨn kɨlegɨ kalɨpsi egɨ kɨmakba yopgwit tamo paŋtɨlɨm aŋ.
Yaŋ aŋakwa yabekbi bamot Banabas gat Pol gat paret aŋ yom do aŋ dakon geni nandaŋ wurɨpdak ɨmalni pɨdaŋek mɨŋat amɨn morap kabɨkon pɨgɨ yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨmal,
Yaŋ egek Jekop jap Isip toŋ yaŋ nandaŋek babɨknin yabekban Isip mɨktɨmon kɨwit.
Yo morap uŋun altaŋ mudaŋakwa Pol Jerusalem kɨk do aŋek mɨktɨm bamot Masadonia ae Akaia baŋ kɨk do nandagɨt. Nandaŋek yagɨt, “Nak Jerusalem kɨŋek don Rom kokup papmon kɨkdosi nandɨsat.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Uŋun nak mani. Ji don kaŋakwa Amɨn Dakon Monji Tapmɨm Ami da amɨnsi tet do yɨkban kokdaŋ. Aŋek kaŋakwa Kwen Kokup dakon gɨkwemon da apban kokdaŋ.”
Yaŋakwan amɨn Pol baljok do awit pasalek dɨma baljawit. Aŋakwa mibɨltok amɨn da Pol Rom amɨn kɨnda naŋ yoyɨko nap teban naŋ aŋteban ayɨŋ yaŋ kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋek uŋun kɨsi pasol pasol agɨt.
Nin abɨsok yaŋsi nandamaŋ, gak yo morap kɨlɨ nandaŋ mudosol, ae amɨn da dɨma gayɨŋakwa gaga tagɨ yoki. Uŋun do aŋek gak Piŋkopmon da apgul yaŋsi nandano bamɨ asak.”
Ae ni bɨsapmon sot asal yaŋ gandaŋek kɨlago agɨmaŋ, ae ni bɨsapmon dam teban yutnon yɨkdal yaŋ gandaŋek abɨŋ gandagɨmaŋ?’
Yaŋ dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda mɨŋatni yumabi dɨma aŋakwan kwɨnɨgek mɨŋat kaluk pasak kaŋ, uŋun wɨli iyɨ yumabi asak.”
Andru Yesu yɨpmaŋek uŋudon gɨn Saimon wɨsɨŋ kaŋ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nin Mesaia kɨlɨ kamaŋ.” (“Mesaia” dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun “Kristo”).
Paŋdet 72 uŋun kɨsɨk kɨsɨgon da tobɨl abɨŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak dakon man yaŋapno koŋ da genin guramɨkgaŋ!”
Yaŋban nandaŋek Ananias pɨlɨgɨ maŋ kɨmakgɨt. Kɨmakban uŋun dakon gen bini nandawit amɨn morap uŋun madepsi pasalgwit.
Yesu bɨlakni 12 aŋakwan Yapyap Bɨlak dakon aŋpak yolek Jerusalem kɨwit.
Aŋobɨŋakwa gen yaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn da pɨdaŋ agek yo yokwisi kɨnda agɨt do bo yaŋ ɨmdaŋ yaŋ nandagɨm. Mani dɨma.
ae Jems dakon monji Judas, ae Judas Iskariot (uŋun da don Yesu uwal da kɨsiron yɨpgut).
Mani kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil nido nak wusɨk do pi amal? Nak Datno da yutnon egɨpmɨsi egɨsat jil uŋun dɨma nandamal?”
Akban kaŋek Sekaraia wurɨpdagek pasalgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn morap joŋ tɨmon yɨtni do yoyɨgɨt. Aŋek bret kɨsit kɨnda ae tap kɨlap bamot pabɨdaŋek Kwen Kokup sɨŋtaŋek gɨsamɨkgɨt. Yaŋ aŋek bret jokgalek paŋdetni do yoban uŋun da amɨn do yomgwit.
Yaŋban Yesu da yagɨt, “Yoyɨŋba mɨŋat amɨnyo pabɨŋ yɨtni.” Uŋun tɨmon joŋ tɨm madep tagɨt. Wɨli 5 tausen yaŋ da tɨlak pabɨŋ yɨkgwit.
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Yesu Nasaret amɨn da obɨgɨsak.”
Dabɨlgo amɨn tet da yokwikon gepban kaŋ, pɨlɨk mabɨ kɨsak. Gɨptɨm dɨwatgo kɨnda pasɨljak kaŋ, uŋun da yo madep dɨma asak. Mani gɨptɨmgo kɨsi kaloŋ maba Tɨpdomon pɨgɨsak kaŋ, uŋun da jɨgɨsi.
Yesu da nandak nandakni da arɨpmon Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋek tɨlak gen uŋuden morapmɨ yoyɨgɨt.
“Mani kɨla amɨn da monji kaŋek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, ‘Amɨn on da egɨ don datni dakon yo morap tɨmɨtdɨsak, do aŋatno kɨmagakwan wain pini nin do aŋawatneŋ.’
Yesu gen yaŋ yaŋakwan uŋudon gɨn paŋdetni da tobɨl abɨŋ kaŋba Yesu mɨŋat kɨnda gat gen yaŋbal pɨndagek wɨrɨpdakgwit. Mani “Gak yo nido galak tosol?” bo “Nido on mɨŋat gat gen yomal?” yaŋ kɨnda da Yesu dɨma iyɨwit.
Gɨldat kabi dɨ egɨ mudaŋakwa Peliks gat mɨŋatni Drusila gat apgumal. Drusila uŋun Juda mɨŋat kɨnda. Peliks da Pol yaŋ ɨban obɨŋ Yesu Kristo nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmɨm dakon mibɨlɨ do iyɨŋakwan nandagɨt.
Asisi, kombɨ amɨn Elaija da bɨsapmon sɨkak dɨma maŋakwan bɨlak kapbɨ ae kanek 6 yaŋ egek jap do madepsi awit. Uŋun bɨsapmon Israel mɨktɨmon sakwabat morapmɨ egɨpgwit.
“Yaŋ pɨndagapbo amɨn kapbɨ Sisaria kokupmon da nak do yabekgwit uŋun amɨn nin da yut egɨpgumaŋ yomakon uŋudon paŋabɨŋ akgwit.
Yesu tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakgwit da kapmatjok pi kɨnda tagɨt. Uŋun pigagagwan kɨmakbi tamo kalugɨ kɨnda tagɨt. Uŋun tamokon bumjot kɨnda dɨma yɨpbi.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban Juda amɨn dɨwarɨ da Pol gat Sailas gat dakon gen nandaŋek nandaŋ gadat aŋek amɨn bamoron saŋbewit. Aŋakwa Grik amɨn morapmɨ Piŋkop gawak ɨmgwit amɨn ae kɨla amɨn mɨŋat morapmɨ kɨsi amɨn bamot yolgwit.
Yesu gen yaŋ iyɨŋakwan, muwut muwut yutni dakon kɨla amɨn Jairus da yutnon da amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ Jairus yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gwago kɨlɨ kuŋwak, uŋun do nido yoyɨŋdet ɨsal dogɨn jɨgɨ ɨmɨsal?”
Kosit niaŋon da nin dakon gen kaloŋ kaloŋ yoŋ?
Nak Dat dakon pi dɨma asat kaŋ, geno do nandaba bamɨ dɨma asak.
“Not kabɨ, Abraham dakon babɨni kabɨ, ae Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ Piŋkop gawak ɨmaŋ amɨn, nandani. Piŋkop da amɨn yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨtjak uŋun dakon but pɨso geni uŋun nin do yɨpban apgut.
“Yaŋ yaŋban gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨni, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ ni bɨsapmon gandano jap do agɨl, bo pakbi do agɨl, bo kokup ŋwakŋwarɨkon da apgul, bo ɨmalgo mɨni, bo sot agɨl, bo dam teban yutnon yɨkgɨl, abɨ dɨma aŋpulugagɨmaŋ?’
Uŋun bɨsapmon emat wuwɨk gat ae dubagɨkon emat aŋ uŋun dakon gen bin apba nandaŋek butji dɨma pasolni. Uŋun yo morap altokdaŋ, mani mɨktɨm da mudosak bɨsap madep kɨlɨ uŋun yaŋ dɨma nandani.
Ae amɨn morap da yo kabɨgo yobi do gayɨŋba kaŋ yobi. Ae amɨn kɨnda da yogo kɨnda abɨdaŋ aŋkɨsak kaŋ, aŋtobɨl gamjak do tebai dɨma iyɨki.
Mani gak bɨsit ak do nandɨsal kaŋ, yutgokon wɨgɨ yoma sopmaŋek Datgo pasɨlɨ egɨsak uŋun bɨsit iyɨki. Yaŋ aŋaki Datgo yo pasɨlɨ pɨndakdak uŋun da kobogɨ tagɨsi gamdɨsak.
Aŋkewalno suŋ kɨnda yaŋakwan gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋon da iyɨwit.
Jon da ɨlɨkba pɨgɨk paŋ egɨpgut uŋun bɨt madep kɨnda mani kamel uŋun dakon daŋgwani baŋ wasaŋbi. Aŋek bɨt gɨp kɨnda bobaŋ napmɨ do wamgut. Japni uŋun pɨlak pɨlak ae kabaŋ kok.
Yaŋban Yesu da monjɨ bamot yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil gen uŋun yomal dɨma nandaŋ pɨsaŋek yomal. Nak da tepmɨ madep pakdɨsat uŋun tagɨ panjil?” Yaŋban iyɨgɨmal, “Tagɨ pandeŋ.”
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Asisi dayɨsat, ji Amɨn Dakon Monji dakon sabam ae yawiyo dɨma noni kaŋ, jikon egɨp egɨp dɨma taŋ damjak.
Kɨla amɨn kɨnda da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet tagɨsi, nak niaŋsi aŋek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokeŋ?”
Piŋkop da Telagɨ Wupni dam do kɨlɨ yaŋ teban tok agɨt. Ji ae mɨŋat monjɨyosi ae amɨn dubagɨkon ekwaŋ, ae amɨn kɨsi morap Piŋkop da yaŋ yomɨsak uŋun Telagɨ Wupni damjak.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak Datnokon dɨma wɨgɨt, do nak dɨma abɨdoki. Kɨŋ notno kabɨ yaŋ yoyɨki, ‘Nak Datno ae ji dakon Datji uŋudon wɨgɨkeŋ. Piŋkopno ae ji dakon Piŋkopji uŋudon wɨgɨkeŋ.’ ”
“Nak naga sipsip dakon kɨla amɨn tagɨsi. Datno da nak nandaŋ namɨŋakwan nak da Datno nandaŋ ɨmɨsat. Uŋudeŋ gɨn sipsipno da nak nandaŋ namɨŋakwa nak da sipsipno nandaŋ yomɨsat. Aŋek sipsipno do aŋek naga dakon egɨp egɨpno parekdat.
Judas kwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat, ae Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon obip amɨn uŋun dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat gen yawit. Niaŋon da Yesu kɨsitnikon yɨpjak yaŋ do yaŋ nandat awit.
Yaŋ yaŋek emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak kɨŋ yo altoni do nandaŋ teban tal uŋun yaŋ gɨn noman taŋ ɨmeŋ kokdɨsal.” Gen uŋun iyɨgɨt uŋun bɨsapmonsi oman monjɨni kɨlek tagɨt.
Amɨn da aŋpak niaŋsi aŋdamni do nandaŋ, uŋun aŋpak amɨn do aŋyomni.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda da ‘Kristo oni!’ bo ‘Asoni!’ yaŋ yaŋban kaŋ, geni dɨma nandaŋ gadani.
Yesu da Mata gat padɨge gat ae Lasarus gat do but dasi galak taŋ yomgut.
Ji uŋun amɨn da aŋ uŋudeŋ dɨma ani, nido Datji dɨma iyɨŋakwa yo morap do wadak wadak aŋ uŋun nandaŋ mudosok.
“Jikon da amɨn kɨnda sipsipni 100 baŋ kaloŋɨ da pasɨljak kaŋ niaŋ asak? Uŋun da sipsip 99 joŋ tɨmon yopban egakwa kaloŋɨ pasɨldak uŋun wɨsɨŋek don aŋalon asak.
Nandani, amɨn dɨwarɨ abɨsok buŋon ekwaŋ, uŋun don mibɨltok amɨn akdaŋ. Ae amɨn dɨwarɨ abɨsok mibɨltok ekwaŋ, uŋun don buŋon amɨn akdaŋ.”
Uŋun amɨn tomni tɨmɨt dogɨn nandɨsak do yaŋ asak. Sipsip tagɨ egɨpni do dɨma nandɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋban Pilip da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak da Dat nolɨŋbɨ nin dakon but mudaŋban.”
pɨlɨn tukgwan ekwaŋ amɨn da teŋteŋɨ kokdaŋ. Uŋun da kosit nolɨŋban kaŋek but yawot dakon kositnaŋ kɨneŋ.”
Pestus da abɨŋ gapman dakon tamo madep abɨdaŋ yɨgek wasaŋek Judia mɨktɨm kɨla agɨt. Aŋek gɨldat kapbɨ egɨ mudaŋek Sisaria kokup pap yɨpmaŋek Jerusalem wɨgɨgɨt.
Yaŋban iyɨgɨmal, “Tagɨ pandeŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋbal Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Uŋun asi, tepmɨ pakdɨsat uŋun pakdamal.
Uŋun bɨsapmon ji butji tagɨsi taŋakwan kɨsɨk kɨsɨk aŋek wɨgɨ mok ani. Nandani. Kobogɨ do tomni wukwisi Kwen Kokupmon taŋ damɨsak. Kalɨp babɨni da kombɨ amɨn do yo yokwi yaŋ gɨn aŋyomgwit.
Peliks uŋun Pol da moneŋ dɨ ɨban dam tebanon naŋ pulugaŋ yɨpban kɨsak uŋun do kɨsi nandagɨt. Yaŋ nandagɨt do bɨsap morapmɨ Pol yaŋ ɨban opban gen yagɨmal.
Pita gat notni bamot gat dɨpmɨn do yokwisi awit. Mani dɨpmɨnon da pɨdaŋ Yesu tɨlɨmni gat ae amɨn bamot gat kɨsi akba pɨndakgwit.
Jap noknok bɨsap aŋakwan Yesu jap noknok tamokon yabekbi kabɨni gat kɨsi yɨkgwit.
Yesu uŋun gen morap yaŋ mudaŋek paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ da kɨŋ Yesu suŋ kɨnda yaŋban nandaŋek gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋ do gen paŋkosit awit.
Publius dakon datni uŋun sot aŋek gɨptɨmɨ kɨndapmɨ soŋakwan pakgɨt. Ae kok ɨlɨtyo kɨsi agɨt, do Pol uŋun kok do wɨgek bɨsit aŋ ɨmɨŋ mudaŋek kɨsitni kwenikon wutjɨŋek aŋmɨlɨp agɨt.
“Abɨgɨ nepba amɨn kɨnda mani Ananias nak nandak do apgut. Uŋun amɨn Piŋkop gawak ɨmɨŋek gen teban guramɨk kɨmakgɨt. Juda amɨn morap Damaskus egɨpgwit da nandaba amɨn kɨlegɨsi kɨnda agɨt.
Yesu ɨleŋon da pɨŋ kɨŋakwan mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyo morapmɨ da yolgwit.
Yaŋba Yesu da amɨn monɨŋ kɨnda iyɨŋban opban paŋdetni da bɨkbɨgon yɨpban agakwan
Ji yokwi pakpak amɨn, mani monjɨsi do yo tagɨ yomaŋ. Do yaŋsi nandani. Ji bɨsit iyɨŋba Datji Kwen Kokup egɨsak uŋun da Telagɨ Wup tagɨ damjak.”
Aeni kɨŋ bɨsit aŋ tobɨl abɨŋ paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji dɨpmɨn sigɨn pagek tapmɨm paŋ, ma? Dɨpmɨn arɨpmɨ kwayɨŋ. Bɨsap kɨlɨ abɨk. Amɨn Dakon Monji yokwi pakpak da kɨsiron kɨlɨ uŋun yɨpmaŋgaŋ.
Dat da amɨn kɨnda dakon aŋpakni dɨma kokwinɨkdak. Amɨn da Dat do man madep ɨmaŋ, yaŋ gɨn Monjɨ do man madep ɨmni do aŋek amɨn kokwin agak pi kɨsi morap uŋun Monji do ɨmɨŋ mudagɨt. Amɨn kɨnda Monji man madep dɨma ɨmɨsak kaŋ, Dat Monji yabekban pɨgɨt uŋunyo kɨsi man madep dɨma ɨmɨsak.
Bɨsap morapmɨ Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut tawiron agek uŋun amɨn Yesu manji ɨmni do pi madepsi agɨm. Nak butjap madepsi nandaŋ yomɨŋek yo yokwisi aŋ yobeŋ do kokup pap dubagɨkon kɨsi yol paŋkɨgɨm.
Mani Pita gat Jon gat da gen yaŋ paŋtobɨl yomgumal, “Dɨsi kokwinɨtni. Piŋkop dakon gen yɨpmaŋek ji dakon gen guramɨtdeŋ kaŋ, Piŋkop da nandaban kɨlek tosak bo niaŋ?
Yaŋ kaŋek kɨsitni kɨsirɨkon wutjɨŋban sotni yɨpmaŋ dekgɨt. Yaŋ aban pɨdaŋek Yesu do jap paŋnoman agɨt.
Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da kabap yaŋ yoyɨkdaŋ, ‘Ji tuwɨl kɨ maŋ nin wɨtjɨŋba pasɨlneŋ!’
‘Amɨn Tagɨno’ yaŋ yaŋ namaŋ amɨn uŋun kɨsisi Piŋkop da Kwen Kokup Kɨla Asagon dɨma wɨgɨkdaŋ. Datno Kwen Kokup egɨsak uŋun dakon gen guramɨkgaŋ amɨn uŋun dagɨn wɨgɨkdaŋ.
Aŋek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gen on yaŋ gamaŋ uŋun asi yoŋ bo top?”
Bulmakau yutnon yɨgakwa Betlehem kokup da kapmatjok sipsip kɨla amɨn dɨwarɨ da pɨlɨn kaga sipsip kɨla aŋek joŋ tɨmon egɨpgwit.
“Nak yaŋ dayɨt, ji nak kɨlɨ nandawit mani sigɨn dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ namaŋ.
Aban Amɨn Tagɨ da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Parisi amɨn ji kap ɨdapyo dakon manji baŋgɨn sugoŋ. Mani kabo gat ae aŋpak yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ gat uŋun butjigwan tugawit da toŋ.
Uŋun do nak yaŋ dayɨsat, Piŋkop da iyɨ Amɨn Kɨla Asak jikon tosok uŋun ji da kɨsiron naŋ gwayeŋ amɨn kabi kɨnda bamɨ tagɨ paŋalon agagɨ uŋun da kɨsiron yɨpdɨsak.
Piŋkop da yo morap agɨt uŋun nin da pɨndakgɨmaŋ. Nin uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋok amaŋ. Ae Telagɨ Wup uŋun kɨsi uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋok asak. Piŋkop da amɨn morap iyɨ dakon gen guramɨkgaŋ amɨn uŋun Telagɨ Wup yomɨsak.”
Uŋun bɨlak dakon bɨsap madep mudaŋakwan meŋi datniyo tobɨl kokupnikon kɨk do kɨgɨmal. Mani Yesu Jerusalem sigɨn egɨpgut. Egakwan meŋi datniyo Yesu sigɨn egɨsak yaŋ dɨma nandagɨmal.
Yaŋ do aŋek bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ Piŋkop da dabɨlon ae amɨn da dabɨlon butnokon gulusuŋno mɨni egɨpbeŋ do kɨlani tebaisi asat.
Nak da gen yosot uŋun do but morap dɨma ani. Bɨsap kɨnda apdɨsak, uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn morap kɨmakbi kokupmon pokgoŋ uŋun Monjɨ dakon gen nandaŋek
Pɨgɨ uŋun kalbi Pol da burɨ pɨsaŋakwan dɨpmɨn yombem kɨnda kaŋakwan Masadonia amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak tap pɨdaŋek Masadonia mɨktɨmon obɨŋ nin paŋpulugoki.”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn wudani kɨbɨdaŋakwa gɨptɨmni kɨlek tagɨt.
Amɨn on bɨsapmon ekwaŋ uŋun amɨn yokwisi gɨn. Piŋkop dakon pi naŋ asat yaŋ nandak do wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda kok do yoŋ. Mani kɨnda dɨma kokdaŋ. Kombɨ amɨn Jona dakon tɨlak naŋgɨn kokdaŋ.” Yaŋ yoyɨŋek yopmaŋ kɨgɨt.
Gen yaŋ yaŋakwa ji kombɨ amɨn dapdap dakon babɨkni yaŋsi nandaŋ damamaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋek uŋudon gɨn Yesu da amɨn kabɨ madep yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nak do kabo noknok kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋek emat agak sɨba ae kɨndap kɨrɨŋyo tɨmɨgek nak abɨdok do abeŋ, ma? Nak gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan ji gat egek amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgɨm. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak abɨdok do dɨma nandawit.
Stiwen da gen kokwin amɨn kabɨ saŋbeŋek tebaisi yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kwen wɨgɨk amɨn ji amɨn Piŋkop dɨma nandaŋ ɨmaŋ da tɨlagon butji uŋun tebaisi ae mɨrakji da Piŋkop dakon gen dɨma nandabi yombem. Babɨkji da Telagɨ Wup do kurak tawit, jiyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn aŋ.
Aba uŋun akgwit kabɨkon da kɨnda da emat agak sɨbani ɨlɨkgɨt. Ɨlɨgek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon oman monjɨ mɨragɨ mandaŋ dagagɨt.
Yesu da gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madepsi da yoyɨŋdet uŋun agɨt do tamtam yawit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Maria tepmɨ kɨŋek mɨktɨm ɨleŋɨ toŋ tɨmon Judia mɨktɨm dakon kokup pap kɨndakon kɨgɨt.
Kɨŋ pɨndakbal amɨn kabi kɨnda da kandap yokwi kɨnda wamaŋ aŋapgwit. Uŋun amɨn meŋi da yaŋ aŋalagɨt. Gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ amɨn uŋun aŋabɨŋ Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon yoma kaga kɨnda mani Kɨldani Tagɨsi uŋudon yɨpmaŋ yɨpmaŋ awit. Amɨn Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan pɨgakwa uŋun amɨn da moneŋ ɨmni do bɨsit yoyɨgɨt.
Gen uŋun yaŋba nandaŋek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido ‘ninon bret mɨni’ yaŋ yoŋ? Gen dayɨsat uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsosok, ma? Nandak nandak kositji sopgwit?
Abɨsok nak Dat yabekban pɨgɨmon tobɨl wɨgɨkdɨsat. Mani jikon da kɨnda da ‘Gak dukon kɨsal?’ yaŋ dɨma nayaŋ.
Amɨn da butni pɨdaŋban but morap aŋek yaŋ nandawit, “Jon uŋun Kristo bo?”
Piŋkop da yo kɨnda ak do nandɨsak kaŋ, arɨpmɨ dɨmasi aŋtɨdok asak.”
Wɨsa dagokdo Yesu gat paŋdetni gat kosiron kɨwit. Kɨŋek pik kɨndap uŋun kɨlɨ wagɨlsi kɨbɨdagɨt kawit.
Yaŋ yaŋban amɨn madep da yaŋ nandawit: On amɨn bamot amɨn ɨsalɨ, papia yutnon dɨma yɨkbi, mani pasol pasolɨ mɨni gen tapmɨmɨ toŋ yomal. Yaŋ pɨndagek but morap nandaŋek on amɨn kalɨp Yesu gat egɨpgwit yaŋ nandaŋ kokwinɨkgwit.
Kɨndap tagɨ da bamɨ yokwi arɨpmɨ dɨma potni, ae kɨndap yokwi da bamɨ tagɨ arɨpmɨ dɨma potni.
Aŋek amɨn bamot tɨmɨkban yutnikon pawɨgɨ yɨgakwal jap yomgut. Amɨn uŋun gat gwakni gat Piŋkop nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmɨŋek burɨkon da kɨsɨk kɨsɨk madepsi nandawit.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, kokup yomasiyo yokwi taŋek yumsi tokdɨsak. Ji nak dɨma nandaŋek egɨ wɨgɨ ni bɨsapmon nak do ‘Amɨn on Amɨn Tagɨ da manon abɨsak, uŋun Piŋkop da gɨsamɨgakwan abɨsak’ yaŋ nak do yoni uŋun bɨsapmon nandakdaŋ.”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak da mɨktɨmon emat aŋyawot ak do pɨgɨm yaŋ dɨma nandani. Nak emat agak sɨbanaŋ aŋaŋ pɨgɨm.
Amɨn da yubam tam, moneŋ madepsi tɨmɨk yoni mɨni amɨn do yomnom.”
Aŋek amɨn da madepsi abɨŋ yɨpmaŋek gen pikon yɨpmaŋek yaŋ dagok kɨlegɨ dɨma aŋɨmgwit. Mɨktɨmon egɨp egɨpni gwayeŋba yerɨ mɨni agɨt.”
Mani gen yoyɨgɨt dakon mibɨlɨ nandabal dɨma pɨsagɨt.
Mani Piŋkop da aŋpulugaŋakwan egɨ aŋaŋ wɨgɨm da abɨsok egɨsat. Yaŋ agɨt do abɨsok ɨdon agek amɨn ɨsalɨ ae amɨn madep ji do gen on yaŋ teŋteŋosot. Gen on kalɨpsigwan kombɨ amɨn gat ae Moses gat da yo don altoni do yawit uŋun baŋgɨn yosot.
Nak bret do yat yaŋ nandaŋ, ma? Dɨma. Ji Parisi gat ae Sadyusi amɨn gat dakon yisni do pakyaŋsi kaŋ kɨmotni, nak uŋun do dayɨt.”
Yaŋban Pita da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak amɨn tɨlak gen yoyɨl uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ tagɨ niyɨŋbɨ nandaneŋ?”
Yoyɨŋban aŋkɨ kɨsit kandapyoni paŋnɨŋnɨŋ aŋek wamgwit. Aŋakwa Pol da kɨla amɨni kapmatjok akban kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gen kokwin amɨn da nak dakon mibɨlno dɨma kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋakwa nak nɨtdaŋ. Uŋun tagɨ dɨma akdaŋ. Nak Rom amɨn kɨnda. Ji Rom dakon gen teban yapmaŋgaŋ.”
Gen yosol uŋun nandano ŋwakŋwarɨsi asak do mibɨlɨ niyɨŋbɨ nandano.”
do Juda amɨn da kɨlek tagɨt amɨn yaŋ iyɨwit, “Abɨsok uŋun Sabat bɨsap. Gak gen teban yapmaŋek yalɨŋ potgo tɨmɨgek agɨsal.”
Mani abɨsok yaŋ dayɨsat, nin kabɨkon kɨnda dɨma pasɨldɨsak. Tap wakga dagɨn wagɨl tasɨk tokdɨsak, do ji but pasol dɨma ani.
Yaŋ yaŋban Pita aeni geni aŋteban aŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Asisi, nak uŋun amɨn dɨmasi nandaŋ ɨmɨsat!”
Mani Yesu Ɨleŋ Olipmon wɨgɨgɨt.
Uŋun da yaŋ yak, ‘Wɨgapbo ji nak wɨsɨkdaŋ, mani dɨma nandakdaŋ.’ Ae ‘Ji nak da kokup egɨpbeŋ uŋudon arɨpmɨ dɨma wɨgɨkdaŋ’ yaŋ yak. Gen uŋun niaŋon da yak?”
Yaŋ aba Amɨn Tagɨ da tapmɨmni kalugɨ ji do damjak. Aŋek Kristo ji paŋpulugok do aŋek manjɨkbi uŋun damjak. Uŋun mani Yesu.
Abɨŋ aŋalon aŋek iyɨwit, “Amɨn morapmɨsi da gak wɨsaŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Ji sigɨn dɨma nandaba pɨsosok, ma?”
Yaŋ yaŋek Yesu da paŋdetni dɨma yoni do kɨrɨŋɨk yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak Kristo egɨsat uŋun amɨn kɨnda dɨmasi iyɨni.”
Mani amɨn dakon yokwini dɨma yopmaŋ yomni kaŋ, Datji da yokwisi dɨma yopmaŋ damjak.”
Datno dakon galaktok uŋun yaŋ: amɨn morap Monjɨ kaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmni, uŋun kɨsisi egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do amɨn ani do nandɨsak. Ae mibɨ gɨldaron kɨsisi pabo pɨdoni do nandɨsak.”
Kɨŋ Telagɨ Yut Madepmon saŋbek saŋbek egek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiwit.
Yaŋba Yesu da kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji kɨŋ yo morap kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋ uŋun Jon iyɨni.
Liwai uŋun Simeon dakon monji. Simeon uŋun Juda dakon monji. Juda uŋun Josep dakon monji. Josep uŋun Jonam dakon monji. Jonam uŋun Eliakim dakon monji.
Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma iyɨgɨt. Aŋakwan paŋdet kabɨni da obɨŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Mɨŋat on yaŋ tɨdaŋek jɨgɨ nimɨŋek noldak. Uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Iyɨŋbɨ kwan.”
Yaŋ nandagɨl, do moneŋno beŋon yopgul tam uŋun tagɨ. Yaŋ agɨl tam abɨŋ nak da moneŋno gat ae beŋ da dɨwarɨ saŋbesak uŋun gat tagɨ tɨmɨkgom.’
Gen yosot uŋun ji da dɨma nandaba pɨsosok. Nido geno abɨdok do dɨma nandaŋ.
Pita gat amɨn kɨwit uŋun kosiron dɨpmɨn kɨnda pakgwit da wɨsa dagokdo Sisaria kokupmon kɨŋ altawit. Altaŋakwa Konilias uŋun do jomjom aŋek egɨpgut. Ae yawi dɨwatni gat ae notsini gat yaŋ yoban apgwit uŋun gat kɨsi jomjom aŋek egɨpgwit.
Uŋun Grik amɨn da Pilip kɨŋ kawit. (Pilip uŋun Galili provins Betsaida kokupmon nani.) Yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn tagɨ, nin Yesu kok do abamaŋ.”
Muwut muwut yutnikon baŋ ji dolek uŋun gat dɨma muwutni do yaŋsop aŋ damdaŋ. Bɨsap kɨnda apjak, uŋudon amɨn da dɨkba kɨmagakwa uŋun amɨn da nin da Piŋkop do yo tagɨsi aŋ ɨmamaŋ yaŋ nandakdaŋ.
Sabat dakon yo paŋtagap ak bɨsap, Neŋgokon yɨpgut. Sabat bɨsap uŋun kɨlɨ wasok do agɨt.
Mani abɨsok yo uŋun altokdaŋ do kɨlɨ dayɨŋ mudat, do don amɨn da yo uŋun aŋ daba gen on dayɨsat uŋun do nandani.” Yesu da saŋbeŋek yagɨt, “Kalɨp naga gat kɨsi egɨpgumaŋ do aŋek on gen morap dɨma dayɨgɨm.
“Nandak nandakni kulabɨk aŋek yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Datno dakon oman monjɨ morapni uŋun japni arɨpmɨsi taŋ yomaŋakwa ekwaŋ, mani nak ɨdon egek jap do kɨmotdɨsat.
Aŋakwa notni bot kɨndakon agɨpgwit amɨn da abɨŋ paŋpulugoni do kɨsit da tɨlak aŋ yomgwit. Tɨlak aŋ yoba apba tap kɨlap bot bamot kɨsikon yopba tugaŋ jɨk taŋek pakbi kagagwan pɨgɨk do agɨmal.
Amɨn da dandaba ji Amɨn Dakon Monji yolyol amɨn yaŋ dandaŋek nandaba yokwi tok aŋdamdaŋ. Ji uŋun gat gadaŋek dɨma egɨpni do dayɨŋek yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ damɨŋek man yokwisi damdaŋ. Yo morap uŋun altaŋ damdaŋ, mani ji kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ani.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Jerusalem kɨŋ altawit. Kɨŋ altaŋek Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan pɨgɨ pɨndakban amɨn moneŋ ɨlɨt pi awit. Uŋun wasaŋek amɨn yolban waŋga abɨgɨwit. Yaŋ aŋek moneŋ kulabɨk awit amɨn dakon tamo, ae mɨnam baŋ moneŋ ɨlɨt awit amɨn dakon tamo uŋun kɨsi paŋtobɨlban tagal kɨwit.
Mɨŋatjok nandaŋ kokwini tagɨ dɨma uŋun lamni tɨmɨgek lam kolek do pakbi dɨ gat dɨma paŋkɨwit.
Yoyɨŋban but galak nandaŋek moneŋ ɨmni do yaŋ teban tawit. Judas uŋun nandaŋek Yesu kɨsitnikon yɨpjak dakon kosit wɨsɨgɨt.
Pɨdagek Lida kokupmon amɨn ae Saron mɨktɨm amɨn morap da Anias kaŋek but tobɨl aŋek Amɨn Tagɨkon kɨwit.
Yɨk mudaŋba bret kɨsit kɨnda ae tap kɨlap bamot uŋun gat tɨmɨgek Kwen Kokup sɨŋtaŋek gɨsamɨkgɨt. Gɨsamɨgek bret jokgal paŋdetni do yoban uŋun da amɨn do kokwinɨk yomgwit. Ae tap kɨlap yaŋ gɨn kokwinɨk paŋdetni do yoban uŋun da amɨn do yomgwit.
Ji da gen uŋun yoŋ, mani Piŋkop da pi morap agɨt uŋun pɨndagek nandano nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi gɨn asak.”
Moses yo uŋun altaŋban kaŋek but morap agɨt. Yaŋ nandaŋek kapmatjok da pakyaŋsi kok do aŋek kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan Amɨn Tagɨ da yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Yaŋ yaŋek Moses gat ae kombɨ amɨn morap dakon gen gat baŋ wasaŋek Piŋkop da papia morapmon gen iyɨ do mandabi uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ yoyɨŋ teŋteŋagɨt.
Sabat bɨsap mudaŋakwan pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo Maria Makdala kokupmon nani, ae Maria Jems dakon meŋi, ae Salome, uŋun mɨŋat kapbɨ da bɨt nelak, ae yo mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ kɨbaŋɨ tagɨsi, Yesu dakon bumjotni soŋ ɨm do yumaŋ paŋkosit awit.
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ gɨn aba amɨn kɨsi yɨk mudawit.
Mani yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak japno toŋ, uŋun jap dakon mibɨlɨ ji dɨma nandaŋ.”
nin da bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ bɨsit pi ae Piŋkop gen yaŋ teŋteŋok pi gɨn aneŋ.”
Mani amɨn kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek egɨp egɨpmon tagɨ egɨpni do kokwinɨkbi kabɨ uŋun bɨsapmon mɨŋat eyo dɨma akdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban mibɨltok amɨn da monjɨsok uŋun yabegek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak tayaŋgok kɨŋ gen nayɨl uŋun do amɨn kɨnda dɨmasi iyɨki.”
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nido kɨni? Dɨsi jap yomgut.”
Yaŋ yaŋakwan dam teban yut dakon kɨla amɨn teŋteŋɨ kɨnda aŋopni do yagɨt. Aŋopba abɨdaŋ pasol pasol nandaŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek kɨŋ Pol gat Sailas gat da buron gawagek nandaban wukwan yomgut.
“Mani yaŋ dayɨsat, gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon ɨsal dogɨn gen yum yawit amɨn morap Piŋkop da mibɨlɨ nido yawit uŋun do yoyɨŋban kobogɨ iyɨŋ iyɨŋ akdaŋ.
mani nak uŋun gat egɨpgumak, ae uŋun da nak yabekban pɨgɨm, do uŋun nandaŋ ɨmɨsat.”
Obɨŋ Pita kɨndap alɨŋek ekwan kagɨt. Mɨŋat uŋun da pakyaŋsi yɨpban kwan kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Yesu Nasaret kokupmon nani gat kɨsi egɨpgumal.”
“Not kabɨ, nandani. Nak ji gat egek Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak dakon gen dayɨŋ teŋteŋagɨm. Nak abɨsok nandɨsat, ji depmaŋ kɨŋapbo jikon da kɨnda da nak ae buŋon dɨmasi nandakdaŋ.
“Ji kaŋ kɨmagek gen pakyaŋsi nandani. Taŋ yomaŋ amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da dɨ gat saŋbeŋ daban tɨmɨtdaŋ. Mani mɨnini amɨn uŋun taŋ namaŋ yaŋ nandɨsak uŋun Piŋkop da gwayekdɨsak.”
Ae abɨŋ yɨp do aŋek gen yokwi morapmɨ dɨ gat kɨsi iyɨwit.
Uŋun babɨknin 12 kabɨkon da dɨwarɨ da Josep do nandaba yokwi tok aŋek amɨn do yomɨŋek tomni tɨmɨkgwit. Tɨmɨkba uŋun amɨn da Josep oman monjɨ egɨpjak do Isip mɨktɨmon aŋkɨwit. Mani Piŋkop uŋun Josep gat egek
tamoni do Piŋkop da yo madepsi ɨmdɨsak. Mɨktɨmon egɨpjak bɨsapmon yo morap kalɨp yopmaŋ dekgɨt uŋun dakon tɨlak yapmaŋek yo morapmɨ ɨmdɨsak. Uŋun amɨn da yutni, peni padɨk padɨkyo, sami, meŋi, mɨŋat monjɨyo ae mɨktɨm morapmɨsi tɨmɨtdɨsak. Mani uŋun gɨn dɨma, amɨn da yo yokwi aŋyomdaŋ. Yaŋ aŋakwa bɨsap madep apjak bɨsapmon egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokdɨsak.
Aŋakwan don paŋdetni iyɨ gɨn obɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin nido koŋ uŋun yol do aŋtɨdok amaŋ?”
Ji mɨnam pɨndakgaŋ uŋun do nandani. Jap yet dɨma kwaokgaŋ, ae jap paŋmuwut yutnon jap dɨma paŋek paŋmuwuk yopmaŋgaŋ. Mani Datji Kwen Kokup egɨsak uŋun da jap upmokdok. Ji pɨŋbi aŋakwa mɨnam da yo madep yaŋ nandaŋ, ma?
Amɨn dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm tɨpmɨ toŋ tɨm yombem, uŋun amɨn Piŋkop gen nandaŋek but galagon da abɨdoŋ.
Mani Piŋkop dakon Wup da nak aŋpulugaŋban koŋ yoldat kaŋ, Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni jikon kɨlɨ abɨk.
Ae Esia gapman dakon amɨn madep dɨ uŋun Pol dakon notni, uŋunyo kɨsi da Pol muwut muwut yut madepmon dɨmasi kɨsak do gen yɨpba apgut.
Aŋek mɨŋat yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gen yaŋbɨ nandaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmamaŋ. Mani uŋun dogɨn dɨma. Nin da nin iyɨ dakon gen nandaŋek yaŋsi nandamaŋ, uŋun amɨn asi mɨktɨm amɨn morap yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn yaŋ nandamaŋ.”
Amɨn uŋun yoni morapmɨ taŋ ɨmgwit, do gen uŋun nandaŋ but yokwi nandaŋek si kɨgɨt.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Epesas amɨn da Yesu Yolyol Kosit do yaŋba yokwi tok aŋek upbalap madepsi awit.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek kokup pap uŋun yɨpmaŋ waŋga pɨgek uŋun pɨlɨn kaga Betani kokupmon paŋkɨ pakgɨt.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat mɨktɨm tɨm kɨnda mani Getsemani uŋudon kɨwit. Kɨŋ altaŋek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji ɨdon yɨgakwa nak asɨdon kɨŋ bɨsit akeŋ.”
Paŋdet kabɨ yo uŋun noman tok do aban kaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, emat agak sɨbanin baŋ tagɨ dapneŋ?”
Kaŋek monjɨ dakon gen bin nandawit uŋun yaŋ teŋteŋaŋba
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun moneŋ kɨnam kɨnda wɨtjɨŋbi yombem. Amɨn kɨnda da moneŋ kɨnam kɨnda mɨktɨm kagagwan yɨpbi naŋ kaŋkwaŋ aeni aŋkɨ sɨbɨgɨt. Aŋek but galak nandaŋek yo kabɨni taŋ ɨmgwit uŋun kɨsisi amɨnon yumaŋ naŋek uŋun dakon moneŋɨ baŋ uŋun mɨktɨm tɨm yumaŋ nagɨt.”
Uŋun nak da naga yabekgo abeŋ do gak uŋun gat pɨgɨ kɨk do but bamot dɨma aki.”
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Moses da yaŋ mandagɨt: Amɨn kɨnda mɨŋatni kwɨnɨt do kaŋ, mɨŋat paŋkwɨnɨt papia kɨnda mandaŋ ɨmɨŋek kwɨnɨtjak.”
Aŋakwan Telagɨ Wup da Pilip yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak uŋun amɨn pawɨl pawɨl tamo da kapmatjok kɨki.”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn uŋun bɨsapmon nani dɨma kɨmagakwa yo morap uŋun kɨsi altaŋ mudokdaŋ.
Aŋakwa Amɨn Tagɨ dakon gen da uŋun mɨktɨm da kokup morap kɨsi ɨreŋ tagɨt.
Solomon uŋun Reoboam dakon datni. Reoboam uŋun Abiya dakon datni. Abiya uŋun Asa dakon datni.
Amɨn morapmɨ da abɨŋ nak dakon man yaŋek yaŋ yokdaŋ, ‘Nak naga Kristo.’ Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn morapmɨ paŋkewaldaŋ.
Kosit yolɨk amɨn, ji dabɨlji mɨni da ekwaŋ. Ji dakon tɨlak uŋun yaŋ. Amɨn da pakbi nok do aŋek yo monɨŋ pakbikon toŋ uŋun pɨndak maba kɨŋakwa pakbi noŋ, mani kamel madep dɨma noknogɨ uŋun dɨma kaŋek kaloŋ galaukba pɨgɨsak.
Amɨn kɨnda da ‘Nido yaŋ amal’ yaŋ dayɨŋban kaŋ, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ da pi kɨnda ak do aŋek yosok’ yaŋ iyɨŋbal uŋun da tepmɨ daban paŋopjil.”
Yaŋ aŋakwa kombɨ amɨn Jeremaia da gen mandagɨt uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ, “Israel amɨn da uŋun amɨn yumaŋ noni do silwa moneŋ 30 baŋ tomni yomgwit.
Aŋtɨdok awit do pasɨlɨkon da amɨn dɨwarɨ yaŋ yoyɨwit, “Ji kɨŋ amɨn yaŋ yoyɨni, ‘Nin nandaŋapno Stiwen da Moses gat Piŋkop gat do gen yokwi yaŋban nandamaŋ’ yaŋ yoyɨni.”
Gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Telagɨ Yut Madepmon amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgɨt. Aŋakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep gat, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat, ae amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn gat da Yesu niaŋ aŋek aŋatno kɨmotjak yaŋ do kosit wɨsɨwit.
Yaŋ iyɨŋban monji mibɨltogɨ butjap nandaŋek yutnon wɨgɨk do kurak tagɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan datni da yomakon pɨŋek butni maŋakwan yutnon wɨgɨsak do iyɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋbal Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Uŋun asi, tepmɨ pakdɨsat uŋun pakdamal. Mani namɨn da nak da amɨn tet do ae gwandeŋ tet do yɨtjak, uŋun nak da arɨpmɨ dɨma yaŋ dagokeŋ. Tamo uŋun Datno da amɨn kɨlɨ manjɨŋ yopgut uŋun dakon.”
“Bo namɨn dasi amɨn tebai kɨnda yɨgakwan yutnikon wɨgɨ yo kabɨni gwayeŋ tɨmɨtjak? Uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma. Mibɨltok tebai kendagek kɨsit kandapmɨyo wamaŋek yo kabɨni tagɨ gwayeni.
Uŋun kɨla amɨn madep da nin dakon babɨknin madepsi paŋkewalek yo jɨgɨsi aŋ yomgut. Yaŋ aŋek gen tebaisi yoyɨŋban monjɨ ŋakŋakni waŋga pabɨgɨ yopba taŋek kɨmakgwit.
Do Yesu jap noknok tamokon da pɨdaŋ ɨmal dubakni kukwaŋ yɨpmaŋek pakbi soŋ wɨrɨrɨt ɨmal kɨnda abɨdaŋek kogɨkon wamgut.
“Iyɨŋba nandaŋek yo kɨla amɨni uŋun yaŋ ɨban opban yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Gak niaŋ aŋaki gengo nandat? Gak kɨŋ yo morapno kɨlɨ niaŋ asal uŋun dakon but pɨso kɨnda mandaŋ nabi. Gak pi uŋun saŋbeŋek dɨma akdɨsal.’
yomanikon aŋkɨsak. Aŋkɨŋek notni gat ae kokup ɨsalni gat yaŋ yoban obɨŋ muwukba yaŋ yoyɨsak, ‘Sipsipno pasɨlak uŋun kɨlɨ wɨsɨŋ kat, do kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ano.’ ”
Muwugek Yesu do paba pɨgɨk gami kɨnda paŋ ɨmgwit. Yaŋ aŋek nap kelɨ toŋ kɨnda naŋ kɨla amɨn madep dakon pelɨt yombem kɨnda wasaŋek busuŋɨkon wamaŋ ɨmgwit.
Apolos uŋun Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgek pasol pasolɨ mɨni Piŋkop dakon gen madepsi yoyɨgɨt. Yoyɨŋakwan Prisila gat Akwila gat da geni nandaŋ Apolos abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ yutnikon egek Piŋkop dakon mibɨlɨ pakyaŋsi nandaŋ pɨsosak do iyɨŋ dekgɨmal.
Aŋakwan sipsip kɨla amɨn da tobɨl kɨŋek aŋelo da gen yoyɨgɨt uŋun da arɨpmon pɨndakgwit, do Piŋkop aŋkɨsiwit.
Kɨŋ altaŋek wain gat pakbi ɨsipmɨ kɨnda mani mea gat ɨktagɨlek ɨmɨŋba nok do kurak tagɨt.
Yaŋban yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak Rom amɨnsi dagok do tomni madepsi yumgɨm.” Yaŋban Pol da iyɨgɨt, “Gak yaŋ agɨl mani nak altagɨmon da Rom amɨnsi kɨnda egɨpgum da egɨsat.”
Yaŋban Juda amɨn da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak da pi tagɨsi kɨnda agɨl do aŋek tɨpbaŋ dɨma gɨtneŋ. Gak amɨn ɨsalɨ kɨnda da nak Piŋkop yaŋ yaŋek Piŋkop kulabɨsal uŋun do aŋek gɨtdamaŋ.”
“Gak da gen uŋun yal, uŋun ni bɨsapmon altokdaŋ? Ni yo da mibɨltok altaŋban kaŋek uŋun yo morap altosak dakon bɨsap kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandaneŋ?”
mani meŋi da yaŋ yagɨt, “Dɨma, mani Jon yaŋsi iyɨneŋ.”
Mani niaŋon da dabɨlɨ sɨŋtak uŋun nit dɨma nandamak. Ae namɨn da dabɨlɨ aban pɨsak, uŋunyo kɨsi nit dɨma nandamak. Uŋun amɨn madep kɨlɨ agɨt, do iyɨnaŋ iyɨŋba kobogɨ tagɨ dayɨsak.”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda nak do nandaŋek ji do Kristo dakon amɨn kabɨ yaŋ nandaŋek pakbi koleŋ damjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn dakon yumaŋ nogɨ dɨma pasɨl ɨmjak.”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Koŋ kɨnda da amɨn kɨnda yɨpmaŋ degek kɨŋ mɨktɨm kɨbɨrɨ tɨmon agek yɨk yawot tamo wɨsisak. Mani tamo kɨnda dɨma kosok do
Yo uŋun yaŋ do yosot: nandak nandak yokwi, amɨn dapba kɨmot, yumabi aŋpak mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ, kabo, topmon da gen pikon yopyop, ae yaŋba yokwi tok.
“On amɨn da amɨn Rom dakon gen teban dɨma guramɨtni do yoyɨŋ degek Piŋkop gawak ɨmɨm dakon kosit ŋwakŋwarɨ yolɨsak.”
Uwal da kɨsiron yɨpyɨp amɨn da gen kɨnda kɨlɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda nak da mandaŋ noko kaŋ, uŋun amɨn naŋ tebai abɨdoni.”
Yaŋ aŋakwa kombɨ amɨn kɨnda da kalɨpsigwan gen yagɨt uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Amɨn Tagɨ da aŋtagap aban yaŋ yagɨt: “Monjɨno Isip egɨsak uŋun opjak do yaŋ ɨmɨsat.” Josep gat mɨŋatni Monjiyo gat Isip mɨktɨmon paŋkɨ egakwa Erot don kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Nak gak gat gen yomak nak uŋun amɨn mani.”
Yaŋ yaŋakwa amɨn muwukgwit kɨsi da yaŋba yokwi tok aŋyomgwit. Yaŋ aba gen kokwin amɨn madep da amɨn bamot dakon paba pɨgɨkni ɨlɨgek kalɨŋ kɨrɨŋbaŋ baljoni do yoyɨwit.
Wɨsa dagaŋakwan Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn gat mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat gen kokwin ak do muwukgwit. Muwugek Yesu gen kokwin tamokon aŋkɨ yaŋ iyɨwit,
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak gen kobogɨ tagɨsi yosol, do koŋ gwago kɨlɨ yɨpmaŋ dek, do tobɨlek yutgokon kɨŋek koki.”
Yaŋ yaŋbal Yesu da amɨn bamot yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil nandaŋ kokwinjil tagɨ mɨni. Kombɨ amɨn da gen morap yawit uŋun butjilon da tepmɨ dɨma nandaŋ gadamal.
do yoyɨŋbɨ amɨn kabɨ madep kokup monɨŋ monɨŋ ae kokup terɨ dɨŋgwan kɨŋek jap yumaŋ noni.”
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Gak kɨlɨ nandal, do nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨsal. Amɨn nak dɨma nandaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ namaŋ, uŋun amɨn kɨsɨk kɨsɨk tagɨ ani.”
Mani Erot uŋun nandaŋek yagɨt, “Kalɨp nak da Jon dakon tegɨ mandaŋ dagagɨm, uŋun amɨn dasi kɨmoron da pɨdagɨt.”
Amɨn kɨnda da ‘Nido yaŋ amal’ yaŋ dayɨŋban kaŋ yaŋ iyɨnjil, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ da pi kɨnda ak do aŋek yosok. Donjok yɨpban opdɨsak.’ ”
Abɨŋ tap wakga tebaisi tɨdaŋakwan nin sigɨn kɨk do aŋtɨdok agɨmaŋ, do tap wakga yum kono mɨrɨm da iyɨ awɨlgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban monjɨ gɨmoŋɨ da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak uŋun gen teban morap guramɨk mudosot. Mani yo kɨnda gat ninaŋsi aŋek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokeŋ?”
Yaŋ nandaŋek Yesu do gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin dɨma nandamaŋ.”
Dat, mɨktɨm dɨma noman taŋakwan nak gak gat egek tɨlɨmno taŋ namgut. Abɨsok gak da ɨŋamon uŋun tɨlɨm aego nabi.
Pɨgɨ tugaŋba ɨlɨkba ɨleŋɨkon wɨkwan yɨgek tap kɨlap kokwinɨkgaŋ. Tagɨ amɨn ɨdap madepmon yopmaŋek yokwi amɨn maba kwaŋ.
Aŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyoni yoyɨŋ dekbɨ mibɨlni nandaba pɨsosak. Piŋkopnin uŋun bupmɨni madepsi, do dɨwarɨni wɨrɨrɨk yomɨŋek pulugaŋ tɨmɨtdɨsak yaŋ nandani. Uŋun da Kwen Kokup dakon teŋteŋɨ madep yɨpban
Gak yo morap pɨndak nandaŋyo agɨl uŋun mɨŋat amɨn morap yoyɨŋ teŋteŋokdɨsal.
Aŋopbal Simeon da Yesu bedaŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiŋek yaŋ yagɨt:
Yaŋ aban kaŋek emat amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn da Piŋkop aŋkɨsiŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Asisi, on amɨn kɨlegɨsi egɨpgut.”
Yaŋba Yesu gat agɨpgwit mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep da yaŋ yawit, “On Yesu, uŋun kombɨ amɨn kɨnda, Nasaret kokup Galili mɨktɨmon da abɨsak.”
Mani gak bɨsap dubagɨ abɨdono egɨpneŋ uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Do nandaŋ yawok nimɨŋek genin pɨsɨpmɨsok on nandaŋ nibi do gayamaŋ.
Wɨli 7 kabɨ kɨsi da pawit, do pɨdot pɨdot bɨsap madepmon namɨn dakon mɨŋatni asak?”
Yaŋba yagɨt, “Nak amɨn 4 tausen do bret 7 kabɨ pɨdaŋ yomgum bɨsapmon, ji jap dɨwat yɨk madepsi niaŋ da sɨmɨlba tugawit?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yɨk madepsi 7 kabɨ.”
Mani Pol gwaktani da kosiron pasɨlɨkon da aŋatdaŋ dakon geni nandaŋek emat amɨn da yutnon wɨgɨ Pol uŋun do iyɨgɨt.
Pol yaŋ yaŋek aeni kwen wɨgɨ bret pɨdaŋban nawit. Yaŋ aŋek gen sigɨn yoyɨŋakwan wɨgɨ wɨsa dagaŋakwan yopmaŋ kɨgɨt.
Aŋakwan Jon dakon paŋdetni da kɨŋ bumjotni abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ wayɨkgwit. Wayɨgek kɨŋ Yesu uŋun dakon geni iyɨwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak yaŋsi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda iyɨ do nandaban wugɨsak kaŋ, Piŋkop da uŋun amɨn abɨŋ yɨpdɨsak. Aŋek iyɨ do nandaba paŋ amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da pawɨgɨkdɨsak. Do takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn uŋun yutnikon tobɨl kɨŋek Piŋkop da dabɨlon dɨwarɨni mɨni egɨpgut. Mani Parisi amɨn uŋun dɨma.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn 120 yaŋ da Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit. Pita uŋun kabɨkon da pɨdaŋ agek yaŋ yagɨt,
Mani oman monjɨ kɨnda pi yokwi asak uŋun burɨkon da yaŋ nandɨsak, ‘Amɨn tagɨno uŋun tepmɨ dɨma apdɨsak.’
Ae jap yet joŋ kelɨ toŋ tɨmon mawit uŋun amɨn kɨnda yombem. Uŋun amɨn Piŋkop dakon gen nandɨsak, mani mɨktɨm dakon yo do nandaba kɨk asak, ae moneŋ da aŋkɨlɨkban uŋun do galagɨsi nandaŋakwan uŋun da Piŋkop gen wɨtjɨŋban bamɨ dɨma tosok.
“Gen uŋun iyɨŋban nandaŋek Moses pasal Midian mɨktɨmon paŋkɨ egek uŋudon mɨŋat kɨnda paŋek monjɨ bamorɨ paŋalagɨt.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Kapaneam kokupmon kɨŋ pɨsaŋek yutnon wɨgek Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kosiron ji ni gen naŋ yaŋ?”
Yaŋban dɨ da gen kɨnda yaŋakwa dɨ da ŋwakŋwarɨ yawit. Yaŋ yaŋek upbalap madep aŋakwa gen bamɨ kɨnda dɨma abɨdagɨt. Do Pol abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ emat amɨn da yomakon awɨgɨni do yoyɨgɨt.
Yesu yutnon wɨgakwan amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni bamot uŋudon wɨŋbal yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak da dabɨljil paŋmɨlɨp abeŋ do nandaŋ gadaŋ namamal bo dɨma?” Yaŋban iyɨgɨmal, “Amɨn Tagɨ, nandaŋ gadaŋ gamamak.”
Nak naga on mɨktɨmon nani dɨma, ae amɨn kabɨno uŋun kɨsi on mɨktɨmon nani dɨma, do nak gengo amɨn kabɨno do yobo mɨktɨm amɨn da nandaba yokwi tok aŋ yomgwit.
Gen yaŋ tosok, do amɨn wam da bamorɨ dɨma, gɨptɨm kaloŋɨ amal. Uŋun do Piŋkop da mɨŋat wɨli kɨlɨ paŋmuwukgɨt, do amɨn da dɨma paŋwasekdo.”
Iyɨ da kokupmon apban dabɨni da dɨma abɨdawit.
Sipsip uŋun yo ɨsalɨ, mani amɨn da yo madepsi. Yaŋdo, Sabat bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda aŋpulugoneŋ kaŋ, gen teban yapmaŋgaŋ yaŋ dɨma nandani.”
Nak dakon amɨn kabɨ uŋun gak dakon. Ae gak dakon amɨn kabɨ uŋun nak dakon. Amɨn da nak dakon amɨn kabɨno pɨndagek tɨlɨmno kaŋek man madep namaŋ.
Monjɨ buŋon nani da datni yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Dat, gak peno gat nit do yo morap nim do nandɨsal uŋun nak dakon dɨwarɨno abɨsok kokwinɨk nabi.’ Yaŋ yaŋban datni da yo kabɨni kokwinɨk monjɨ bamotni do yomgut.
Yesu pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda do kɨŋ altaŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da but dasi abɨdawit, nido uŋun do jomjom aŋek egɨpgwit.
Nandaba kɨkji yɨpmaŋek Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni uŋun wɨsɨŋ kok do pi ani. Yaŋ aŋakwa yo dɨwarɨ do wadak wadak aŋ uŋun kɨsi damdɨsak.”
Kalɨp nandaŋ kokwini tagɨ dɨma amɨn egakwa Piŋkop da yo kɨnda dɨma aŋyomɨŋek yum pɨndagakwan egɨpgwit. Mani abɨsok amɨn morap dukwan dukwan ekwaŋ but tobɨl ani do gen tebai yosok.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Dabɨl uŋun gɨptɨm dakon teŋteŋɨ. Dabɨlgo tagɨsi kaŋ, gɨptɨmgo kaloŋ teŋteŋɨni toŋ.
Bulmakau da tegon amɨn da yɨk pawɨl kɨndap kɨrɨŋ paŋteban aba yo jɨgɨ ɨlɨkgaŋ, uŋun da tɨlak ji nak dakon kɨndap kɨrɨŋ pani. Nak dakon kɨndap kɨrɨŋ uŋun yaworɨ ae yɨk ɨmetni uŋun tagapmɨ. Nak amɨn yaworɨ ae butno pɨŋbi, do nak gat egek Piŋkop do dayɨŋ dekgo butji yaworɨ tosak.”
Iyɨŋba yagɨt, “Piŋkop da ji baŋgɨn iyɨ dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ pasɨlɨ toŋ uŋun damɨsak. Mani amɨn dɨwarɨ tɨlak gen gɨn nandaŋ. ‘Do dabɨl sɨŋtaŋek kokdaŋ, mani dɨma kaŋ nandaŋyo akdaŋ. Ae gen nandakdaŋ, mani mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaba pɨsokdaŋ.’ ”
Yesu da gen uŋun yaŋban nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi aban yɨpmaŋ kɨwit.
Yaŋ yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Sunduk uŋun Kwen Kokup da mal da yaŋ maŋban kagɨm.
Egɨ Amɨn Tagɨ da paŋdet 72 gat manjɨgɨt. Aŋek iyɨ kokup dukwan dukwan kɨk do agɨt, uŋudon mibɨltok uŋun da kalɨp kɨni do bamot bamot yabekgɨt.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek Tomas yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak abɨŋ kɨsitno wɨtjɨŋek pɨndat. Aŋek kɨsitgo awɨŋ gekgeknokon wɨtjɨki. Gak but bamot dɨma aŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ nabi.”
Gen gayɨsat uŋun asi Piŋkop da bɨsap yɨpgut uŋun bɨsapmon noman tokdɨsak, mani nandabɨ bamɨ dɨma asak, do gen yogok kositgo sopmaŋakwan gen dɨmasi yaŋek egɨ wɨgaki gen gayɨsat uŋun bamɨ noman tokdɨsak.”
Aŋakwan Jonyo kɨsi amɨn telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomgut. Ainon kokupmon pakbi morapmɨ tawit do amɨn uŋudon apba telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomgut. Ainon uŋun Salim kokup da kapmatjok tosok.
Pol kɨlan kɨlan dɨ paŋmuwuk kɨndapmon soŋakwan tuŋon amɨn emarɨ toŋ kɨnda kɨndap tedep da yolban wɨgɨt. Wɨŋ Pol da kɨsiron ɨnjɨŋek geni duban pɨgakwan tegaŋ tagɨt.
Amɨn bamot uŋun kɨŋ Yesu altaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨmal, “Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn da yaŋ gayɨk do aŋek nit yabekban abamak, ‘Gak Piŋkop da amɨn yabet do yagɨt uŋun, bo nin amɨn kɨnda don apdɨsak do jomjom aneŋ?’ ”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, wit yet mɨktɨmon maŋek dɨma kɨmotjak kaŋ, ɨsal tokdɨsak. Mani kɨmotjak kaŋ, bamɨ morapmɨ tokdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋba amɨn kɨnda bɨkbɨknikon yɨkgɨt, mani Kaiapas, uŋun bɨlak do mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn egɨpgut, uŋun da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nandak nandakji mɨni.
Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun namɨn? Nayɨŋbɨ uŋun amɨn nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨbeŋ.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop da papiakon Yesu kɨmoron da ae pɨdokdɨsak dakon gen tosok uŋun do dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt.
Parisi amɨn moneŋ do galagɨsi nandaŋ, do Yesu da gen yagɨt uŋun nandaŋek yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmgwit.
Yesu telagɨ yut nagalgwan egek amɨn yoyɨŋ degek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da gen kɨnda yaŋ yoŋ, ‘Kristo uŋun Dewit dakon yawi dɨwatni.’ Mibɨlɨ nido yaŋ yoŋ?
“Yaŋba yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nandani. Amɨn morap yoni taŋ yomaŋ uŋun saŋbeŋek morapmɨ yomdɨsat. Mani amɨn kɨnda yoni mɨni kaŋ, yo kaloŋgok dɨ taŋ ɨmaŋ uŋun gwayekdɨsat.
Yaŋ iyɨŋban yo dɨ namdamal yaŋ nandaŋek tebai pɨndakgɨt.
(Wɨli 5 tausen da tɨlak egɨpgwit.) Yaŋba Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn 50 50 yaŋ paŋmuwuk yopba yɨk yɨk ani.”
Yoyɨŋban yaŋ yawit, “Nin Yesu Nasaret amɨn naŋ wɨsamaŋ.” Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Nak uŋun mani.” Yesu uwal da kɨsiron yɨpjak amɨn Judas uŋun amɨn kabɨ gat kɨsi akgwit.
dɨma apdɨsak yaŋ nandaŋakwan amɨn tagɨni da but pɨsogɨ mɨni abɨŋ uŋun oman monjɨ tepmɨ pi ɨmɨŋek gen kɨrɨŋɨt amɨn kabɨ gat yopban egɨpdaŋ.
Amɨn kɨnda dabɨlɨ mɨni meŋi da yaŋ aŋalagɨt naŋ amɨn kɨnda da wasok aban dabɨlɨ pɨsagɨt yaŋ kɨnda dɨma nandagɨmaŋ. Mɨktɨm wasok wasogɨkon da egɨ aŋaŋ obɨŋek abɨsok ekwamaŋon gen bin kɨnda yaŋ dɨma nandamaŋ.
Ae wain kalɨpmɨ nosok amɨn wain kalugɨ nok do kuragɨ nandaŋek yaŋ yosok, ‘Wain kalɨpmɨ uŋun tagɨsi.’ ”
Juda amɨn Jerusalem egɨpgwit uŋun da mukwa sogok amɨn ae Liwai amɨn yabekba Jonon kɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak niaŋen amɨn kɨnda?”
Tɨlak gen on dakon wasɨpmɨ do Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yaŋgɨn notji da yokwi aŋdaba yokwi yopyop but dasi nandaŋek dɨma ani kaŋ, Kwen Kokup Datno da yo jɨgɨ yaŋ gɨn aŋ damdɨsak.”
Do Pita Jerusalem kwan nandaŋ gadat amɨn gɨptɨmɨ mandabi da nandaba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmgwit.
Yaŋba Pol da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jon da amɨn telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomgut uŋun but tobɨl aŋek telagɨ pakbi soni do agɨt. Jon da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Amɨn kɨnda nak da buŋon noldak uŋun amɨn naŋ nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmni.’ Jon da gen yagɨt uŋun Yesu do yagɨt.”
“Mani pi asat uŋun yo kɨnda da joŋɨgek nak do yaŋ teŋteŋok asak uŋun da Jon da yaŋkwok agɨt uŋun yapmaŋdak. Yo uŋun pi morap Datno da aŋ mudokeŋ do namgut uŋun. Uŋun aŋapbo asi Dat da nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun nandaba bamɨsi asak.
Dɨwarɨ da dam tebanon yɨp do nandawit, mani amɨn kɨnda da dɨma abɨdagɨt.
Aŋek bɨt da bɨrap gɨp nawit uŋun pɨndak galak taŋek uŋun baŋ naŋek butno kadɨm tosak yaŋ nandagɨt. Mani amɨn kɨnda da jap kɨnda dɨma ɨmgut.
Yaŋ aban monji da datni yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Dat, nak Piŋkop da ɨŋamon ae gagon yo yokwisi agɨm, do buŋon monjɨno yaŋ dɨma nayɨki.’
Mani Pita da yagɨt, “Gen yosol uŋun dɨmasi nandɨsat.” Gen uŋun yaŋakwan pup uŋudon gɨn yagɨt.
“Amɨn da ji Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut madepmon, bo gapmanon, bo ae amɨn mani wukwi da ɨŋamon paŋkɨ depni bɨsapmon, dɨsi kutnok do aŋek ni gen baŋ yoyɨneŋ yaŋ nandaŋek nandaba kɨk dɨma ani.
Nin ɨleŋɨkon tagɨsi wɨgɨgɨmaŋ. Wɨgek mɨktɨm tɨmjok kɨnda tap binap tosok uŋun mani Malta uŋudon obɨmaŋ yaŋ kokup amɨn da niyɨŋba nandagɨmaŋ.
Mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyo madepsi pɨndakban paŋpulugogɨ mɨni yokwi egɨpgwit. Sipsip kɨla amɨni mɨni yombemsi ekwa pɨndagek bupmɨsi nandaŋ yomgut.
Nak asisi gayɨsat, gak dam tebanon sigɨn egaki wɨgɨ moneŋ niaŋ yopbi do gayɨni uŋun kɨsisi yopmaŋek don waŋga kɨkdɨsal.”
Uŋun amɨn bamot pɨndagek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Abɨŋ nak nolgɨl, aŋakwal amɨn tɨmɨt tɨmɨt dakon kosit dolɨko.”
Yesu da nandak nandakni uŋun pɨndak nandaŋyo aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido butjikon da nandak nandak uŋun nandaŋ namaŋ?
Yesu uŋun nandaŋek Jairus yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Dɨma pasolgi. Ɨsal nandaŋ gadat gɨn aŋaki gwago kɨlek tosak.”
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Amɨn tagɨ, uŋun bret bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ nin do nibi.”
Aŋakwan Yesu da yagɨt, “Namɨn da ɨgayɨŋ namɨk?” Yaŋban amɨn morap nin dɨma dɨma yaŋakwa Pita da iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, amɨn morapmɨsi da gak gat gadat gadatsi akwaŋ.”
Yaŋbal Yesu bupmɨ nandaŋek kɨsit da dabɨlɨ wɨtjɨŋban uŋudon gɨn sɨŋtaŋek Yesu yolgɨmal.
Konilias gat gwakni gat uŋun Piŋkop do pasal gawak ɨmɨŋek egɨpgwit. Yaŋ aŋek Konilias da Juda amɨn yoni mɨni amɨn paŋpulugagɨt. Ae bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ Piŋkop do bɨsit pi aŋek egɨpgut.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji amɨn dakon aŋpak dɨma kokwinɨtni kaŋ, Piŋkop da jiyo kɨsi dɨma kokwinɨtjak. Ji amɨn yokwi aba uŋun do kobogɨ tɨmɨtni do dɨma yoyɨni kaŋ, Piŋkop da jiyo kɨsi yokwisi do tebai dɨma dayɨkdɨsak. Ji amɨn dakon dɨwarɨni yopmaŋ yomni kaŋ, Piŋkop da ji dakon dɨwarɨsi yaŋ gɨn yopmaŋ damdɨsak.
Gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Yesu da amɨn Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan yoyɨŋ dekgɨt. Aŋek kalbi Ɨleŋ Olipmon yut kɨndakon paŋkɨ pak pak agɨt.
Bɨsap kaloŋ kaloŋ amɨn mɨktɨmni toŋ ae yutni toŋ uŋun amɨn do yomɨŋek moneŋ tɨmɨk paŋkɨ yabekbi kabɨ do yoba bupmɨ amɨn do kokwinɨk yomgwit, do bɨkbɨknikon bupmɨ amɨn kɨnda dɨma egɨpgut.
Yesu Kapaneam kokupmon pɨgakwan Rom dakon emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn kɨnda da abɨŋ aŋpulugosak do aŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Ae pi aban amɨn gen pikon yopyop dakon bɨsap apdɨsak yaŋ nandani, nido on mɨktɨm dakon kɨla amɨn madep uŋun kobogɨ yokwi tɨmɨtdɨsak.
Yaŋban gen tebaisi yaŋ yawit, “On amɨn Juda mɨktɨm kɨsisi agek amɨn yoyɨŋ degakwan kwen wɨgɨk aŋ. Galili mɨktɨmon da pi wasaŋek aŋakwan obɨŋ ɨdon obɨk.”
Yaŋban mɨŋatjok wagɨl kuŋwak yaŋ nandaŋek jɨkgo yanjaŋ ɨmgwit.
Uŋun kokupmon sakwabat kɨnda egɨpgut. Uŋun mɨŋat bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ gen kokwin kɨla agak amɨn madepmon abɨŋ abɨŋ aŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Uwalno gen pikon yɨpmaŋek nak aŋkutna.’
“Amɨn kɨnda da gen pikon gep do gen yaŋ gaban kaŋ, jil gen pi tamokon kɨk do aŋek kosiron kɨŋek gen uŋun tepmɨsi aŋmɨlɨp ak do pi anjil. Yaŋ dɨma anjil kaŋ, uŋun amɨn da gen kokwin kɨla agak amɨn da kɨsiron gepban uŋun da obip amɨn da kɨsiron gepban dam teban yutnon gepdɨsak.
Aŋakwan amɨn kɨsi da wɨsa dagokdosi pɨdaŋ Telagɨ Yut Madepmon geni nandak do kɨŋ kɨŋ awit.
Ae amɨn morapmɨ koŋni toŋ uŋun yol yomgut. Yolakwan koŋ da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Gak Piŋkop dakon Monji.” Yesu uŋun Kristo yaŋ nandaŋ ɨmgwit, do Yesu da koŋ gen dɨmasi yoni do kɨrɨŋɨk yomgut.
Judas uŋudon gɨn Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet!” Yaŋ iyɨŋek mogɨmɨkon mandaŋ nagɨt.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak jibaŋ gen kɨnda dayɨkdɨsat. Dayɨko kobogɨ nayɨni kaŋ, nakyo kɨsi kobogɨ tagɨ dayɨkeŋ.
Konilias da uŋun amɨn kapbɨ yo morap altaŋ ɨmeŋ uŋun kɨsi yoyɨŋ mudaŋek yabekban Jopa kɨwit.
Mani don monjɨ uŋun abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ kɨŋakwa notni uŋun bɨsapmon jap kelek ekwaŋ.
Mani kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek nak da kalɨp Galili mɨktɨmon mibɨltaŋ damɨŋek kɨkeŋ.”
Yesu da gen uŋun nandaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Sotni mɨni amɨn wuda wamagon dɨma kwaŋ. Sotni toŋ amɨn dagɨn wuda wamagon kwaŋ.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ae gen kɨnda babɨk da abɨdawit uŋun ji kɨlɨ nandawit. Gen uŋun yaŋ: ‘Notgo do but dasi galak taŋ yomɨŋek uwalgo do nandabɨ yokwi toni.’
Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn uŋun kɨsisi but kaloŋɨ ae nandak nandak kaloŋɨ paŋek egɨpgwit. Amɨn kɨnda da yo kabɨni do uŋun nak dakon yo yaŋ dɨma yagɨt. Yo morapnin uŋun amɨn kɨsin dakon yo yaŋ nandawit.
Iyɨŋban Maria Makdala kokupmon nani da kɨŋ paŋdet kabɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ nak da kɨlɨ kat.” Yaŋ yoyɨŋek Yesu da gen iyɨgɨt uŋun yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋba emat amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da pɨndakban gen emat madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋek amɨn kabɨ bamot uŋun da Pol terɨ terɨ da ɨlɨkba gɨptɨmɨ dagaŋakwan kɨmotjak yaŋ do pasalgɨt. Do emat amɨni yabekban pɨgɨ Pol amɨn kabɨ da binapmon naŋ gwayeŋ aŋaŋ emat amɨn da yutnon aŋkɨwit.
Ji dakon babɨkji da kalɨp kombɨ amɨn kɨsi morap do yo yokwisi aŋ yomgwit. Aŋek kombɨ amɨn dɨwarɨ Amɨn Kɨlegɨ don apjak do yaŋkwok awit babɨkji da uŋun amɨn dapba kɨmakgwit. Uŋun Amɨn Kɨlegɨ ji da uwal da kɨsiron yɨpba kɨlɨ aŋakba kɨmakgɨt.
Bo pup kwap do dayɨŋban skopion kɨnda tagɨ ɨmni?
“Yaŋba nandaŋek amɨn tagɨ uŋun da oman monjɨ uŋun iyɨŋban opban yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Gak pi monjɨ yokwi. Gak bɨsit tebai nayɨŋbɨ goman kɨsisi yɨpmaŋ gamɨt.
Yaŋban Saimon da iyɨgɨt, “Goman madepni dɨma sopjak do iyɨgɨt amɨn uŋun da, yaŋ nandɨsat.” Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak kokwin kɨlegɨsi aŋek yosol.”
Aŋakwan Pita da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ agɨt uŋun dakon geni Jopa amɨn kɨsi da nandawit. Nandaŋek amɨn morapmɨ da Amɨn Tagɨ do nandaŋ gadawit.
Aŋakwan paŋdetni mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ kɨŋ Piŋkop dakon geni yoyɨŋ aŋaŋ kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Amɨn Tagɨ uŋun gat egek paŋpulugaŋakwan wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ aŋek geni joŋɨk paŋteban agɨt.
Ae uŋun da buŋon nani mibɨltok yosok uŋun yombem gɨn. Uŋun yaŋ yosok: Gaga do but dasi niaŋ galak tosol, uŋudeŋ gɨn amɨn do but dasi galak taŋ yobi.
Betsaida kokupmon kɨŋ altaŋba amɨn dɨ da amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni kɨnda aŋaŋ opgwit. Aŋobɨŋek Yesu da kɨsitni da wɨtjɨsak do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit.
“Nak Daron kɨŋek ji gen pikon depdɨsat yaŋ dɨma nandani. Moses da ji paŋpulugosak yaŋ nandaŋ teban toŋ, mani dɨma. Moses da iyɨ gen pikon depdɨsak.
“Oman monjɨ gen uŋun nandaŋek amɨn tagɨ ŋwakbeŋ aŋ ɨmɨŋek bɨsit tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Butgo yaworɨ taŋakwan egaki don gomango kɨsisi sopbeŋ.’
Yesu do gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin dɨma nandamaŋ.” Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nakyo kɨsi namɨn da pi uŋun abeŋ do yaŋ mudaŋ namgut da pi asat uŋun dɨma dayɨkeŋ.”
Ae yerɨ dɨwarɨ da mɨktɨm tɨpmɨ toŋ tɨmon mawit. Uŋun kwenjok tawit, do tepmɨ kwawit, mani tɨp kwenon mɨktɨm morapmɨ dɨma, do gelɨ tagɨ dɨma yopba kɨwit. Do gɨldat da wɨŋ pɨndakban alek tawit.
Yesu Betani kokupmon altaŋek Lasarus uŋun kɨlɨ kɨmakgɨt da gɨldat 4 kabɨ kɨmakbi tamogwan tosok yaŋ nandagɨt.
Aŋakwan Jon dam tebanon yɨgek Kristo da pi agɨt dakon gen bin nandaŋek paŋdet kabɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Pɨlɨndo yoni morapmɨ amɨn kɨnda Arimatea kokupmon da apgut. Uŋun mani Josep. Uŋun Yesu dakon paŋdetni kɨnda.
Amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋun yut da nagalon kɨndap soŋek yɨgakwa Pita yo kɨsi uŋun gat yɨkgwit.
Jap naŋ yɨgakwa Yesu da bret kɨnda abɨdaŋ, Piŋkop ya yaŋ iyɨŋek, pudaŋ paŋdetni do yomgut. Yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Pabɨdaŋek noni, on nak dakon gɨptɨm tɨmno.”
Aban mɨŋat uŋun da Yesu dakon bin nandaŋek, mɨŋat amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋun da bɨkbɨgon egek manjikon kɨŋek ɨlɨkba pɨgɨknikon ɨgayɨgɨt.
Don bɨlak bamorɨ egɨ mudaŋakwa Posius Pestus da Peliks dakon tamo abɨdagɨt. Aŋakwan Juda amɨn da Peliks do nandaba tagɨ asak yaŋ do Peliks da Pol dam tebanon sigɨn yɨpban egɨpgut.
Uŋun Maria da pakbi kɨbaŋɨ toŋ tagɨsi Amɨn Tagɨ da kandapmon tagalek busuŋ daŋgwi naŋ ɨkdɨgaŋban kɨbɨdagɨt. Lasarus uŋun Maria gat peni gat dakon olapmɨ.
Mani nak gen bamɨ yosot, ae ji geno do nandaba bamɨ dɨma asak.
“Nak asisi dayɨsat, gen mɨktɨmon yaŋ aŋteban asal, Kwen Kokupmon Piŋkop da yaŋ gɨn yaŋ aŋteban akdɨsak. Ae gen mɨktɨmon yaŋ wɨtdaldal, Kwen Kokupmon Piŋkop da yaŋ gɨn yaŋ wɨtdaldɨsak.
Gen teban on da gen teban dɨwarɨ yapmaŋ mudosok.
Mani amɨn uŋun koŋ da yɨpmaŋ dek kɨwit amɨn da Yesu yol do bɨsit tebai iyɨgɨt. Iyɨŋban Yesu da tobɨl kɨsak do yabegek yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
nin kɨŋ Yesu dakon paŋdet kabɨni pɨndatno uŋun gat gɨldat 7 kabɨ egɨpgumaŋ. Egapno Telagɨ Wup da paŋtagap aban Pol yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak Jerusalem dɨma kɨki.”
Jerusalem amɨn gat ae kɨla amɨn gat da Yesu uŋun namɨn amɨn kɨnda yaŋ uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt. Ae kombɨ amɨn dakon gen Sabat bɨsap morap manjɨwit, mani dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt. Do uŋun amɨn gen pikon yɨpmaŋek aŋakba kɨmakgɨt. Yaŋ aba kombɨ amɨn da gen yawit uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt.
Yaŋ aŋakwa Banabas da Sol aŋaŋ yabekbi kabɨ da egɨpgwiron aŋkɨgɨt. Aŋkɨŋek Sol da kosiron Amɨn Tagɨ kagɨt ae Amɨn Tagɨ da gen iyɨgɨt uŋun dakon geni yoyɨgɨt. Yoyɨŋek Sol da Damaskus Yesu dakon mani pasol pasolɨ mɨni yaŋ teŋteŋaŋ yomgut uŋun kɨsi do yoyɨgɨt.
Datji kaloŋɨ uŋun Kwen Kokup egɨsak, do mɨktɨm amɨn kɨnda do dat yaŋ dɨma iyɨni.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Piŋkop dakon gen nandaŋek guramɨkgaŋ uŋun meŋno ae padɨk padɨknoni.”
Kalɨp Moses da gen teban damgut, mani jikon da amɨn kɨnda da uŋun gen teban dɨma guramɨkdak. Ji nak nido nɨkba kɨmokgeŋ do nandaŋ?”
Uŋun kokupmon amɨn morapmɨ da Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit.
Amɨn morap burɨ kɨlegɨsi toŋ, uŋun amɨn da Piŋkop kokdaŋ, do uŋun kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ekwaŋ.
Iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn dabɨlɨ kɨlek taŋban Yesu yolek Piŋkop aŋkɨsigɨt. Yaŋ aban mɨŋat amɨn morap kɨsi da kaŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiwit.
Mɨktɨm amɨn kɨnda da Dat dɨmasi kagɨt. Amɨn uŋun Piŋkop gat egɨpgumal da apgut uŋun dagɨn Dat kagɨt.
Uŋun amɨn pɨlɨn tukgwan egek kɨmot do pasolgoŋ, mani uŋun da teŋteŋɨ madep altaŋ yoban kɨlɨ kaŋ.”
“Kalɨp Israel amɨn da Moses abɨŋ yɨpmaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, ‘Namɨn da mibɨltok amɨn ae gen kokwin amɨnin manjɨŋ gepmak?’ Piŋkop da uŋun Moses naŋgɨn mibɨltok amɨni ae jɨgɨkon baŋ tɨmɨtjak amɨni yabek yomgut. Aŋelo kɨndap monɨŋon akgɨt uŋun da Piŋkop dakon gen abɨdaŋek Moses yabekgɨt.
Amɨn kɨnda nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨŋek telagɨ pakbi sosak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn Kwen Kokup do amɨn asak. Ae amɨn kɨnda nak dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ namjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn Tɨpdom do amɨn asak.
Yesu bot bamorɨ ɨleŋɨkon taŋbal pɨndakgɨt. Uŋun tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl amɨn da yopba taŋakwal tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨkni pakbikon sugawit.
Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil ni gen baŋ yaŋ nandat aŋek kwamal?” Yaŋ yoyɨŋban bupmɨ tomno dabɨlyo aŋek akgɨmal.
Gak da pi morap namgul, uŋun pi aŋ mudoko mɨktɨm amɨn da tɨlɨmgo kɨlɨ kawit.
Uŋun yo morap altaŋakwa Amɨn Tagɨ da kombɨ amɨn aŋtagap aban gen yagɨt uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ tosok.
Yoyɨŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon bɨsap kwaŋ tosok, do ji but tobɨl ani.”
Uŋun kɨsit kɨlda kɨnda, Maria dakon monji. Padɨk padɨkni uŋun Jems, Josep, Judas ae Saimon. Ae samɨni binapninon ekwaŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋek ɨŋtaŋ ɨmɨŋek nandaba pɨŋban ɨmgwit.
kaŋek nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi aban yaŋ nandawit, “Mao! On amɨn yoma kaga mani Kɨldani Tagɨsi uŋudon yɨgek amɨn da moneŋ ɨmni do bɨsit asak amɨn oni. Uŋun da kɨlek tak!”
Iyɨŋban yagɨt, “Ji Amɨn Tagɨ Piŋkopji uŋun but gat ae wup gat ae tapmɨmgo gat ae nandak nandakgo gat kɨsi but dasi galak taŋ ɨbi. Ae gaga do but dasi niaŋ galak tosol, uŋudeŋ gɨn amɨn do but dasi galak taŋ yobi.”
“Jɨgɨ mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ paŋek wararɨ nandaŋ amɨn, ji nagon opba bɨkbɨk dabo yɨk yawotni.
(Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmni amɨn da don Telagɨ Wup abɨdoni do gen uŋun yagɨt. Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu man madep dɨma pagɨt, do Telagɨ Wup dɨma yobi.)
Amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ Piŋkop do pasalek gawak ɨmaŋ ae aŋpak kɨlegɨ aŋ, uŋun amɨn do Piŋkop da nandaban tagɨsi asak.
Uŋun bɨsapmon gɨn Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak ɨdon dɨma egɨpbi, kokup dɨgwan kɨki. Erot da gak gɨkban kɨmokgi do nandɨsak.”
Mani nak da amɨn kɨnda do pakbi ɨbo nosak kaŋ, ae pakbi do dɨma akdɨsak. Nak da pakbi ɨbeŋ uŋun da butnikon pakbi dabɨl kɨnda mudok mudogɨ mɨni taŋ ɨmdɨsak. Pakbi dabɨl uŋun da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni ɨmdɨsak.”
“Yaŋ paŋ muwugek pi monjɨ pɨlɨndosi abeŋ uŋun do moneŋ 1 danari yomɨŋ yomɨŋ agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban yum kaŋek kɨŋ gen bin yaŋ aŋɨreŋ agɨt. Uŋun do aŋek Yesu kokup papmon noman kɨsak do nandaban tɨdok tagɨt. Kokup ɨleŋɨ ɨleŋɨkon gɨn agakwan amɨn morap dukwan dukwan egɨpgwit Yesukon apgwit.
Kɨŋ uŋun kokup dakon tɨp dam dakon wigat aŋkapmat agɨt. Aŋek amɨn da amɨn kɨmakbi kɨnda wamaŋ aŋaŋ waŋga pɨŋba pɨndakgɨt. Amɨn kɨmakgɨt uŋun dakon meŋi uŋun sakwabat egakwan monjɨ kaloŋɨsi da kɨmakgɨt. Uŋun kokup madep dakon amɨn morapmɨsi uŋun sakwabat gat kɨsi pɨŋba pɨndakgɨt.
Yaŋba yutgwan amɨn kɨnda da Yesu iyɨgɨt, “Meŋgo padɨk padɨkgo yomakon abeŋ da gak gat yaŋ nandat ak do yoŋ.”
Ae nin da kabɨkon nani mɨŋat dɨ da gen ŋwakŋwarɨsi niyɨŋba nandamaŋ. Uŋun wɨsa dagokdosi tɨp kɨnamon kɨŋ
“Uŋun amɨn madep kɨlɨ agɨt, do iyɨ naŋ iyɨŋba kobogɨ dayɨsak.”
Mani Pol da pɨgɨ monjɨ uŋun da kwenon pagek kɨsirɨ da kendagek yagɨt, “Ji nandaba kɨk dɨma ani. Egɨp egɨpni taŋ ɨmɨsak.”
Yaŋ aŋek amɨn Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan yoni tɨmɨgek kɨŋ ap dɨma ani do yaŋsop aŋyomgut.
Yo uŋun Amɨn Tagɨ da agɨt, aŋakwan nin da kono yo masɨ masɨmɨsi asak.’ ”
Mani Piŋkop da Elaija Israel sakwabat kɨnda do dɨma yabekgɨt. Sakwabat kɨnda Sarepat kokupmon egɨpgut uŋun do yabekban kɨgɨt. Sarepat uŋun Saidon kokup da tetgɨn do tosok.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon obip amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat obip amɨn kabɨni gat da kɨŋ yabekbi kabɨ tɨmɨk paŋopgwit. Mani mɨŋat amɨnyo da tɨpbaŋ nindapni yaŋ do pasalek yo jɨgɨ dɨ dɨma aŋ yomɨŋek tayaŋgok paŋopgwit.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Mibɨlɨ nido? Ni gulusuŋ naŋ agɨt?” Yaŋban mibɨltok yawit si yapmaŋek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakbɨ kɨmotjak!”
Elisabet monjɨ kwap awɨlgɨt uŋun dakon kanek 6 mudaŋakwan Piŋkop da aŋeloni Gebriel yabekban mɨŋatjok kɨnda mani Maria uŋun do kɨgɨt. Galili mɨktɨmon, kokup kɨnda mani Nasaret uŋudon egɨpgut. Maria uŋun amɨn kɨnda mani Josep, Dewit da kabɨkon nani uŋun pasak do manjɨkbi.
Yaŋban Yesu da aŋtobɨlek iyɨgɨt, “Mango namɨn?” Yaŋ iyɨŋban yagɨt, “Nak mano Amɨn Kabɨ Madep. Nin morapmɨ da ekwamaŋ.”
“Awa! Ji kombɨ amɨn dakon bumjot tamo wasoŋ. Mani babɨkji da dapba kɨmakgwit.
Yaŋban Yesu agek amɨn uŋun abɨdaŋ aŋopni do yoyɨgɨt. Yoyɨŋban kapmat aŋapba Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋakwan pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo paŋdetni da abɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Mɨktɨm amɨn dɨma ekwaŋon ekwamaŋ, ae gɨldat kɨlɨ pɨgɨkdɨsak,
Yesu Ɨleŋ Olipmon yɨgakwan Telagɨ Yut Madep ason tet tagɨt. Aŋakwan Pita, Jems, Jon ae Andru da iyɨ gɨn Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit,
“Ji gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn do pɨndak kɨmotni. Uŋun ɨmal dubagɨ baŋ paŋek agɨp do galak toŋ. Ae yumaŋ gwayek tamokon amɨn da gɨldat tagɨ yaŋ yoyɨni do galagɨ nandaŋ. Ae muwut muwut yutnon tamo tagɨsikon yɨt do galak toŋ. Ae jap noknok bɨsap madepmon tamo amɨn mani toŋ do tɨlak abi uŋudon yɨt do galak toŋ.
Mani abɨsok nak da yaŋ dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda mɨŋat kɨnda kaŋek uŋun do galak taŋ ɨmjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn butnikon da yumabi kɨlɨ ak.
Aŋek amɨn dɨ yabekban uŋun da kalɨp mibɨltaŋ Samaria dakon kokup kɨndakon yut tamoyo paŋnoman ani do kɨwit.
Yaŋ aba kɨla amɨn madep uŋun japmɨsi nandaŋek emat amɨni yabekban kɨŋ pi monjɨni dapgwit amɨn uŋun kɨsisi dapba mɨni awit. Aŋek kokupni sowit.
Parisi amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Ni bɨsapmon Piŋkop Amɨn Kɨla Agakni yɨpban apdɨsak?” Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Agakni yɨpban apban amɨn da dabɨlni da kaŋba pɨsosak dakon tɨlak altaŋba dɨma pɨndatdaŋ.
Emat amɨn da Pol aŋaŋ yutnikon awɨgɨk do aŋakwa emat amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn Grik genon da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gen kɨnda tagɨ gayɨkeŋ?” Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Gak Grik gen nandɨsal, ma?
Paŋpulugok damdɨsak uŋun gen bamɨ dakon Wup. Mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma abɨdogɨ, nido dɨma koŋ, ae dɨma nandaŋ ɨmaŋ. Mani ji da nandaŋ ɨmaŋ. Ji gat egɨsak, ae don ji da butgwan egɨpdɨsak.
Yesu da tɨlak gen uŋun yaŋban dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt.
Mani ni gen bamɨ kɨnda naŋ mandaŋ yɨpbo amɨn madepninon kɨsak uŋun dɨma nandako pɨsosok. Dam tebanon amɨn kɨnda yɨpbo kɨŋakwan gen yaŋ ɨmgwit dakon but pɨso gen kɨnda gat dɨma yɨpbo kɨsak kaŋ uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Do kɨla amɨn madep Agripa, gak ae amɨn kabɨ ji kɨsi da on amɨn dakon mibɨlɨ nandani do aŋek muwamaŋ. Mibɨlni pakyaŋsi nandano pɨsaŋakwan gen bamɨ papiakon tagɨ mandakeŋ.”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn morap mɨktɨmon altoŋ uŋun Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn da yapmaŋ mudosok. Mani amɨn morap Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan pɨŋbisi ekwaŋ uŋun da Jon yapmaŋgaŋ.
Bɨsap kɨnda apdɨsak uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da yaŋ yokdaŋ, ‘Mɨŋat monjɨ suŋ ekwaŋ ae mɨŋat monjɨ mɨni ae mɨŋat monjɨ da mumɨ dɨma naŋbi, uŋun kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ekwaŋ.’
Juda amɨn Maria dakon but aŋteban ak do yutnon egɨpgwit uŋun da kaŋba Maria tepmɨsi pɨdaŋ waŋga pɨkwan kaŋ, kɨmakbi tamokon kunam tat do kɨsak yaŋ nandaŋek buŋon yolgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋek Yesu da gen teban dakon nandak nandak amɨn yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Niaŋ nandɨsal, uŋun amɨn kapbɨ da kabɨkon namɨn da kabo noknok da aŋakgwit amɨn uŋun do but dasi galak taŋ ɨmgut?”
Ɨmalno mɨni egapbo ɨmal namgwit. Sot abo aŋpulugawit. Dam teban yutnon yɨgapbo abɨŋ nandawit.’
Yesu yagɨt da arɨpmon Piŋkop da kɨlɨ aban pɨdak. Ɨdon dɨma egɨsak. Abɨŋ tamoni do konjil.
Yesu bɨlakni 30 da tɨlak aŋakwan pini wasagɨt. Yesu uŋun Josep dakon monji amɨn da yaŋ nandawit. Josep uŋun Eli dakon monji.
Yesu gen yaŋakwan uŋudon gɨn paŋdetni 12 kabɨkon da kɨnda mani Judas altaŋ yomgut. Amɨn kabɨ madep emat agak sɨbani ae kɨndap kɨrɨŋni tɨmɨgek buŋon yolgwit. Mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae kɨla amɨn uŋun da yabekba apgwit.
Piŋkop da yaŋ abeŋ yaŋ kɨlɨ nandagɨt, do amɨn uŋun ji da kɨsiron yɨpgut. Yɨpban ji da amɨn yokwi da kɨsiron yɨpba uŋun da abɨdaŋek tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmakgɨt.
Yesu uŋun boron wɨgek pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda do wɨgakwan amɨn morapmɨsi abɨŋ muwukgwit.
Yaŋ nandaŋakwan iyɨgɨt, “Maria, dɨma pasolgi. Piŋkop da gak do nandaban tagɨsi asak.
Yaŋ yaŋakwa dɨwarɨ da yawit, “Gen yosok uŋun koŋni toŋ amɨn dakon gen naŋ dɨma yosok. Koŋ da dabɨlɨ mɨni amɨn arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋmɨlɨp agagɨ.”
Yesu da gen uŋun yaŋ mudaŋakwan amɨn dɨwarɨ da Pailat da yo agɨt uŋun do iyɨwit. Pailat da obip amɨni yoyɨŋban kɨŋ Galili amɨn dɨwarɨ Piŋkop do mukwa soŋakwa uŋun dapba kɨmakgwit. Do uŋun amɨn dakon yawini gat ae paret do yo mukwa sowit dakon yawini kɨsi mawit.
Uŋun gɨldaron gɨn amɨn 3 tausen Pita dakon gen nandaba bamɨ agɨt. Yaŋ aŋek telagɨ pakbi soŋek Yesu da paŋmuwukbi kabɨkon saŋbewit.
Banabas uŋun amɨn tagɨsi, nandaŋ gadatni tebaisi taŋakwan Telagɨ Wup uŋun da buron tugagɨt, do amɨn morapmɨsi da Amɨn Tagɨkon kɨwit.
Amɨn da yumaŋ naŋek dɨpmɨn pokgoŋ yut uŋun amɨn da yɨkba tugagɨt, do bulmakau yut kɨndakon pawɨgɨ yɨkgɨmal. Yɨgakwal monjɨ mibɨltogɨ altaŋban Maria da ɨmalnaŋ wamaŋ bulmakau ɨdapmon yɨpban pakgɨt.
Yesu da tɨlak gen uŋun yaŋban gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat da nin pabɨŋ nip do aŋek yosok yaŋ nandawit. Yaŋ nandaŋek Yesu uŋudon gɨn abɨdokdosi nandawit, mani mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep uŋun do si pasalgwit.
Wɨsa dagok do Yesu gat paŋdetni gat ɨleŋ yɨpmaŋ pɨgakwa amɨn kabɨ madepsi kosiron domdom awit.
Uŋun kokup papmon amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut uŋun mani Saimon. Uŋun koŋ da tapmɨm ɨmɨŋakwa wasok amɨn da dɨma agagɨ morapmɨ kɨlɨsok aban Samaria mɨŋat amɨn morap kɨsi da kaŋek but morap nandaŋ ɨmgwit. Uŋun amɨn da iyɨ do nak kɨla amɨn madep kɨnda yaŋ yagɨt.
Mani ji uŋun nak dakon sipsip kabɨ dɨma, do dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ namaŋ.
Pol Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yutnon wɨgek Piŋkop gen madepsi yoyɨgɨt. Aŋek Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak dakon gen do yaŋek gulusuŋ nandak nandakni paŋmɨlɨp ak do aban notni pabɨŋ yopmaŋ yopmaŋ awit. Pol pi uŋun aŋek kanek kapbɨ egɨpgut.
Pol da wasok uŋun aban kaŋek mɨŋat amɨn morapyo da Likonia genon da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Mao, piŋkop ekwaŋ dɨ da amɨn gɨptɨm paŋek ninon peŋ!”
Pol Ariopagus muwut muwut tamokon kɨla amɨn da binapmon pɨdaŋ agek yaŋ yagɨt, “Atens amɨn nak kokupji aŋgwasɨŋek agek piŋkop gawak yomyom aŋ uŋun dakon yo kɨdat pɨndakgɨm. Pɨndagek alta kɨndakon gen kɨnda yaŋ mandabi kagɨm: On Alta Uŋun Piŋkop Kɨnda Mibɨlni Dɨma Nandamaŋ Uŋun do Wasaŋbi. Nak yaŋ kagɨm do aŋek ji do yaŋ nandɨsat, ji piŋkop gawak yomyom dakon aŋpak do nandaba yo madepsi asak. Uŋun Piŋkop mibɨlni dɨma nandaŋek ɨsal dogɨn gawak ɨmaŋ uŋun dakon mibɨlɨsi dayɨko nandabɨt.
Egɨp egɨpmon niyɨŋ paŋpaŋ kɨgɨk amɨn uŋun ji da aŋakba kɨmakgɨt. Mani Piŋkop da kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdagɨt. Pɨdaŋban kagɨmak do nit uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋok amak.
Kalɨpsigwan nin dakon babɨknin gak dakon oman amɨngo Dewit Telagɨ Wup da aŋtagap aban gen yaŋ yagɨt: ‘Amɨn kabi kabi mibɨlɨ nido japmɨsi nandaŋek iyɨ do nandaba wukwanek ɨsal dogɨn yo yokwi ak do gen yaŋ paŋteban aŋ?
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk ɨmni. Amɨn kɨnda nak dakon man yaŋek wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ asak uŋun amɨn nikon da nak do yaŋba yokwi tok asak? Uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma.
Mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madepsi mibɨltok kɨwit ae buŋon yolgwit kɨsi da gen pap yaŋek yaŋ yawit: “Osana! Dewit Dakon Monji aŋkɨsino! Amɨn on Amɨn Tagɨ da manon abɨsak, uŋun Piŋkop da gɨsamɨgakwan abɨsak. Piŋkop Wɨkwisi aŋkɨsino!”
Pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nandaŋ gadat awit bɨsapmon Telagɨ Wup abɨdawit bo dɨma?” Yaŋ yoyɨŋban yawit, “Dɨma, nin Telagɨ Wup kɨnda egɨsak yaŋ dɨma nandagɨmaŋ.”
Piŋkop da amɨn kɨmakbi ae wayɨŋ abi uŋun kɨsi aŋpakni kokwin asak do uŋun amɨn manjɨgɨt. Nin da gen uŋun amɨn yoyɨneŋ do Yesu da yaŋ nimgut.
Aban Josep da kɨŋ ɨmal kwakwagɨ kɨnda yumaŋ aŋabɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjot tɨlak kɨndapmon naŋ abɨŋ uŋun ɨmal naŋ wamgut. Wamaŋ aŋkɨ tɨp kɨnam kɨndakon yɨpmaŋek tɨp madepsi kɨnda aŋtobɨlban abɨŋ yoma sopgut.
Do gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil kɨŋ abɨsok yo pɨndak nandaŋyo amal uŋun do Jon iyɨnjil. Dabɨlni mɨni amɨn sɨŋtoŋ, ae kandapmɨ alek taŋbi amɨn kosit akwaŋ, ae wuda tebani toŋ amɨn uŋun kɨlek toŋ, ae mɨragɨ mɨni amɨn da gen nandaŋ, ae amɨn kɨmakbi pɨdoŋ, ae yoni mɨni amɨn da Gen Bin Tagɨsi nandaŋ.
Aŋakwan Kwen Kokupgwan da gen kɨnda yaŋ altagɨt: “Gak Monjɨno. Butdasi galak taŋ gamɨsat. Butno gak do tagɨsi asak.”
Yaŋba Pailat da aeni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji dakon galaktok on amɨn bamoron baŋ namɨn naŋ pulugaŋ yɨpbo kɨsak do nandaŋ?” Yoyɨŋban “Barabas naŋ” yaŋ yawit.
Paŋdetni gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaba pɨsawit. Mibɨlɨ pasɨlɨ tagɨt, do gen uŋun mibɨlɨ nido yosok uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt.
Yaŋ nandaŋakwa Yesu uŋun burɨkon da pɨndak nandaŋ yomɨŋ mudaŋek yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido butjikon da nandak nandak uŋun nandaŋ namaŋ?
Do, niaŋ nandɨsal, Sisa do takis ɨmno tagɨ asak, bo dɨma?”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban kosiron kɨŋ Itopia amɨn kɨnda kagɨt. Uŋun amɨn gapman dakon amɨn madepni kɨnda egɨpgut. Itopia dakon kɨla amɨn madep mɨŋat Kandasi dakon moneŋ kɨla amɨn madepni egɨpgut. Uŋun amɨn Piŋkop gawak ɨm do Jerusalem opgut.
Nak uŋun gat egɨpgumaŋ bɨsapmon man namgul uŋun naŋ paŋkutnaŋapbo tagɨsi egɨpgwit. Uŋun amɨn kabɨkon da amɨn pasɨljak do yaŋbi uŋun dagɨn pasɨlgɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan Piŋkop da papiakon gen uŋun do mandabi uŋun bamɨ toŋ agɨt.
Mani bɨsap kɨnda apjak, ae kɨlɨ abɨk, uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn Telagɨ Wup da tapmɨmon da, ae aŋpak bamɨsikon da Dat gawak ɨmdaŋ. Dat da uŋuden amɨn da gawak ɨmni do galak tosok.
Paŋdetni 11 kabɨ Galili mɨktɨmon kɨŋ, Yesu da kabap kɨnda uŋudon wɨgɨni do kɨlɨ yoyɨgɨt uŋudon wɨgɨwit.
Yaŋban Yesu da mibɨlni amɨn dɨmasi yoyɨni do yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋban mɨŋat uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma pasɨlgeŋ yaŋ nandaŋek nɨmnɨmɨk abɨŋ Yesu da kandap mibɨlon maŋ pakgɨt. Maŋ pagek amɨn morap da dabɨlon mibɨlɨ nido Yesu ɨgayɨgɨt uŋun dakon yaŋkwok aŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ɨgayɨko sotno uŋudon gɨn pasɨlak.”
Yolɨŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On yut madep madep pɨndakgaŋ uŋun dakon tɨp notni da kwenon dɨma taŋ taŋ akdaŋ. Tuwɨlba kɨsisi maŋ mudokdaŋ.”
Nak kɨŋ ji dakon tamo paŋnoman aŋek, aeno tobɨl abɨŋ ji tɨmɨkgo paŋkɨ nak gat egɨpneŋ.
Mani amɨn kɨnda egɨsak uŋunyo kɨsi nak da pi asat uŋun joŋɨgek yaŋ teŋteŋok asak. Nak nandɨsat, gen yaŋ teŋteŋok asak uŋun bamɨsi yosok.
Yesu da mukwa sogok amɨn tagɨ gat ae kɨla amɨn gat saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda monjɨ bamorɨ gat egɨpgwit. Egek monji mibɨltogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Monjɨno abɨsok kɨŋ wain pinokon pi aki.’
“Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae Parisi amɨn ji jamba but amɨnsi. Awa! Ji amɨn kaloŋɨ kɨnda da paŋdetji dagosak do pi teban aŋek tap kwenon da mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ akwaŋ. Ji Tɨpdom do amɨn aŋ, do amɨn kɨnda abɨdoni kaŋ, iyɨŋ dekba uŋun amɨn yaŋ gɨn Tɨpdom do amɨn akdɨsak. Ae uŋun gɨn dɨma, ji da aŋpak yokwi aŋ uŋun si yapmaŋek uŋun amɨn aŋpak yokwisi asak.
Aŋakwa aŋpak yokwi da madepsi ɨreŋ taŋ aŋ aŋ kɨkdɨsak. Yaŋ aŋakwa amɨn morapmɨ da not do but dasi galak taŋ yomyom aŋpak yɨpba wɨtdal kɨkdɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋban yokwi pakpak terɨ kɨnda aŋakbi uŋun da gen tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Piŋkop do dɨma pasoldol, ma? On amɨn da tepmɨ pasak nityo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn pamak.
Mani Mata uŋun jap dakon oman do nandaba kɨk morapmɨ aŋek obɨŋ Yesu iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, padɨgɨno nepmak da naga gɨn pi madep asat. Gak uŋun do dɨma nandɨsal? Iyɨŋbɨ obɨŋ nak aŋpulugaŋban.”
Mani gen yokwi yomaŋ uŋun nandak nandakninon da wɨŋ butnin paŋupbal asak.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, kokup yomasiyo yokwi taŋek yumsi tokdɨsak.
amɨn wam kɨlɨ abi da yumabi aŋpak, pɨndak galaktok, aŋpak yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ, top gen yogok, kwen wɨgɨk, tagɨsi ekwaŋ amɨn do nandaba yokwi tok nandak nandak, ae not do yokwi yogok, gen kɨrɨŋɨt, ae ŋugɨgɨ aŋpak.
Wasaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Wɨli da meŋi datniyo yopmaŋek mɨŋatni gat muwukbal gɨptɨm kaloŋɨ anjil.’
Aŋek amɨn dakon galaktok yolek amɨn uŋun kalɨp gapman gat emat wamgut, ae amɨn kɨnda aŋakban kɨmakban dam tebanon yɨpgwit, uŋun yɨpban kɨgɨt. Ae galaktokni yolek Yesu aŋakba kɨmotjak do emat amɨn da kɨsiron yɨpgut.
Mani Pita waŋga yoma kaga da kapmatjok akgɨt. Do paŋdet uŋun mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da nandaŋ ɨmgut uŋun da kɨŋ oman mɨŋat kɨnda yoma kɨla agɨt uŋun iyɨŋek Pita abɨdaŋban nagalgwan pɨgɨgɨmal.
Pol gat Banabas gat Antiok kokupmon Piŋkop dakon pi agɨmal uŋudeŋ gɨn Ikoniam kokupmon yaŋ gɨn agɨmal. Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yut kɨndakon wɨgek gen tagɨsi yoyɨŋakwal Juda ae Grik amɨn morapmɨ da nandaŋ gadat awit.
Yesu bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok egek kokup kɨnda mani Nain uŋudon kɨŋakwan paŋdetni gat ae amɨn morapmɨsi gat kɨsi kɨwit.
Yaŋ yaŋek paŋdet kabɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nak da pino ani do yabekgɨm bɨsapmon, moneŋ sɨmɨl yɨk monɨŋ, ae yɨk madep, ae kandap gwɨlyo dɨma tɨmɨkgwit. Uŋun bɨsapmon ji yo kabɨ do wadak wadak awit bo dɨma?” Yaŋ yoyɨŋban iyɨwit, “Dɨma.”
