“Amɨn Tagɨ, gak monjɨno do bupmɨ nandaŋ ɨbi! Uŋun bɨsap morapmɨ tebaisi nɨmnɨmɨgek jɨgɨ tepmɨyo madepsi pasak. Aŋek bɨsap morapmɨ kɨndapmon mosok bo ae pakbi kagagwan maŋ pɨgɨsak.
Yaŋ kaŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek kɨŋ Saimon Pita gat ae Yesu da paŋdetni kɨnda but dasi galak taŋ ɨmgut uŋun bamot yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ kɨmakbi tamokon naŋ aŋabɨgeŋ. Aŋkɨ dukwan yɨpmaŋ uŋun dɨma nandamaŋ.”
Yaŋ kosok, do kɨŋ koŋ 7 kabɨ iyɨ yapmaŋek wagɨl yokwisi gat tɨmɨkban kwa uŋun yutnon egek aŋpak yokwisi aŋ. Mibɨltok uŋun amɨn yokwi egɨpgut, mani abɨsok uŋun yapmaŋek wagɨl yokwisi egɨsak. Yaŋgɨn abɨsok yokwi pakpak amɨn ekwaŋon yaŋ gɨn altosok.”
Gen teban mibɨlɨ nandak nandak amɨn kɨnda da gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, Parisi amɨn do gen uŋun yaŋek, ninyo kɨsi pabɨŋ nipmaŋdal.”
Wɨli 7 kabɨ kɨsi da pawit, do amɨn da kɨmoron da pɨdoni bɨsap madepmon namɨn dakon mɨŋatni asak?”
Yaŋba Jon da kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda paba pɨgɨkni bamorɨ kaŋ, mɨnini amɨn do kɨnda ɨmjak. Ae japni taŋ ɨmaŋ amɨnyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn asak.”
“Gen tebano uŋun yaŋ: nak da ji do but dasi galak taŋ damɨsat, jiyo yaŋ gɨn dɨsikon notji do but dasi galak taŋ yomɨŋ yomɨŋ ani.
Amɨn morapmɨ da bɨsap madepmon yaŋsi nayɨkdaŋ, ‘Amɨn Tagɨnin, nin gak da manon kombɨ gen yagɨmaŋ, ae koŋ yolgɨmaŋ, ae pi madep agɨmaŋ.’
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Ni bɨsapmon sotni yɨpmaŋ dek?” Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Apma gɨldat tobɨl do 1 kilok gɨptɨmɨ kɨndap sogɨt uŋun yawokgɨt.”
Mani Piŋkop dakon gen da ɨreŋtaŋ kokupmɨ kokupmɨ kɨgɨt.
Gaga da dabɨlon kɨndap kwɨk tosok uŋun do dɨma nandaŋek notgo da dabɨlon jɨmjɨm nido kosol?
“Yaŋ yoyɨŋek Amɨn Madep uŋun da tobɨl gwandeŋ tet do amɨn yaŋ yoyɨsak, ‘Jobɨt pabi kabɨ ji aŋgwikon kɨŋek kɨndapmon pɨgɨt. Uŋun kɨndap uŋun Sunduk gat aŋelo kabɨni gat uŋun do aŋnoman abi, uŋun kɨmot kɨmorɨ mɨni.
Aŋek Yesu yutnon wɨgakwan amɨn kabɨ madepsi aeni uŋudon muwukgwit. Muwugakwa Yesu gat paŋdetni gat jap noni dakon bɨkbɨk dɨma pɨsaŋ yomgut.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu da wasaŋek yo noman taŋ ɨmdaŋ uŋun do paŋdetni yoyɨŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak Jerusalem kokup papmon kɨŋek kɨla amɨn, ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn uŋun da yo yokwisi aŋ namɨŋek nɨkba kɨmotdɨsat. Aŋek gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan Piŋkop da aban pɨdokdɨsat.”
Kalɨpsi da wɨŋ abɨsok on ekwamaŋon kokup pap morap taŋ aŋaŋ kwaŋon Moses dakon gen yaŋ teŋteŋawit. Sabat bɨsap morapmon Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yutnon Moses dakon gen manjɨŋ manjɨŋ awit. Do yum but pɨso papia kɨnda yaŋ mandaŋ yomneŋ. Ji kokup kɨdat do paret abi uŋun dakon jap dɨma noni. Jap uŋuden Piŋkop da pɨndakban dɨma noknogɨ aŋ. Ae mɨŋat wɨliyo yumabi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ dɨmasi ani. Ae bɨt kɨlapyo si tɨpba kwoŋ gat ae yawiyo kɨsi dɨmasi noni.”
Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Dewit ae amɨn kabɨni jap do aŋek yo awit uŋun ji manjɨŋ nandaŋyo awit bo dɨma?
Jopa kokup papmon Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgut mɨŋat kɨnda egɨpgut mani Tabita. (Grik genon Dokas yaŋ iyɨwit.) Uŋun bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ aŋpak kɨlegɨsi aŋek yoni mɨni amɨn paŋpulugagɨt.
Mani Parisi amɨn da yaŋ yawit, “Koŋ dakon kɨla amɨn madep da tapmɨmon koŋ yoldak.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Bɨsit ani bɨsapmon yaŋ yoni: ‘Dat, gak dakon man telagɨ tosak. Amɨn Kɨla Agakgo yɨpbɨ ninon apjak.
Yaŋ aŋakwa Yesu da nandaŋ gadatni kaŋek amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Monjɨ, dɨwarɨgo yopmaŋ gamɨsat.”
Kɨlɨ jap noknok bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan kalɨp yaŋ yomgut amɨn yoyɨŋba opni do pi monjɨni yabekban kɨwit. Mani kɨŋ yoyɨŋba op do dɨma galak tawit.
“Mani babɨknin Moses dakon gen nandaŋ guramɨt do dɨma galak tawit. Geni maba kɨŋakwan burɨkon da Isip mɨktɨmon tobɨl kɨk do nandawit.
“Yaŋ yaŋban iyɨwit, ‘Amɨn tagɨ, uŋun amɨn moneŋ tabɨlni 10 kabɨ kɨlɨ tɨmak!’
Juda amɨn da Yesu abɨdaŋ Kaiapas dakon yut yɨpmaŋek gapman dakon amɨn madep da yutnon aŋkɨwit. Uŋun kɨlɨ wɨsa dagagɨt, do iyɨ gapman dakon amɨn madep da nagalon dɨma pɨgɨwit, nido pɨgɨneŋ kaŋ Piŋkop da dabɨlon kɨlek taŋek Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap noknoknin aŋsuŋ akdamaŋ yaŋ nandawit.
Pol gɨldat kapbɨ egek Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn yaŋ yoba apgwit. Abɨŋ muwugakwa yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Not kabɨ, nak nin dakon amɨn kabɨ bo ae babɨknin dakon aŋpak pabɨŋ yop do aŋek yo yokwi kɨnda dɨma agɨm. Mani amɨn da nak Jerusalem abɨdaŋ Rom amɨn da kɨsiron nepgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn burɨ wagɨl yokwi taŋban iyɨ dakon paba pɨgɨkni pudaŋek yagɨt, “Mibɨlni nandak do amɨn nido saŋbeŋek yoyɨno apni? Iyɨ Piŋkop kulabɨŋek ‘nak Piŋkop dakon Monji’ yaŋ yosok,
Yaŋba emat amɨn da kɨŋ amɨn bamot Yesu gat dapgwit dakon kandapni dapmaŋ jokgalgwit.
Gɨldat pɨgakwan pɨlɨndo koŋni toŋ amɨn morapmɨ paŋpaŋ apba gen yaŋek koŋ yol yomgut. Aŋek sot amɨn kɨsisi paŋmɨlɨp agɨt.
Jon nawa gen morapmɨ gat kɨsi amɨn dakon but pɨsoni do yoyɨgɨt. Yaŋ aŋek Gen Bin Tagɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋaŋ yomgut.
Yaŋba Yesu da burɨ yokwi taŋban yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Mɨŋat monjɨ yopba nagon apgut. Dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk yomni. Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun amɨn mɨŋat monjɨyo da tɨlagon ekwaŋ uŋuden amɨn dakon.
Jon telagɨ pakbi sogɨt bɨsapmon, pi agɨt uŋun Kwen Kokup dakon pi, bo amɨn dakon pi naŋ agɨt?”
Upbalap madep awit da dagaŋakwan Pol da paŋmuwukbi yaŋ yoban abɨŋ muwukba burɨ paŋteban aŋek galok gen yoyɨŋek Masadonia mɨktɨmon kɨgɨt.
Tɨlak gen uŋun yoyɨŋ mudaŋban paŋdet kabɨni da abɨŋ iyɨwit, “Mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyo madep gen yoyɨŋek tɨlak gen baŋ nido yoyɨsal?”
Yo yokwi kɨnda yaŋ ak, do tagɨ aŋatneŋ yaŋ kɨnda dɨma kawit. Mani Pailat da aŋakban kɨmotjak do madepsi yawit.
Nak uwal pɨdok pɨdokyo noman tosak do pɨgɨm. ‘Amɨn kɨnda da datni uwal aŋ ɨmdɨsak. Ae gwa kɨnda da meŋi uwal aŋ ɨmdɨsak. Aŋakwan mɨŋat kɨnda da namdi uwal aŋ ɨmdɨsak.
“Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn tagɨni da yo agɨt uŋun kaŋban amɨn nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi da arɨpmon agɨt, do yo kɨla agak pi amɨni yokwi uŋun do nandaban wukwan ɨmgut. On mɨktɨm dakon amɨn kabɨ da nandaŋ kokwin tagɨsi aŋek notni gat yumaŋ gwayek pi aŋ. Uŋun teŋteŋɨ dakon amɨn kabɨ yapmaŋgaŋ.
Kɨndap morap bamɨ dɨma pokgoŋ uŋun amɨn da mandaŋ kɨndapmon sosoŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban amɨn tagɨni da bupmɨ nandaŋ ɨmɨŋek goman madepni yɨpmaŋ ɨmɨŋakwan ɨsal kɨgɨt.
“Yaŋ iyɨko Pol yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak Sisa da geno nandɨsak do nandɨsat. Do ɨdon dam tebanon egapbo don nepbɨ Sisakon kɨkeŋ.’ Yaŋ yagɨt do dam tebanon sigɨn egɨpjak do yaŋ dagagɨm. Uŋudon egakwan Sisakon kɨgɨk dakon kosit aŋnoman aŋek don yɨpbo kɨsak.”
jɨgɨ morapni altaŋ ɨmgwit uŋun aŋpulugaŋek kukwaŋ ɨmgut. Aŋakwan Josep da Isip dakon kɨla amɨn madep Pero gat gen yagɨmal bɨsapmon Piŋkop da nandaŋ kokwin tagɨsi ɨmɨŋakwan kɨla amɨn madep da kaŋban tagɨsi agɨt. Yaŋ kagɨt do Isip mɨktɨm ae yutni dakon yo morap kɨla asak do yɨpgut.
Pailat da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat, ae kɨla amɨn gat, ae amɨn kɨsi yaŋ yoban opba
“Nido paŋdet kabɨgo babɨk dakon gen teban yapmaŋek kɨsirɨ dɨma sugaŋek jap noŋ?”
Yaŋ agɨt do Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgɨgɨt. Uŋudon Juda amɨn gat ae Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨkon amɨn Piŋkop gawak ɨmaŋ amɨn gat kɨsi egɨpgwit. Uŋun amɨn da Piŋkop dakon mibɨlɨ pakyaŋsi nandani do gen tebaisi yoyɨgɨt. Ae gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ maket tamokon paŋkɨ egek amɨn kɨŋ ap awit uŋun gat kɨsi yaŋ gɨn agɨt.
Juda amɨn Beria egɨpgwit uŋun amɨn tagɨsi. Aŋpakni da Juda amɨn Tesalonaika egɨpgwit uŋun yapgut. Pol dakon gen do galagɨsi nandaŋek gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Piŋkop dakon gen uŋun pakyaŋsi manjɨŋ nandawit. Manjɨŋ nandaŋek Pol da gen asi yosok bo suŋ yosok yaŋ do kokwin awit.
Yesu tagaŋek nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi taŋ ɨmgut, ae Piŋkop da galak taŋ ɨmɨŋakwan amɨnyo kɨsi da galak taŋ ɨmgwit.
Mani uŋun dakon aŋpak uŋun jikon dɨma tosak. Jikon da amɨn kɨnda amɨn tagɨ man pak do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn oman amɨnji egek amɨn tagɨ man pasak.
Banabas uŋun Sus yaŋ iyɨŋek Pol uŋun gen yogok amɨn do Emes yaŋ iyɨwit.
“Ji uŋun amɨn dakon mibɨlɨ amɨn dɨma yoyɨŋdetni do yaŋsop tebaisi yaŋ damgumaŋ. Mani ji sigɨn yoyɨŋ degakwa Jerusalem kokup pap amɨn kɨsi da ji dakon gen nandayɨŋ. Ae ji da nin do top kɨnda yaŋ yoŋ. Kɨla amɨn nin da Yesu aŋatno kɨmakgɨt, top yaŋ yaŋ nimaŋ.”
Yut kɨndakon wɨgek mibɨltok yaŋ yoyɨni, ‘On yut amɨn butji yaworɨ tosak.’
Kɨmakban uŋun da buŋon nani da sakwabat paŋek yaŋ gɨn monji mɨni egɨ kɨmakgɨt. Ae uŋun da buŋon nani yaŋ gɨn agɨt.
Tap wakga dakon pi monjɨ uŋun niaŋ aŋek tap wakga tayaŋgok yɨpmaŋ degek gɨptɨmnin paŋkutnoneŋ yaŋon da kosit wusɨk awit. Do bot monɨŋɨ wɨtdalba pɨgakwan kɨrat madep tap wakga abɨdaŋban akgaŋ uŋun tomnikon da yopno pɨgɨni yaŋ top yoyɨwit.
Bo Dat nagon egakwan nak Daron egɨsat uŋun nandabɨ bamɨ dɨma ak? Nak gen dayɨt uŋun naga da nandak nandagon da dɨma dayɨt. Dat nagon egɨsak uŋun da pini asak.
Muwut muwut yutnikon ae jap noknok bɨsap madepmon amɨn mani toŋ da yɨyɨt tamokon yɨt do galak toŋ.
Kɨŋ egɨ don wain sop pakpak bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan pi monjɨni yabekban wain bamɨ tɨmɨk paŋopni do kɨwit.
Yoyɨŋban kokup pap yɨpmaŋek Yesukon apgwit.
Nak naga uŋun amɨn dɨma nandaŋ ɨmgum. Mani Piŋkop da nak telagɨ pakbi soŋ yobeŋ do yabegek yaŋ nayɨgɨt, ‘Gak kaŋbɨ Telagɨ Wup amɨn kɨnda da kwenon pɨŋ yɨkban kaŋ yaŋ nandaki, uŋun amɨn da amɨn Telagɨ Wup naŋ telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomdɨsak.’
Kosiron kɨŋakwa amɨn kɨnda da iyɨgɨt, “Dukwan dukwan agɨpbi uŋun nak gol awɨlgeŋ gɨn.”
Kɨŋ uŋudon gɨldat 40 japmɨ mɨni egek jap do madepsi agɨt. Aŋakwan Sunduk da aŋkewalgɨt.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae kɨla amɨn da “Tɨlak gen uŋun nin do yosok” yaŋ nandaŋek Yesu abɨdok do nandawit. Mani mɨŋat amɨn do pasalek yɨpba si kɨgɨt.
Yɨpmaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: ‘Uŋun da aŋeloni yoyɨŋban kɨlago tagɨsi ani. Ae kandapgo tɨpmon dɨma gɨtni yaŋ do aŋelo da gak kɨsit da kendak abɨŋ gepni.’ Gen yaŋ tosok, do gak asi Piŋkop dakon Monji kaŋ, gak amon mibɨlɨkon paŋ ma.”
Yaŋ yaŋek monjɨ uŋun abɨdaŋ ɨlɨk pigaga da waŋga aŋaŋ abɨgɨ aŋakba kɨmakgɨt.
Gɨldat 7 kabɨ mudaŋakwa paŋdet kabɨ ae notni Tomas gat kɨsi yutnon muwugek yoma beŋgan awit. Mani Yesu abɨŋ bɨkbɨk nikon altaŋban kawit. Altaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Butji yaworɨ tosak.”
Satu wasok aba mudaŋban mɨktɨmon pabɨŋ yɨgek kɨla aŋek kaŋ egɨpgwit.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jikon bret niaŋ da toŋ?” Yaŋban iyɨwit, “7 kabɨ.”
Yo uŋun dɨma altaŋakwa gen uŋun kɨlɨ dayɨt. Do don yo uŋun bamɨ noman taŋakwa yaŋsi nandaŋ gadani, Nak Naga Uŋun Amɨn.
Waŋga jomaŋ agakwa Pailat da pɨŋ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji on amɨn mibɨlɨ nido gen yaŋ ɨmeŋ?”
Nandani. Jap nosok amɨn da mibɨltok amɨn bo jap pɨlɨkdak amɨn da mibɨltok amɨn? Jap naŋek yɨkdak amɨn uŋun da mibɨltok amɨn asak. Mani nak ji da binapmon oman monjɨsi egɨsat.
Sunduk da paŋkewal morap uŋun aŋ mudaŋek ae bɨsap kɨndakon don aŋkewalgeŋ yaŋ nandaŋek Yesu yɨpmaŋ kɨgɨt.
Yesu abɨdawit amɨn uŋun da Yesu abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da yutnon wɨgɨwit. Uŋun yutnon mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet ae kɨla amɨn kɨsi muwuk egɨpgwit.
Emat amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da obɨŋ Pol abɨdaŋek nap teban bamorɨ baŋ Pol abɨsɨni do yoyɨgɨt. Aŋek amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On namɨn amɨn kɨnda? Ae ninaŋ agɨt?”
Amɨn morap mɨrak paŋek yɨkgwit uŋun nandak nandakni ae kobogɨ bamɨsi yagɨt uŋun do nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
“Ji yo dɨwarɨ dɨ dɨma paŋek kɨni, wɨn kɨrɨŋ baŋgɨn pabɨdaŋek kɨni. Jap bo yɨk bo moneŋyo dɨma paŋek kɨni.
Yaŋban uŋudon gɨn Josep uŋun kalbi monjɨ ŋakŋak gat meŋi gat tɨmɨkban Isip kɨk do kosit wasawit.
Yaŋban Mata da iyɨgɨt, “Asi, mibɨ gɨldaron pɨdot pɨdot bɨsap madepmon don pɨdokdɨsak yaŋ nandɨsat.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon Pita da abɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, notno kɨnda da yokwi aŋnaban kosirɨ niaŋ da yokwini yopmaŋ ɨbeŋ? Kosirɨ 7 kabɨ bo niaŋ?”
Do ji genji dɨ yaŋ paŋmɨlɨp ak do nandaŋ kaŋ, gen kokwin muwut muwut bɨsapmon tagɨ yaŋ paŋmɨlɨp ani.
Mani uŋun kokup papmon amɨn kabi bamorɨ pudaŋ kɨwit. Kabi kɨnda Juda amɨn gat akgwit, ae kabi kɨnda yabekbi bamot gat akgwit.
“Yaŋ yoyɨŋban uŋun amɨn kabɨ kobogɨ yokwisi dagok dagogɨ mɨni pakdaŋ. Mani kɨlegɨ amɨn kabɨ uŋun da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni uŋudon kɨkdaŋ.”
Kɨlɨ Saimon Pita da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gak dukon kɨkdɨsal?” Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak da kokup kɨkdɨsat uŋudon abɨsok gak arɨpmɨ dɨma noldɨsal. Mani don nak noldɨsal.”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban Pailat da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat, ae mɨŋat amɨn morap egɨpgwit yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak on amɨn dakon yokwini kɨnda dɨma kosot.”
Iyɨŋakwan uŋudon gɨn Elisabet monjɨ burɨgwan yɨkgɨt uŋun wɨgɨ mok agɨt. Aŋakwan Elisabet Telagɨ Wup da burɨkon pɨgɨ tugaŋban
Amɨn kɨnda da ‘Donki nido wɨtdalgamal?’ yaŋ dayɨŋban kaŋ, yaŋ iyɨnjil, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ da pisok kɨnda ak do aŋek yosok.’ ”
Yɨgakwan amɨn da “Yesu Nasaret amɨn obɨsak” yaŋ yaŋba nandaŋek gen madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yagɨt, “Yesu, Dewit Dakon Monji, bupmɨ nandaŋ nam!”
“Yaŋ yaŋban kɨlegɨ kabɨ da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨni, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ, ni bɨsapmon jap do abɨ gandaŋek jap gamgumaŋ, ae ni bɨsapmon pakbi do asal yaŋ gandaŋek pakbi gamgumaŋ?
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Mani ji dɨsi nak do namɨn yaŋ yoŋ?” Yaŋban Pita da aŋtobɨlek iyɨgɨt, “Gak Kristo, Piŋkop da yabekban apgul.”
Uŋun gɨldaron gɨn Sadyusi amɨn dɨwarɨ da Yesukon apgwit. (Sadyusi amɨn kabɨ amɨn kɨmakbi dɨma pɨdoŋ yaŋ nandaŋ.) Abɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit,
Mani Yesu da yabekbini yoyɨgɨt, “Dɨsi jap yomgut.” Yoyɨŋban yawit, “Nin japnin morapmɨ dɨma. Bret 5 kabɨ gat ae tap kɨlap bamorɨ gat gɨn. Nin kɨŋ on mɨŋat amɨn morap do jap moneŋ baŋ si yumneŋ do nandɨsal?”
Nin tap wakga abɨdaŋek Itali mɨktɨmon kɨneŋ do yaŋ aŋteban awit. Aŋek Pol gat ae dam tebanon amɨn dɨ gat tɨmɨk emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn da kɨsiron yopgwit. Kɨla amɨn uŋun mani Julius. Uŋun Sisa Dakon Emat Amɨn Kabɨkon nani kɨnda.
Amɨn tagɨ uŋun kalbi binap bo wɨsa dagokdosi abɨŋ pɨndakban tagap taŋek egɨpni kaŋ tagɨsi.
Jap noknok bɨsapmon oman monjɨni kɨnda yabekban amɨn yaŋ yomgut uŋun yoyɨk do kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Yo morap kɨlɨ paŋkosit abi, do ji tagɨ opni.’
Uŋun mastat yet yombem. Mastat dakon yerɨ uŋun jap yet kɨsi morap dakon pɨŋbi, monɨŋɨsisok.
Yesu Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut yɨpmaŋek Saimon da yutnon kɨgɨt. Saimon dakon yopmi sot aŋek gɨptɨmni kɨndapmɨ sogɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan Yesu da aŋpulugosak do iyɨwit.
Aŋakwa pabɨŋ yɨgek paŋdetni 12 kabɨ yoyɨŋban apba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda mibɨltok amɨn ak do nandɨsak kaŋ, buŋonsi agek amɨn morap dakon oman amɨn egɨpjak.”
Ji Piŋkop dakon gen teban yɨpmaŋek babɨkji dakon gen paŋteban aŋek paŋ ekwaŋ.”
“Yaŋ yoyɨŋek egɨ pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo pi ami da kɨŋ pi monjɨ dakon kɨla amɨn yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Pi monjɨ yaŋ paŋmuwugek moneŋni yobi. Buŋonsi abeŋ uŋudon da wasaŋek yomɨŋaki wɨgɨ mibɨltok abeŋ uŋudon dagosak.’
Yaŋ aŋek pakgwit da Sonda wɨsa dagokdo tɨp kɨnamon kɨk do kɨŋakwa gɨldat wɨgɨt.
“Saion kokup pap amɨn do gen yaŋ yoyɨki, ‘Kabɨt, kɨla amɨn madepgo abɨsak. Burɨ maŋbi da donki da kwenon yɨgek abɨsak. Donki gɨmoŋɨ da kwenon yɨgek abɨsak.’ ”
Amɨn uŋun dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit, do Yesu uŋudon wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ morapmɨ dɨma agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋakwan tɨp madep aba kɨŋakwan Yesu kwen sɨŋtaŋban wɨgakwan yaŋ yagɨt, “Dat, gak bɨsitno kɨlɨ nandal, do ya yaŋ gayɨsat.
Jap naŋ mudaŋek Yesu da Saimon Pita yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, Jon dakon monji, gak nak do but dasi galak taŋ namɨŋ kɨmagek on amɨn kabɨ da but dasi galak taŋ namaŋ uŋun yapmaŋdal, ma?” Yaŋban Pita da yagɨt, “Asi, Amɨn Tagɨ, gaga nandɨsal. Nak but dasi galak taŋ gamɨsat.” Yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Sipsip monɨŋ kabɨno upmokgi.”
Uŋun kokupmon amɨn da kaŋba Pol da kɨsiron tuŋon amɨn uŋun telɨŋ telɨŋ aban kawit. Yaŋ kaŋek iyɨ gɨn notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yawit, “Koni, on amɨn uŋun amɨn kɨnda aŋakban kɨmakgɨt. Tap kaga pɨgɨ dɨma kuŋwak, mani abɨsok kobogɨ yomyom piŋkop da dɨma egɨpjak do nandɨsak, do kobogɨ ɨmɨsak.”
Pita yaŋ yaŋban amɨn muwuk yɨkgwit kɨsi tayaŋgok yɨgek Pol gat Banabas gat do mɨrak yopgwit. Mɨrak yopmaŋakwa Piŋkop da paŋpulugaŋakwan Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨkon wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ agɨmal uŋun do yoyɨgɨmal.
Mani egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨnikon kɨgɨk dakon wigat gat ae kositni uŋun gɨtnisi, uŋudon kɨgɨk dakon pini jɨgɨsi. Amɨn kaloŋ kaloŋ dagɨn wigat uŋun kaŋ kwoŋ.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Dat, kundu ae mɨktɨm dakon Amɨn Tagɨ, amɨn dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm dakon nandak nandakni uŋun wukwisi, mani iyɨ do nandaba wɨgɨsak, do uŋuden amɨn do gen bamɨ morap si paŋkɨsɨbɨsal. Aŋek amɨn monɨŋɨ da tɨlagon ekwaŋ amɨn, uŋun do yolɨsal.
Yolakwal Yesu da tobɨl pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Yo ninaŋ wɨsamal?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨgɨmal, “Rabai, gak dukon egɨsal?” (“Rabai” uŋun gen dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun “Yoyɨŋdet.”)
Meŋji datji, ae padɨk padɨkji, ae yawi dɨwatji, ae notji uŋunyo kɨsi da ji uwal da kɨsiron depba ji kabɨkon dɨ si dɨkba kɨmotdaŋ.
Josep uŋun mɨktɨm tɨmni kɨnda amɨn do yomɨŋek moneŋ tɨmɨk paŋkɨ yabekbi kabɨ do yomgut.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Nak kɨlɨ dayɨko dɨma nandayɨŋ. Ae nido sigɨn nandak do yoŋ? Ji kɨsi paŋdetni egɨp do aŋek yoŋ, ma?”
Amɨn uŋun yoni morapmɨ taŋ ɨmgwit, do gen uŋun nandaŋ burɨ jɨk taŋban si kɨgɨt.
Pita gat Jon gat gen kokwin yutnon da pɨŋ dabɨni kabɨkon kɨgɨmal. Kɨŋek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae kɨla amɨn gat da gen morap yoyɨwit uŋun kɨsi yoyɨŋ mudagɨmal.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, nak wain ae dɨma naŋek egɨ wɨgɨ Datno da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan don ji gat wain kalugɨ noneŋ.”
Aŋek samɨni kabɨ bɨkbɨk ninon ekwaŋ. Yo morap uŋun dukon tɨmɨkgɨt?”
Pailat da Yesu tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋatni do emat amɨn da kɨsiron yɨpban abɨdaŋ aŋkɨwit.
Pita gat Jon gat da amɨn uŋun tebai kaŋek Pita da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak nit ninda!”
Yaŋban uŋudon gɨn mɨŋatjok pɨdaŋek kɨŋ ap aban kaŋek yaŋ kɨmakgwit. (Mɨŋatjok bɨlakni 12 kabɨ.)
Jon dam teban yutnon yɨpba yɨgakwan Yesu Galili Provinskon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ Piŋkop dakon Gen Bin Tagɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋaŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Yaŋ yaŋba Jon da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak amɨn pakbisi baŋ telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomɨsat, mani amɨn kɨnda ji da bɨkbɨgon akdak, uŋun amɨn ji dɨma nandaŋ ɨmaŋ.
Obip amɨn uŋun tobɨl mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat Parisi amɨn garon kwa yaŋ yoyɨwit, “Ji nido uŋun amɨn dɨma abɨdaŋ aweŋ?”
Yaŋ yaŋakwa Pita yo kagɨt uŋun do but morap sigɨn nandaŋek yɨgakwan Telagɨ Wup da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, amɨn kapbɨ gak wɨsaŋ.
Yaŋba Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn morap yokwi aŋ uŋun yokwi dakon oman monjɨni ekwaŋ.
Piŋkop da Israel amɨn kabɨ nin do Gen Bin Tagɨsi niyɨgɨt uŋun ji dɨsi nandaŋ. Geni kɨnda uŋun yaŋ: Yesu Kristo uŋun amɨn morap dakon Amɨn Tagɨ egɨsak. Yesu da pi aban Piŋkop gat but kaloŋ agɨmaŋ.
Kɨlɨ Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Mɨŋat gak nido takdal? Gak namɨn naŋ wɨsɨsal?” Maria da pikaga uŋun dakon pi monjɨ kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, gak da bumjot aŋkɨl kaŋ, dukwan yɨpmal nayɨŋbɨ kɨŋ abɨdaŋ aŋopbeŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋban mɨŋat da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, uŋun pakbi nam. Nabɨ naŋek pakbi do dɨma akeŋ. Aŋek buŋon pakbi kolek do ɨdon saŋbeŋek dɨma apbeŋ.”
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Yesu, mani kɨnda Kristo yaŋ yoŋ, uŋun do ninaŋ aŋ ɨbeŋ?” Yaŋ yaŋban amɨn kɨsi da yaŋ yawit, “Tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotjak!”
Mani gen bamɨ paŋek egɨsak amɨn uŋun teŋteŋɨkon abɨsak. Abɨŋek teŋteŋɨkon egakwan amɨn da kaŋba Piŋkop da aŋpulugaŋban aŋpak tagɨsi asak.”
pɨdaŋ Yesu yolba kokup da waŋga pɨgɨgɨt. Kokup uŋun ɨleŋon tagɨt, do tɨpdomon maba pɨgɨsak do aŋkɨwit.
Eni kɨmagakwan sakwabat egakwan bɨlakni 84 agɨt. Ana uŋun telagɨ yut dɨma yɨpmaŋ dekgɨt. Jap kelek egek bɨsit pi aŋek kalbi ae gɨldat kalba Piŋkop gawak ɨmɨŋek egɨpgut.
Yaŋ aban uŋun mɨktɨm tɨmon sot amɨn dɨwarɨ kɨsisi apba paŋmɨlɨp agɨt.
Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Gen teban papiajikon Piŋkop dakon gen kɨnda yaŋ tosok: ‘Nak yaŋ dayɨsat, ji uŋun piŋkop.’
Yaŋ aŋek Pisidia mɨktɨm naŋ kɨŋek Pampilia mɨktɨmon kɨŋ altagɨmal.
“Aba, Dat, gak da yo morap tagɨ aki. Do nak da kwenon jɨgɨ apdɨsak uŋun kukwoki do nandɨsat. Mani nak dakon galaktok dɨma yolgi, gaga dakon galaktok uŋun gɨn yolgi.”
Pol Atens egek Timoti gat Sailas gat do jomjom aŋek egɨpgut. Egek uŋun kokup papmon kokup kɨdat dakon wup morapmɨsi pɨndagek burɨ yokwisi agɨt.
Gen uŋun yaŋ yaŋek Galili Provinskon sigɨn egɨpgut.
Nin amɨn notnin dakon yokwini yopmaŋgamaŋ. Uŋudeŋ gɨn yokwinin wɨrɨrɨk nibi.
Yolek amɨn wuda tebani toŋ kɨnda da Yesukon kɨŋ ŋwakbeŋ aŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, Piŋkop da dabɨlon kɨlek tokeŋ do nandɨsal kaŋ, tagɨ aŋmɨlɨp abɨ kɨlek tokeŋ.”
Wɨgɨ yut uŋun dakon ami yaŋ iyɨnjil, ‘Yoyɨŋdet da yaŋ yosok, “Nak gat paŋdetnoni gat da Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap noneŋ dakon yut burɨ dukwan tosok?” ’
dam tebanon kɨŋ Jon dakon busuŋɨ mandaŋ dagawit.
Mani ji dabɨlji da tagɨ pɨndakgaŋ, ae mɨrakji da tagɨ nandaŋ, do ji kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ekwaŋ.
Mani uŋun amɨn kabɨkon dɨwarɨ uŋun Saiprus ae Sairini kokupmon nani uŋun da Antiok kɨwit. Kɨŋ Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu dakon Gen Bin Tagɨsi Grik amɨn kɨsi do yoyɨwit.
Wɨsa dɨma dagaŋakwan Yesu pɨlisisok pɨdaŋ yut yɨpmaŋek mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon paŋkɨ egek bɨsit pi agɨt.
Piŋkop da papiakon gen toŋ uŋun da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni nimaŋ ji yaŋ nandaŋ. Yaŋdo, ji pini tebaisi aŋek manjɨŋek nandaŋ kokwinɨk mudoŋ. Uŋun papia da nak do yaŋkwok asak,
Abɨsok teŋteŋɨ ji gat egakwan gɨn egɨp egɨpji teŋteŋɨkon tosok yaŋsi nandaŋek teŋteŋɨ dakon monjɨni dagoni.” Yesu gen uŋun yoyɨŋ mudaŋek dɨma koni do yopmaŋ kɨŋ pasɨlɨkon egɨpgut.
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Kɨnda nak gat jap ɨdapmon kɨsitnit kaloŋɨ yɨpmaŋgamak, uŋun amɨn da nak uwalno da kɨsiron nepdɨsak.
“Amɨn kɨnda meŋi datniyo do but dasi galak taŋ yomɨsak uŋun yapmaŋek nak do wukwisi yaŋ dɨma nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn nak dakon notno dɨma. Ae amɨn kɨnda monji bo ae gwi do but dasi galak taŋ yomɨsak uŋun yapmaŋek nak do wukwisi yaŋ dɨma nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn nak dakon notno dɨma.
Yaŋ aban kaŋek pi monjɨ mibɨltok apgwit uŋun nin da moneŋ madep tɨmɨtdamaŋ yaŋ nandawit. Mani dɨma, kɨsi morap moneŋ 1 danari gɨn tɨmɨk tɨmɨk awit.
Ae Piŋkop dakon gen kɨnda gat yaŋ tosok: “Amɨn da gɨptɨmɨ sugawit uŋun kokdaŋ.”
Gak jap noknok kɨnda abi kaŋ, yoni mɨni amɨn, ae gɨptɨmɨ yokwi taŋbi, ae kandap yokwi ae dabɨlɨ mɨni amɨn baŋgɨn yaŋ yobi.
Yesu yaŋ aŋek aeni pakbi ɨdap ɨleŋɨkon pɨgɨgɨt. Pɨgakwan amɨn morapmɨ yol aŋaŋ uŋudon kwa Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt.
Sisa Ogastus da gen teban yaŋ yɨpgut, do amɨn kɨsisi mani mandani do kokupni kokupni kɨŋ mudawit.
Egɨpgumaŋ dakon bɨsap mudaŋakwan Yesu dakon paŋdetni gat ae mɨŋat monjɨyoni gat kɨsi kokup pap yɨpmaŋ degek tap kɨdɨpmɨŋon pɨgɨgɨmaŋ. Pɨgɨ uŋudon ŋwakbeŋ aŋek bɨsit agɨmaŋ.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda pakbi kɨlɨ sogɨt kaŋ, uŋun amɨn kandapni baŋgɨn sugosak. Yaŋ aban gɨptɨmni kɨsi kɨlegɨsi akdaŋ. Ji kɨlɨ kɨlek tawit. Mani ji kɨsi do dɨma yosot.”
Kundu gat mɨktɨm gat pasɨldamal, mani nak dakon gen uŋun dɨmasi pasɨldɨsak.”
Yaŋban Pol da yagɨt, “Kɨla amɨn madep Pestus, nak but upbal dɨma asat. Nandak nandakno tagɨsi taŋakwan gen bamɨ yosot.
Bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu kokup pap kɨndakon egakwan amɨn wuda tebani toŋ kɨnda egɨpgut. Uŋun da Yesu kaŋek ŋwakbeŋ aŋ ɨmɨŋek mɨktɨmon gawagek Yesu bɨsit tebai iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, Piŋkop da dabɨlon kɨlek tokeŋ do nandɨsal kaŋ, tagɨ aŋmɨlɨp abɨ kɨlek tokeŋ.”
Datgo da amɨn do bupmɨ nandɨsak, do jiyo yaŋ gɨn amɨn do bupmɨ nandani.”
Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdet, gak gen bamɨ yogok amɨn yaŋ nandamaŋ. Gak amɨn do dɨma pasoldol. Amɨn mani toŋ ae amɨn mani mɨni uŋun kɨsi Piŋkop dakon aŋpak yoyɨŋ dek mudosol. Gak niaŋ nandɨsal? Sisa do moneŋ ɨmno tagɨ asak bo dɨma? Ɨmneŋ bo dɨma?”
Yaŋban Pita gat ae paŋdet kɨnda uŋun gat kɨmakbi tamokon kɨgɨmal.
Wɨsa dagokdosi Yesu amɨn dɨma egɨpgwit tɨm kɨndakon kɨgɨt. Aŋakwan amɨn da wusɨŋ aŋalon aŋek dɨma yopmaŋ kɨsak do nandaŋek abɨdok do awit.
Yaŋ yaŋban ae amɨn kɨnda da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, gol do nandɨsat, mani nandaŋ namɨŋaki kɨŋ gwakno galok gen yoyɨŋek don abɨŋ golgeŋ.”
Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Asisi gayɨsat, gak abɨsok nak gat Paradais kon egɨpdamak.”
Nak yaŋ dayɨsat, jap on ae dɨma nokeŋ. Yaŋ aŋapbo wɨgɨ on jap dakon mibɨlɨsi Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak kagagwan bamɨ don noman tokdɨsak.”
Yaŋ aba yokwi iyɨkon gɨn tosok yaŋ nandani do kandapnikon kɨmbabaŋ tawit uŋun tɨdaŋbal kɨŋakwa Ikoniam kokup papmon kɨgɨmal.
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Yaŋ kaŋ nido Telagɨ Wup da Dewit aŋpulugaŋakwan Kristo do ‘Amɨn Tagɨ’ yaŋ iyɨgɨt? Dewit uŋun yaŋ yagɨt:
Yo morap pasɨlɨ toŋ uŋun don nomansi altaŋ mudokdaŋ. Ae yo morap wutjɨŋbi da toŋ uŋun noman taŋ mudaŋakwa amɨn da pɨndak nandaŋyo akdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban iyɨgɨmal, “Gak Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmɨŋaki Piŋkop da gak gat ae yutgokon amɨn ekwaŋ gat kɨsi yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨtjak.”
Aŋek Juda amɨn Grik gen yawit uŋun gat gen emat aŋ aŋ awit. Aŋek Sol si aŋakba kɨmotjak do nandawit.
Nak yabekban pɨgɨm amɨn uŋun nak gat ekwamak. Bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ nak Dat dakon galaktok yoldat, do dɨma nepmaŋ dekdak.”
Amɨn da Yesu do nandak nandak yaŋ paŋek waseŋ kɨ kabi bamorɨ awit.
Iyɨŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Monjɨsok kɨnda mɨŋat pak do asak bɨsapmon monjɨsok notni gat kɨsi ekwaŋ, do bupmɨ dɨma nandaŋ. Mani don monji uŋun gwayeŋ aŋaŋ kɨŋakwa notni uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek ekwaŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋbal Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Jil abɨŋ konjil.” Yaŋ yaŋban kɨŋ yutni kagɨmal. Kaŋek pɨlɨndo 4 kilok agɨt do Yesu gat egɨpgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da aeni dabɨlɨkon kɨsirɨ wɨtjɨgɨt. Yaŋ aban dabɨlɨ wagɨl kɨlek taŋban yo morap tagɨ pɨndakgɨt.
Yaŋdo, ji kɨŋ kosit papmon agek amɨn pɨndak yoyɨŋba apba jap pakbiyo aneŋ.’
Aŋkɨ wasaŋek gen yaŋ ɨmɨŋek yawit, “On amɨn da Israel amɨn kabɨ nin paŋupbal aŋek nin da Sisa do takis dɨma ɨmneŋ do yosok. Ae iyɨ do nak kɨla amɨn madep kɨnda, nak Kristo yaŋ yosok.”
Yaŋ yaŋba nandaŋek Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon obip amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ kɨsi but morap nandaŋek yawit, “Uŋun amɨn dukon keŋ?”
Yaŋ aba yoyɨgɨt, “Ji dɨwarɨ koleŋ paŋpaŋ jap noknok kɨla amɨnon paŋkɨt.” Yoyɨŋban paŋkɨ ɨmgwit.
Aŋek amɨn kɨlek tagɨt uŋun kɨsi akba pɨndagek gen dɨ aeni yoyɨk do dɨma nandawit.
“Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat ae Parisi amɨn gat da kalɨp Moses da man madepni gat yɨgek gen teban yoyɨŋ dekgɨt uŋudeŋ gɨn dayɨŋ dekgaŋ.
Ji dɨsi do ‘Nin Abraham dakon babɨkni’ yaŋ dɨma yoni. Yaŋsi dayɨsat, Piŋkop da yaŋban on tɨp kabɨ da Abraham dakon babɨkni tagɨ dagoni. Ji uŋun Abrahamon da altawit uŋun da yo madep dɨma asak.
“Mani uŋun da yaŋ dayɨkdɨsak, ‘Nak asisi dayɨsat, nak dɨma nandaŋ damɨsat. Ji dukon nani uŋun dɨma nandɨsat. Yokwi pakpak ji kɨsisi nepmaŋ dek kɨt!’
Do ji bamɨ pakpak dakon Amɨn Tagɨni bɨsit iyɨŋba pi amɨn paŋalon aŋ yopban pinikon kɨŋ jap paŋ paŋmuwutni.”
Aŋakba kɨmagakwan Sol da yo tagɨsi kɨnda naŋ aŋ yaŋ pɨndakgɨt. Stiwen aŋagakwa Piŋkop aŋtelak aŋek egɨpgwit amɨn dɨ da Stiwen do bupmɨ kunamyo madepsi aŋek bumjotni aŋkɨ yɨpgwit. Uŋun gɨldaron da wasaŋek Piŋkop dakon gen dakon uwalni da paŋmuwukbi Jerusalem egɨpgwit uŋun paŋupbal ak do pi madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋek paŋmuwukbi yolba waseŋ kɨ Judia tetgɨn do ae Samaria tetgɨn do kɨŋ kɨŋ awit. Kɨŋakwa yabekbi kabɨ dagɨn Jerusalem egɨpgwit.
Aŋakwan koŋ amɨn uŋun yɨpmaŋ degek wɨŋ abɨgɨ bɨt da butgwan pɨgɨwit. Pɨgakwa bɨt uŋun tɨmtɨm yaŋek obandom naŋ pɨgɨ pakbi ɨdapgwan pɨgek pakbi naŋ kɨmakgwit.
Yesu kɨmoron da pɨdaŋ paŋdet kabɨnikon on altaŋ yomgut uŋun da aban kosirɨ kapbɨ agɨt.
Uŋun bɨsapmon kombɨ amɨn mɨŋat pelaŋsi kɨnda egɨpgut, mani Ana. Uŋun Panuel, Ase da kabɨkon nani dakon gwi. Uŋun kalɨp amɨn paban egakwal bɨlak 7 kabɨ mudaŋakwan eni kɨmakgɨt.
Wigat kɨla amɨn da uŋun amɨn do yoma wɨtdal ɨban pɨgɨsak. Pɨgɨ sipsipni kaloŋ kaloŋ dakon mani yaŋban tegɨ nandaŋakwa mibɨltaŋ yoban waŋga kwaŋ.
(Paŋdetni jap yum do kokup papmon kɨlɨ kɨwit.)
Mani Piŋkop da kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdagɨt.
Josep uŋun Galili provinskon, Nasaret kokupmon egɨpgut. Mani Dewit da yawi dɨwaron da altagɨt, do Judia provinskon, Dewit dakon kokup Betlehem uŋudon kɨgɨt.
Babɨknin Abraham yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Nak asisi uwalji da kɨsiron baŋ pulugaŋ depbo pasol pasolɨ mɨni egek oman amɨno egɨpdaŋ.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Jon abɨŋek jap morapmɨ dɨma nagɨt, ae wain dɨma nagɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan, ‘Koŋni toŋ’ yaŋ yawit.
Yaŋ aŋakwa gak tapmɨmgo madep do kalɨp yo don altoni do nandabɨ teban tagɨt uŋun noman tawit.
Yaŋ tɨdaŋek ɨmal dubakni ɨlɨk maba kɨŋakwa kɨmbabaŋ tɨmɨk maba kwen wɨgɨwit.
Mani amɨn dɨwarɨ da gak do yaŋ yoyɨwit, ‘Pol da Juda amɨn Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ da bɨkbɨgon ekwaŋ uŋun Moses dakon gen teban dɨma guramɨtni do yoyɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨsak, “Ji monjisi dakon gɨptɨm dɨma mandani. Ae Juda amɨn dakon aŋpak dɨma yolni.” ’
Yaŋ aŋek iyɨwit, “Gak amɨn gɨptɨmni dɨma mandabi da yutnon kwi uŋun gat jap nido nawit?”
Mani amɨn morapmɨ da uŋudon kwaŋ yaŋ pɨndak nandaŋyo awit. Yaŋ nandaŋek kokup morapni yopmaŋ yopmaŋ aŋek amɨn morapmɨ mɨktɨm kosit tɨmtɨm yaŋek uŋun da kalɨp kɨŋ altawit.
Yaŋ yaŋek tobɨl paŋdetni kapbɨ egɨpgwiron kɨŋ pɨndakban dɨpmɨn pakgwit. Pɨndagek Pita yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, gak dɨpmɨn pokdol, ma? Bɨsap awa kaloŋɨ da arɨpmon gɨn nak gat Piŋkop do nandaŋek dɨma egɨpneŋ?
Ɨreŋtaŋ egakwa kɨla amɨn madep kalugɨ kɨnda noman tagɨt. Uŋun amɨn da Josep dɨma nandaŋ ɨmgut.
Yaŋban nandaŋek Juda amɨn da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Datnin uŋun Abraham.” Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Ji asi Abraham dakon monjini tam, Abraham da iyɨ aŋpak agɨt uŋun baŋ abam.
Amɨn kɨnda jikon da mibɨltok amɨn egɨp do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn mɨŋat amɨn morap dakon oman amɨni egek mibɨltok amɨn tagɨ egɨpjak.
Jon da amɨn pakbi soŋ yomgut, mani gɨldat kabisok kɨnda egek Piŋkop da Telagɨ Wup soŋ damdɨsak.”
Ae amɨn morap kalugɨ egek nandaŋ gadaŋ namni uŋun amɨn wagɨl dɨma kɨmotdaŋ. Gen uŋun yosot uŋun nandabɨ bamɨ asak, bo dɨma?”
Aŋagek mibɨlɨ yaŋ do aŋakgamaŋ uŋun dakon but pɨso gen yaŋ mandawit, JUDA AMƗN DAKON KƗLA AMƗN MADEP.
Apban Piŋkop da Abraham iyɨ do mɨktɨm tɨmjok kɨnda dɨmasi ɨmgut. Mani Abraham gat yawi dɨwatni gat da on mɨktɨm don abɨdoni do yaŋ teban tok gen kɨnda yagɨt. Gen uŋun iyɨgɨt bɨsapmon Abraham monjɨ mɨni egɨpgut.
Mani Pol da obip amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Manit Rom gapmanon tosok. Do nidosi nit dakon mibɨlnit pakyaŋsi dɨma kokwinɨgek amɨn morapmɨ da dabɨlon nindapmaŋek dam teban yutnon nipmaŋ? Yaŋ ayɨŋ da abɨsok nit pasɨlɨkon da nipba kɨkdamak? Uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Amɨn madep uŋun da iyɨsi abɨŋ pulugaŋ nipba kɨndeŋ.”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji apjak bɨsapmon Kwen Kokup dakon tɨlɨmni gat ae aŋelo kabɨni gat abɨŋek kɨla amɨn madep yɨyɨt tamokon uŋudon yɨtdɨsak.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn dɨwarɨ Piŋkop da paŋpulugaŋakwan mɨŋat dɨma paŋek tagɨ egɨpni.
Amɨn kapmatjok akgwit da gen uŋun nandaŋek Pol yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak Piŋkop dakon mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn do yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmɨsal, ma?”
Gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋ egakwa Yesu tɨlak gen kɨnda yoyɨgɨt. Yesu uŋun Jerusalem kɨlɨ kɨŋ aŋkapmat agɨt, ae amɨn da Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Akdɨsak dakon bɨsap kɨlɨ uŋun kwaŋ tokdɨsak yaŋ nandawit do
Yaŋ iyɨŋba Yesu da pɨdaŋ agek mɨrɨm gat ae pakbi gat tebai yoyɨŋek yagɨt, “Yawokgɨl!” Yaŋban mɨrɨm yawogakwan pakbi wayɨŋ dɨmasi agɨt.
Yoyɨŋba amɨn kɨsisi Yesu kok do abɨŋ mudawit. Abɨŋ kaŋek mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋek kɨsak do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu Galili Provins yɨpmaŋek Jodan Pakbikon, Jon da telagɨ pakbi soŋ ɨmjak do opgut.
“Buŋon don mɨŋat kabɨ pakbi do kɨwit uŋun abɨŋ yawit, ‘Amɨn tagɨ, amɨn tagɨ, abɨŋ yoma wɨtdal nim!’
Nak asisi gayɨsat, nin yo si nandamaŋ uŋun do yomaŋ, ae yo si pɨndakgɨmaŋ uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋok amaŋ. Mani dayɨno ji gen uŋun tɨmɨt do dɨma galak toŋ.
Yesu gen sigɨn yaŋakwan amɨn kabɨ madep kɨnda apgwit. Paŋdet 12 kabɨkon da kɨnda mani Judas uŋun da mibɨltok aban apgwit. Uŋun da Yesu mandaŋ nok do kapmatjok apgut.
“Mani Parisi amɨn, awa! Ji jap tam galagɨsi pi kagasi toŋ uŋun paŋ kabi 10 kabɨ yopmaŋek uŋun kabɨkon baŋ kabi kɨndanaŋ Piŋkop do paret aŋ. Mani gen kokwin kɨlegɨ agak gat, ae Piŋkop do but dasi galak taŋ ɨmɨm uŋun ji dɨma aŋ. Aŋpak kɨlegɨ uŋun gat ae paretyo kɨsi ani kaŋ tagɨsi.
Yaŋ yaŋek japmɨ nandaŋek obip amɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Ji aŋakba tepmɨ nandaŋek gomano kɨsisi sopban don yɨpbo kɨsak.’ ”
Ae jobɨt tɨmɨtni do dayaŋ amɨn, uŋun Piŋkop da paŋpulugosak do bɨsit iyɨni. Ae yokwi aŋ damaŋ amɨn do bɨsit ani.
“Nandaki. Mɨŋat kɨnda amɨn gat dɨma pakbi kɨnda da monjɨ kwap awɨlek monjɨ wɨli kɨnda aŋalasak. Aŋalaŋban mani Emanuel yaŋ yoni.” (Emanuel dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun yaŋ: “Piŋkop nin gat egɨsak.”)
Mandaŋ dagaŋban Yesu da obip amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nak do kabo noknok kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋek emat agak sɨba ae kɨndap kɨrɨŋ tɨmɨgek nak abɨdok do abeŋ, ma?
Agakwa Telagɨ Wup da nak yaŋ nayɨgɨt, ‘Gak but bamot dɨma aŋek pɨgɨ uŋun gat kɨni.’ Yaŋ nayɨŋban pɨgapbo notno 6 kabɨ on akgamaŋ uŋun kɨsi buŋon nolba kɨŋ Konilias da yutnon wɨgɨgɨmaŋ.
Mani Sol (mani kɨnda Pol) uŋun Telagɨ Wup da burɨkon tugaŋban Elimas tebaisi kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Yesu uŋun Nasaret kokupmon kɨgɨt. Kalɨp uŋun kokupmon egek tagaŋ teban taŋek amɨn tagɨ agɨt. Sabat bɨsapmon Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgɨ wɨgɨ agɨt uŋudeŋ gɨn Sabat kɨndakon wɨgɨgɨt. Aŋek Piŋkop dakon gen manjɨk do pɨdaŋ akgɨt.
Kalɨpsigwan Piŋkop da kombɨ amɨn Jonakon tɨlak aban Niniwe kokup pap amɨn da asi Piŋkopmon da abɨk da asak yaŋ kawit. Uŋudeŋ gɨn yo Amɨn Dakon Monjikon noman taŋ ɨba apmiap amɨn da kaŋek asi Piŋkop da yabekban abɨk yaŋ kokdaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋban Pol Jerusalem dɨmasi kɨsak do nin gat ae amɨn egɨpgumaŋ gat kɨsi da aŋkutnaŋek tebaisi iyɨgɨmaŋ.
Mani telagɨ yut uŋun iyɨ dakon gɨptɨm do yagɨt.
Nak mɨktɨmon teŋteŋɨ da yaŋ apgum. Do nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namni amɨn uŋun pɨlɨn tukgwan dɨma egɨpdaŋ.
Mani padɨgɨgo kɨmoron da yaŋ abɨk, ae pasɨlbikon naŋ aŋalon amaŋ, do nin but kwaktok nandaŋek kɨsɨk kɨsɨk tagɨsi amaŋ.’ ”
“On amɨn yokwi morapmɨsi paŋalon aban komaŋ. On mɨktɨmon kokup kɨsi morapmon Juda amɨn dakon burɨ sugaŋban emat upbalapyo madepsi aŋ. Ae Juda amɨn nin nipmaŋ degek nandaŋ gadat ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda awit. Amɨn da uŋun kabɨ do Nasaret Amɨn yaŋ yoŋ. Uŋun amɨn kabɨ dakon mibɨltok amɨni oni akdak.
Aŋek kɨndɨrɨŋ kɨnda wagɨl mani toŋsi tomni wukwisi kɨnda kosok bɨsapmon kɨŋ yo kabɨni taŋ ɨmgwit uŋun kɨsisi amɨnon yumaŋ naŋek uŋun dakon moneŋɨ baŋ uŋun kɨndɨrɨŋ tagɨsi yumgut.”
Stiwen da gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek butjap madepsi nandaŋek mam nawit.
Wɨgakwan Pita yo uŋun kagɨt dakon mibɨlɨ niaŋsi yaŋ nandaŋek but morap agɨt. Yaŋ nandaŋek egakwan Konilias da amɨn yabekgɨt uŋun apgwit. Abɨŋ amɨn yoyɨŋba Saimon dakon yut yolɨŋba uŋun da yoma kagakon paŋkɨ akgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋek kɨŋ kaŋban sɨbɨt sɨbɨt wɨrɨrɨgek yo morap paŋkosit abi pɨndakdak.
Ji yaŋ aŋek babɨkji dakon yaŋ teban tok gen guramɨgek Piŋkop dakon gen maba kɨsak. Ae uŋun gɨn dɨma, yo morap dɨwarɨ kɨsi yaŋ gɨn aŋ.”
Aŋakwa mɨŋat dɨwarɨ dubagɨsogon da agek yo uŋun pɨndakgwit. Yesu Galili mɨktɨm yɨpmaŋ abɨŋakwan uŋun mɨŋat kabɨ da yol awɨlek oman aŋ ɨmɨŋek agɨpgwit.
“Yaŋban Abraham da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Moses gat ae kombɨ amɨn gat dakon gen dɨma nandani kaŋ, amɨn kɨnda kɨmoron da pɨdaŋban kaŋek nandaŋ gadat arɨpmɨ dɨma akdaŋ.’ ”
Amɨn kɨnda yut madep kɨnda ak do kaŋ, mibɨltok yɨgek moneŋni manjɨsak. Aŋek yut tagɨ aŋ mudogɨ bo dɨma uŋun dakon nandak nandak asak.
Amɨn da ji tɨmɨk paŋpaŋ gen pikon depni bɨsapmon dɨma pasolni. Ni gen baŋ yoyɨneŋ yaŋ dɨma nandani. Uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop da ni gen dayɨsak uŋun baŋ yoyɨni. Yaŋ aŋakwa ji dakon gen dɨma asak, uŋun Telagɨ Wup dakon gen asak.
Mɨrɨm gat tap gat da nin tebaisi ukwayɨkgɨmal, do wɨsa dagokdo tap wakga dakon pi monjɨ da yɨk morap maba tap kaga pɨgɨ mudawit.
Pol kɨŋ yut uŋun da maŋ wɨgɨgon altaŋakwan amɨn da Pol si aŋakba kɨmotjak do gwayan tebaisi awit. Yaŋ aba emat amɨn da pasalek Pol si kendak aŋaŋ wɨgɨwit.
“Niaŋ nandaŋ? Monjɨ bamoron da jɨt amɨn da datni dakon gen guramɨkgɨt?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Mibɨltok amɨn.” Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi yosot, takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn yokwi gat ae kosit oba mɨŋat gat da ji gwapmaŋek Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan mibɨltaŋ damɨŋek kwaŋ.
Yaŋban Saimon da iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn tagɨ, nin kalbi tap kɨlap sɨmɨl do pi madep aŋek tap kɨlap kɨnda dɨma ɨlɨgapdo wɨsa dagak. Mani gak dakon gen guramɨgek yɨk yum yopno pɨgɨni.”
Yaŋ nandaŋek amɨn morap tɨmtɨm yaŋek abɨŋ kaŋba amɨn uŋun Pita Jonyo tɨmɨkban akba pɨndakgwit. Tamo uŋun akgwit dakon mani uŋun Solomon dakon Yɨk Nandat Tamo.
Judas bret dɨwat uŋun abɨdaŋek uŋudon gɨn waŋga pɨgɨgɨt. Waŋga uŋun pɨlɨn tuk kɨlɨ agɨt.
Maria Makdala kokupmon nani gat ae Maria kɨnda gat tɨp kɨnam da kapmatjok yɨgek yo agɨt uŋun nomansi kagɨmal.
Yesu Lasarus da sot agɨt uŋun dakon geni nandaŋek kokup egɨpguron gɨldat bamorɨ gat egɨpgut.
Kɨŋ altaŋban wain pi dakon kɨla amɨn da uŋun pi monjɨ abɨdaŋ aŋagek bamɨ kɨnda dɨma ɨmɨŋek yɨpba kɨgɨt.
Kɨlek taŋban uŋudon gɨn Yesu da amɨn uŋun yabegek gen tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Gen uŋun yaŋba nandaŋek ɨmalni kukwaŋ yɨpmaŋek Yesukon opgut.
Yaŋ yaŋban mɨŋatjok uŋun dakon wupmɨ aeni tobɨl abɨŋ pɨgakwan uŋudon gɨn pɨdagɨt. Pɨdaŋakwan Yesu da jap dɨ ɨba nosak do yoyɨgɨt.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ amɨn da Gen Bin Tagɨsi yoyɨŋek mɨŋat on da yo ak uŋun dakon gen bin kɨsi yoyɨŋakwa nandakdaŋ. Aŋek uŋun mɨŋat dakon man bini dɨma pasɨldɨsak.”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek boron wɨgek pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda kɨwit.
Ae uŋun da buŋon Galili amɨn kɨnda mani Judas uŋun da noman tagɨt. Noman taŋ gapman da man manjɨwit bɨsapmon Judas da amɨn kabi kɨnda tɨmɨkban gapman gat emat wamgwit. Uŋun kɨsi aŋakba kɨmagakwan uŋun yolgwit amɨn tayɨŋɨgɨ kɨwit.
Koŋ uŋun Yesu da nandaŋ yoban bɨt da butgwan pɨgɨni do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat aeni Jerusalem kɨŋ altawit. Aŋek Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan pɨgɨ agɨpgut. Agakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae gen teban dakon yoyɨŋdet amɨn, ae kɨla amɨn Yesukon opgwit. Obɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit,
Yesu yaŋ yaŋek ae kɨnda gat yaŋ yagɨt, “Notnin Lasarus uŋun yum dɨpmɨni pokdok, do nak da kɨŋ aŋyolbo pɨdosak.”
Jon da gapman dakon kɨla amɨn madep Erot tebai kaŋ yagɨt, nido Erot da padɨge dakon mɨŋatni Erodias tuwɨl pagɨt, ae aŋpak yokwi dɨ kɨsi agɨt.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kaloŋɨ kɨnda agɨm uŋun do wɨrɨpdakgwit.
Yaŋban Pita da Yesu gen kɨnda yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nin yo morap yopmaŋek gak naŋ gɨn gol awɨlgamaŋ. Do nin yo ni baŋ tɨmɨtneŋ?”
“Nandani! Amɨn kɨnda da jap yet tɨŋtɨŋok do pigaga kɨgɨt.
Kɨŋ donki meŋi gat monji gat paŋabɨŋ ɨmalni donki bamot da kwenikon yopmaŋakwal Yesu pawɨgɨ uŋudon yɨkgɨt.
“Yaŋdo, kaŋ kɨmotni. Amɨn Tagɨsi ni gɨldaron apdɨsak uŋun ji dɨma nandaŋ.
Uŋun bɨsapmon paŋdetni 12 kabɨkon da kɨnda mani Judas Iskariot uŋun da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨkon kɨgɨt.
Aŋek topmon da man madep ɨmɨŋ mudaŋek ɨmal gami ɨlɨgek iyɨ dakon pabɨ pɨgɨk paŋ ɨmgwit. Paŋ ɨmɨŋek tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotjak do ɨlɨk aŋaŋ kɨwit.
Yaŋ iyɨŋek abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋbal Yesu da Saimon kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Saimon, Jon dakon monji. Buŋon amɨn da Sipas yaŋ gayɨni.” (“Sipas” uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun “Pita”)
Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “On amɨn iyɨ yokwi agɨt bo ae meŋ datniyo da yokwi agɨmal uŋun do dɨma. Piŋkop da wasok kɨnda on amɨnon noman aban amɨn da koni do dabɨlɨ mɨni altagɨt.
“Monjɨsok kɨnda oni uŋun dakon bret tɨmɨ 5 bali baŋ wasaŋbi uŋun gat ae tap kɨlap bamorɨ gat taŋ ɨmaŋ. Mani on mɨŋat amɨn morapyo do yomno arɨpmɨ dɨma asak.”
Yaŋban nandaŋek Juda amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yaŋ yaŋaki gak da buron koŋ kɨnda asisi egɨsak yaŋsi nandamaŋ. Abraham gat kombɨ amɨn gat uŋun kɨsi kɨlɨ kɨmakgwit, mani gak da yosol ‘Amɨn kɨnda da nak dakon gen guramɨtjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn dɨmasi kɨmotjak.’
Parisi dabɨlɨ mɨni amɨn, ji mibɨltok kap dakon burɨ ɨkdɨgoni kaŋ, manji iyɨ tagɨ kɨlek tosak.
Aŋakwan Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ da Yesukon abɨŋ aŋkewalek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin da gen tebanon niaŋ tosok? Amɨn kɨnda da mɨŋatni galak toknikon tagɨ kwɨnɨtjak, bo dɨma?”
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Jikon bret niaŋ da toŋ?” Yaŋban yawit, “Ninon bret 7 ae tap kɨlap monɨŋgok bamorɨsok dagɨn taŋ nimaŋ.”
Yaŋba Pailat da yagɨt, “Yum koni. Gen kɨlɨ mandat uŋun dagɨn tosak.”
Yaŋ yaŋek Yesu tobɨl paŋdetni baŋgɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji da yo pɨndak nandaŋyo aŋ, uŋun pɨndakgaŋ amɨn uŋun kɨsɨk kɨsɨk ekwaŋ.
Sipsip dakon kɨla amɨn yokwi moneŋ do nandaŋek pi asak uŋun sipsip dakon ami dɨma, do joŋ pɨŋan abɨsak bɨsapmon si pasalek sipsip yopmaŋ kɨsak. Yopmaŋ kɨŋakwan joŋ pɨŋan da obɨŋ sipsip dapmaŋ nok do aŋakwan waseŋ kwaŋ.
Piŋkop da dɨpmɨnon Erot do dɨma tobɨl kɨni do yoyɨŋban nandaŋek kosit ŋwakŋwarɨ naŋ mɨktɨmnikon si kɨwit.
Dat, mango aŋpap abɨ madepsi asak.” Yesu yaŋ yaŋban Kwen Kokupmon da gen kɨnda yaŋ pɨgɨt, “Nak mano aŋpap abo madepsi agɨt da aeno akdɨsat.”
Amɨn wurɨpdak pasalek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Yo on altaŋban komaŋ uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ niaŋ?”
Yaŋ aban uŋun da buŋon nani da kwabatni uŋun paŋek monjɨ mɨni da kɨmakgɨt.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda amɨn monɨŋ da Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun abɨdoŋ uŋun da tɨlak dɨma abɨdoni kaŋ, uŋungwan arɨpmɨ dɨma pɨgɨkdaŋ.”
Mani Yesu da kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: ‘Bret dagɨn amɨn egɨp egɨp tagɨ dɨma yomjak. Piŋkop dakon gen kɨsi morap paŋek egɨp egɨp paŋ.’ ”
Uŋun muwut muwut yut dakon mibɨltok amɨni mani Krispus uŋun gat gwakni gat Pol da Piŋkop dakon gen yaŋban Amɨn Tagɨ nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit. Ae Korin kokup papmon amɨn morapmɨ nandaŋ gadat aŋek telagɨ pakbi sowit.
Iyɨŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Ji wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ dɨma pɨndatni kaŋ, nandaŋ gadat dɨma akdaŋ.”
On amɨn da Telagɨ Yut Madep aŋupbal aban telagɨ dɨma tosak do pini aŋakwan abɨdagɨmaŋ. Do gak da gaga iyɨŋaki gen morap yaŋ ɨmamaŋ uŋun bamɨ yomaŋ yaŋ iyɨ yaŋakwan nandaki.”
Wɨsa dagokdo 9 kilok aŋakwan aŋakgwit.
Yesu uŋun gat gɨldat bamorɨ egɨ mudaŋek uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Galili Provinskon kɨgɨt.
“Nin da nandaŋapno Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak da Telagɨ Yut Madep amɨn da awit uŋun tuwɨlek gɨldat kapbɨ da butgwan yut ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda abeŋ. Yut uŋun amɨn kɨsit da agagɨ dakon tɨlak dɨma abeŋ.’ ”
Uŋun amɨn dogɨn Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: ‘Nandani, geno yaŋ teŋteŋosak do amɨn kɨnda yabekgo uŋun da mibɨltaŋ gamjak. Aŋek kositgo aŋnoman asak.’
Jamba but amɨn, ji da mɨktɨmon ae kwen yo morap toŋ pɨndagek kokwin tagɨsi aŋ. Mani abɨsok yo morap altoŋ uŋun pɨndagek kokwin nido tagɨ dɨma aŋ?”
Yesu da tɨlak gen uŋun yaŋ mudaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨsi altaŋ damjak uŋun dakon bɨsap ji dɨma nandaŋ, do tagap taŋek egɨpni.”
Amɨn Tagɨ da sakwabat uŋun kaŋek bupmɨsi nandaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak kunam dɨma takgi.”
Uŋun gɨldaron gɨn paŋdetni bamorɨ Emeas kokupmon kɨk do kɨgɨmal. Emeas uŋun Jerusalem da dubagɨsi, 11 kilomita da arɨp tosok.
Yaŋba Yesu da paŋmuwugek tɨlak gen kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt: “Sunduk da Sunduk notni arɨpmɨ dɨma yolyolɨ.
“Nak yaŋsi dayɨsat, amɨn morapmɨ da egɨp egɨpmon wɨgɨk do pini akdaŋ, mani arɨpmɨ dɨma wɨgɨkdaŋ. Do ji yoma kosit gwagak monɨŋɨ naŋ wɨgɨk do pi tebai ani.
Iyɨ do ‘nak Piŋkop dakon Monji’ yaŋ yosok, do ji da niaŋ aŋ ɨmneŋ do nandaŋ?” Yaŋban kɨsi morap da yawit, “Gulusuŋ asak, do si kɨmotjak.”
Yaŋsi dayɨsat, bɨsit yaŋ ani kaŋ, tepmɨsi paŋpulugokdɨsak. Mani, Amɨn Dakon Monji mɨktɨmon apjak bɨsapmon amɨn nandaŋ gadatni toŋ pɨndatjak, bo dɨma?”
Yaŋban yawit, “On amɨn gulusuŋni dakon mibɨlɨ nandak do amɨn dɨ gat yaŋ yomno nido apni? Iyɨ dakon gen kaga da kɨlɨ uŋun yaŋban nandamaŋ.”
Uŋun dɨmasi! Nak asisi dayɨsat, ji but tobɨl dɨma ani kaŋ, uŋun amɨn kabɨ da kɨmakgwit jiyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn kɨmotdaŋ.
Iyɨŋba nandaŋek Yesu uŋun boron wɨgakwan amɨn koŋ gat egɨpgut uŋun da Yesu yol do bɨsit tebai iyɨgɨt.
Judas uŋun yomakon pɨgakwan Yesu yaŋ yagɨt, “Abɨsok Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun man madep pakdɨsak. Ae Monji do aŋek Piŋkop yo kɨsi man madep paŋek
Yesu yaŋsi nandagɨt, Dat da yo morap kɨla abeŋ do tapmɨm namgut yaŋ nandagɨt. Ae Piŋkopmon da apgum, do ae Piŋkopmon tobɨl kɨkdɨsat yaŋ kɨsi nandagɨt.
“Amɨn Tagɨ, oman monjɨno yutnon pokdok. Kɨdarɨ alek taŋ, ae tepmɨ madepsi nandɨsak.”
Yesu da tɨlak gen kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Dabɨlɨ mɨni kɨnda dabɨlni mɨni notni kɨnda kosit tagɨ yolɨsak? Kaŋ kɨsi bamot gapmagwan mokdamal.
Yaŋ yaŋban amɨn yabekgɨt uŋun tobɨl yutnon wɨgɨ oman monjɨ uŋun kɨlɨ kɨlek tagɨt kawit.
Nak dakon man yaŋ teŋteŋaŋek jɨgɨ pasak uŋun yolɨko pɨndatjak.”
Yaŋ asak, do butno da tagɨsi aŋakwan kɨsɨk kɨsɨk gen yosot. Ae gɨptɨmno Piŋkop da aŋpulugosak do jomjom asat.
Amɨn da kɨndap sop bamɨ baŋ pɨndagek kɨndap yokwi bo tagɨ yaŋ pɨndak nandaŋyo aŋ. Amɨn da pik kɨndap dakon bamɨ pak do nap kelɨ toŋon kɨŋ dɨma dekgaŋ. Ae wain sop kɨndap yokwi kelɨ toŋon kɨŋ dɨma paŋ.
Yesu uŋun tɨlak gen morap yoyɨŋ mudaŋek uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek
Yaŋban amɨn uŋun da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn kɨnda mani Konilias uŋun da yabekban abamaŋ. Uŋun amɨn kɨlegɨsi ae Piŋkop do pasalek gawak ɨmɨŋek egɨsak. Juda amɨn morap da uŋun amɨn do nandaba wukwan ɨmaŋ. Telagɨ aŋelo kɨnda da gak yaŋ gaban yutnikon kɨki do iyɨgɨt. Kɨŋek gak da gen dɨ yaŋbɨ nandɨsak do iyɨgɨt.”
Bɨsap kɨndakon Yesu dakon paŋdetni namɨn da mibɨltok amɨnin egɨsak yaŋ do gen emat kɨnda awit.
Pol da Esia mɨktɨmon bɨsap noknok dɨma aneŋ yaŋ nandagɨt, do nin tap wakgakon da Epesas kokup pap si yapmaŋek Miletus kokup pap kɨgɨmaŋ. Bɨsap noknok dɨma aŋek tepmɨ kɨneŋ kaŋ, Pentikos Bɨsap Madep Jerusalem koneŋ yaŋ nandagɨt.
“Ji abɨŋ amɨn kɨnda koni. Uŋun amɨn da yo morap kalɨp agɨm uŋun nayɨŋ mudak. Uŋun Kristo bo?”
Yesu da nak naga bret Kwen Kokup da pɨgɨm yaŋ yagɨt do Juda amɨn da nandaba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmɨŋek gen morapmɨ yawit.
‘Amɨn Tagɨ da yaŋ yosok, Kwen Kokup uŋun kɨla amɨn madep yɨyɨt tamono ae mɨktɨm uŋun kandap yɨpyɨp tamono. Do nak do yut kɨnda arɨpmɨ dɨma agagɨ. Ae yɨk yawot tamono dukwan tosak?
Aŋakwan Epikorian ae Stoik amɨn kabɨ bamot uŋun dakon nandak nandak amɨn dɨwarɨ da opba Pol gat gen emat aŋakwa dɨ da yaŋ yawit, “On gen pakbi amɨn ni gen naŋ yosok?” Ae dɨ da yawit, “Mɨktɨm dubagɨkon nani dakon piŋkop uŋun do bo yosok?” Pol da Gen Bin Tagɨsi yoyɨŋek Yesu do yoyɨgɨt ae amɨn kɨmoron da pɨdoni do kɨsi yoyɨgɨt uŋun do aŋek gen uŋun yawit.
Yaŋdo, Parisi amɨn ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nido paŋdetgoni uŋun babɨk dakon gen teban yapmaŋek kɨsirɨ dɨma sugaŋek jap noŋ?”
Dagaŋakwan boron yɨkgwit amɨn uŋun Yesu gawak ɨmɨŋek yawit, “Asisi, gak Piŋkop dakon Monji.”
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨm, ‘Rom amɨn ninon gen teban kɨnda yaŋ tosok. Amɨn kɨnda da amɨn kɨnda gen yaŋ ɨmjak kaŋ, amɨn uŋun da geni yaŋ ɨmjak amɨn da ɨŋamon agek gen yaŋ ɨban kobogɨ tagɨ yosak. Yaŋ aban asi yo yokwi kɨnda agɨt kaŋ, kobogɨ do yo yokwi tagɨ aŋ ɨmɨmɨ. Yaŋ dɨma ani kaŋ, Rom nin dakon gen teban yapmaŋgaŋ.’
Do gak moneŋgo abɨdaŋek kɨ. Naga da galaktogon amɨn buŋon abeŋ uŋun gat moneŋ tɨlak kaloŋɨkon damɨsat.
Yesu da tɨlak gen bamot uŋun yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat ae Parisi amɨn gat da nin do yosok yaŋ nandawit.
Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon nagal yɨpmaŋek waŋga kɨŋakwan paŋdetni da Yesukon kɨŋek Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon yut madep madep pɨndatjak do yolɨwit.
Gen dayɨsat uŋun amɨn morap kɨsi do yosot. Kaŋ kɨmotni.”
Yaŋ yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gen uŋun nandaŋek Yesu aŋakba kɨmotjak do kosit wɨsɨwit. Uŋun Yesu do si pasalgwit, nido mɨŋat amɨnyo da Yesu dakon gen yogokni do tamtam yawit.
Ji nandaba kɨk aŋek egɨp egɨpji tɨmɨsok dɨ gat tagɨ saŋbeŋba wɨgɨsak yaŋ nandaŋ, ma? Uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨmasi.
Paŋdetni da gen uŋun do yaŋba yokwi tok aba burɨ pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen uŋun do nandaŋ gadatji wɨtdal kɨsak, ma?
Muwugek paŋdet kabɨnikon da dɨwarɨ kɨsitni dɨma sugaŋek jap ɨsal tɨmɨk naŋyo aba pɨndakgwit.
Ji aŋpakni pɨndak nandaŋyo aŋek kombɨ amɨn toptopmɨ yaŋ pɨndakba pɨsoni. Nap kelɨ toŋ da wain sop arɨpmɨ dɨma potni. Ae jal da kɨmɨp arɨpmɨ dɨma wigɨljak.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji nak do but dasi galak taŋ namaŋ kaŋ, yo morap ani do yagɨm uŋun guramɨtni.
Bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ kalugɨsi egek Piŋkop da tapmɨm daban yo morap uŋun altokdaŋ uŋun tagɨ yapni, ae Amɨn Dakon Monji da ɨŋamon tagɨ atni yaŋ do bɨsit pi ani.”
Yesu da gen uŋun yagɨt do nandaban yo madepsi aban buŋon yol awɨlgwit amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Asisi dayɨsat, Israel amɨnon nandaŋ gadatni madep on amɨn dakon yombem kɨnda dɨma kagɨm.
Iyɨŋ mudaŋba amɨn morapmɨsi kɨŋ abɨŋ abɨŋ aŋakwa Yesu gat yabekbi kabɨni gat jap noknok dakon bɨkbɨk dɨma pɨsaŋ yomgut. Aban Yesu da yabekbi kabɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Opba mɨktɨm amɨn dɨma ekwaŋ tɨmon kɨno. Uŋudon egek tapmɨm pani.”
Amɨn bamot yabekba Antiok pɨgɨ paŋmuwukbi kabɨ yaŋ yobal muwukba papia uŋun yomgumal.
Yaŋban tap kɨlap kɨlɨ paŋkɨbɨt abi tɨmɨsok kɨnda ɨmɨŋba
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ nandani do tɨlak gen kɨnda gat dayɨko nandani. Amɨn kɨnda jap yet pigaga tɨŋtɨŋosok.
Aŋakwa Sailas gat Judas gat uŋun kombɨ amɨn bamorɨ do gen tagɨsi morapmɨ paŋmuwukbi yoyɨŋek burɨ paŋteban agɨmal.
Amɨn da Apolos Amɨn Tagɨ dakon mibɨlɨ do iyɨŋ dekba kɨlɨ nandagɨt. Ae Amɨn Tagɨ dakon gen but dasi nandaŋek amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgɨt. Yaŋ aŋek Yesu dakon mibɨlɨ suŋ dɨma yagɨt. Bamɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋagɨt. Mani Jon da telagɨ pakbi sogɨt uŋun dogɨn nandagɨt.
Papia on manjɨŋek amɨn da gen morap gayɨwit uŋun nandabɨ bamɨsi asak.
“Yaŋban amɨn tagɨ da oman monjɨ uŋun yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Gak oman monjɨ wagɨl yokwisi! Gaga gen yosol uŋun dogɨn gen pikon gepbeŋ. Nak teban teban amɨn kɨnda ae amɨn da yo yopmaŋgaŋ tɨmɨkdat, ae jap amɨn da kwaokgaŋ uŋun pɨlɨkdat yaŋ nandaŋ namɨsal.
Kalbi kɨndakon Amɨn Tagɨ da Pol burɨ pɨsaŋakwan dɨpmɨn yombem kɨnda kaŋakwan altaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak dɨma pasalek nak dakon geno sigɨn yaŋ teŋteŋoki. Gen mapmɨt dɨma aki.
Mani amɨn dɨpmɨn pak mudaŋakwa uwalni da abɨŋ jap yet tagɨ yopgut uŋun bɨkbɨkgwan joŋ yokwi dakon yerɨ tɨŋtɨŋaŋek kɨgɨt.
Monji do man madep ɨmdɨsak. Yaŋ uŋun tepmɨsi akdɨsak.
Yesu paŋdetni 12 kabɨ yaŋ yoban opba, bamot bamot Piŋkop dakon gen yoni do yabekgɨt. Yabegek koŋ yolni do yaŋ mudaŋ yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Jon Yesu da gen yagɨt nandaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, nin kaŋapno amɨn kɨnda da gak da manon koŋ yolban kamaŋ. Mani nin da kabɨkon nani kɨnda dɨma, do yaŋsop aŋɨmɨmaŋ.”
Wɨsawɨsa do Pol da amɨn morap jap noni do yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Bɨsap dubak butji tagɨ dɨma taŋakwa jap dɨma nawit. Ɨsalsi agakwa gɨldat 14 mudak.
Yesu da gen yaŋ yaŋban Juda amɨn da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak Samaria amɨn kɨnda, koŋ kɨnda da gak da buron egɨsak. Uŋun gen bamɨ yomaŋ?”
Saimon Pita kɨndapni alɨŋ agakwan yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak Yesu dakon paŋdetni kɨnda, ma?” Yaŋ iyɨŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Nak paŋdetni kɨnda dɨma.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon yo jɨgɨsi altokdaŋ. Piŋkop da mibɨlɨkon yo morap wasagɨron da egɨ abɨsok ekwamaŋon yo jɨgɨsi uŋuden kɨnda dɨma altagɨt, ae buŋon dɨma altokdɨsak.
Yoyɨŋakwa Amɨn Tagɨ da paŋpulugaŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da nandaŋ gadat awit. Yaŋ aŋek but tobɨl aŋek Amɨn Tagɨkon kɨwit.
Pita gat Jon gat amɨn gen sigɨn yoyɨŋakwal mukwa sogok amɨn gat Sadyusi amɨn gat ae Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon obip amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat kɨsi apgwit.
Wɨkwan Yesu da wain naŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Kɨlɨ uŋun mudosok.” Yaŋ yaŋek busuŋɨ tadɨk pɨŋek wupni yɨpban kɨgɨt.
Apban kokup ɨsalni gat ae yo do bɨsit yaŋakwan kawit amɨn gat da yaŋ yawit, “On amɨn uŋun kalɨp yɨgek amɨn da moneŋ ɨmni do bɨsit yoyɨgɨt uŋun amɨn bo?”
Maria yaŋ iyɨgɨmal, “Mɨŋat gak kunam nido takdal?” Yaŋbal yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨno abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ dukwan yɨpmaŋ uŋun dɨma nandɨsat.”
mani ji da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdok do nagon ap do dɨmasi galak toŋ.
Jiyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn ekwaŋ. Amɨn da dandaba ji amɨn kɨlegɨsi ekwaŋ yaŋ nandaŋ, mani butjikon ji jamba but amɨnsi ae gen teban yapyap amɨnsi ekwaŋ.
Yaŋ aban kaŋek Yesu tebai abɨdawit.
Gen tebanon Moses da gen kɨnda yagɨt uŋun yaŋ: mɨŋat uŋuden tɨpbaŋ aŋakba kɨmotjak. Gak da uŋun do niaŋ nandɨsal?”
Yum kaŋapno mɨrɨm da tap wakganin awɨl aŋkɨ mɨktɨm tɨm kɨnda tap binap tosok uŋudon yɨpban tegaŋ atdɨsak.”
Amɨn kɨnda da egɨp egɨpno arɨpmɨ dɨma gwayesak. Naga dakon galaktok yolek egɨp egɨpno parekgeŋ. Egɨp egɨpno parekgeŋ ae abɨdokeŋ uŋun dakon yaŋ dagok uŋun nagon tosok. Dat da yaŋsi abeŋ dosi yagɨt.”
Asisi gayɨsat, gak monjɨ gɨmoŋɨ egɨpgul bɨsapmon ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkgo paŋek kokup dukwan kɨk do nandagɨl uŋudon kɨŋ kɨŋ agɨl. Mani amɨn pelaŋ aki bɨsapmon, kɨsitgo aŋenagaki amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ da ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkgo paŋ gamɨŋek gak aŋaŋ kosit dɨma kɨk do nandaki uŋun naŋ aŋkɨkdaŋ.”
uŋun da aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Aŋakwa gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan Piŋkop da kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdokdɨsak.” Gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek bupmɨsi nandawit.
Bɨlak kwenikon bamɨ tosak kaŋ tagɨsi. Mani bamɨ dɨma tosak kaŋ, tagɨ pasɨki.’ ”
ji gat ae Israel amɨn kabɨ gat kɨsi dayɨko nandani. Yesu Kristo Nasaret kokupmon nani uŋun da tapmɨmon on amɨn aŋmɨlɨp agɨmak da ji da dabɨlon akdak. Ji da Yesu tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmakgɨt mani Piŋkop da kɨmoron naŋ aban pɨdagɨt.
Nandak nandak amɨn uŋun kɨŋ mudaŋakwa, Amɨn Tagɨ dakon aŋelo da Josep dɨpmɨnon altaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Erot da Monjɨ aŋakban kɨmotjak do wɨsɨkdɨsak, do gak pɨdaŋ monjɨ ŋakŋak gat meŋi gat tɨmɨkbɨ Isip mɨktɨmon pasal kɨni. Isip sigɨn egakwa nak da aesi apni do don gayɨkeŋ.”
Buŋon paŋdetni bamorɨ da kokup kɨndakon kɨk do kɨŋakwal Yesu da gɨptɨmɨ kulabɨk aŋek altaŋ yoban amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda yaŋ kagɨmal.
Yaŋ yaŋek mɨŋat amɨnyo dɨwarɨ yopmaŋek, Pita, Jems ae padɨge Jon uŋun baŋgɨn tɨmɨkban kɨwit.
Uŋun kokupmon Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit amɨn dɨ pɨndakgɨmaŋ. Pɨndatno uŋun da Sonda kɨnda nin gat egɨpneŋ do niyɨwit. Do uŋun gat egek don mɨktɨm kosit Rom kokup papmon kɨgɨmaŋ.
Yesu uŋun tɨlak gen yoyɨŋ mudaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn yaŋ yobi uŋun da morapmɨsi asak, mani yutnon amɨn tagɨ gat yɨtni do kokwinɨkbi uŋun da tagapmɨ.”
Ae uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Pilipai kɨŋ altagɨmaŋ. Pilipai uŋun Masadonia mɨktɨm dakon kokup pap madepni. Uŋun Rom da kɨla agɨt. Rom amɨn morapmɨ da kalɨp kɨlɨ apgwit da uŋun kokupmon ekwaŋ. Nin uŋudon gɨldat kabi dɨ egɨpgumaŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋba Pita da tebaisi yaŋek yagɨt, “Asisi dayɨsat, amɨn uŋun yoŋ nak dɨmasi nandaŋ ɨmɨsat. Top yosot kaŋ, jobɨt tagɨ tɨmɨkgeŋ.”
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Mani abɨsok moneŋ sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨk monɨŋji taŋ damaŋ kaŋ, uŋun si tɨmɨtni. Ae yɨk madepji kɨsi tɨmɨtni. Ae emat agak sɨbani mɨni amɨn uŋun ɨmal dubakni yumaŋ naŋek uŋun dakon moneŋ baŋ emat agak sɨbani yumni.
Mani kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek nak da kalɨp Galili mɨktɨmon mibɨltaŋ damɨŋek kɨkeŋ.”
Amɨn da mani pawɨgɨni do galagɨsi nandawit. Mani Piŋkop da mani pawɨgɨsak do dɨma nandawit.
Yesu abɨdawit amɨn uŋun Yesu abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn Kaiapas da yutnon aŋkɨwit. Uŋudon gen teban dakon yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat ae kɨla amɨn gat kɨsi muwukgwit.
Aŋakwan pi ɨsalni dɨwarɨ da kaŋek burɨ yokwi taŋba kɨŋ amɨn tagɨnikon yo uŋun agɨt do iyɨwit.
Gapman dakon mibɨltok amɨn madep da papia uŋun manjɨŋek Pol yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak provinsgo dukon?” Yaŋban Pol da iyɨgɨt, “Nak provinsno Silisia.”
Yaŋ aŋek Piŋkop Datji Kwen Kokup egɨsak uŋun dakon monjinisi egɨpni. Uŋun da gɨldatni yɨpban amɨn yokwi ae kɨlegɨ kɨsikon mosok. Ae sɨkak yɨpban amɨn aŋpak kɨlegɨ aŋ ae yokwi aŋ kɨsikon mosok.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban wɨsa dagaŋakwan aŋelo da yoyɨgɨt uŋun da tɨlagon kɨŋ Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalon pabɨgɨ amɨn wasaŋek yoyɨŋ dekgwit. Aŋakwa mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat dabɨni gat gen kokwin tamo madepmon opgwit. Obɨŋek Israel amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn obɨŋ muwutni do yaŋ yomgwit. Obɨŋ muwugek yabekbi kabɨ dam teban yutnon da opni do gen yɨpba kɨgɨt.
Kɨlɨ Yesu pakbi ɨdap yɨpmaŋek ɨleŋ kɨndakon wɨgɨgɨt. Wɨgek yabekbini dagoni do nandagɨt amɨn yoyɨŋban iyɨkon abɨŋ muwukgwit.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek Peliks do papia kɨnda yaŋ mandagɨt,
Mani yopmaŋ kɨk do aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da ji do aeno opbeŋ do nandɨsagon don opbeŋ.” Yaŋ yoyɨŋek tap wakgakon wɨgek Epesas yɨpmaŋek kɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋba amɨn bamot da yo kosiron altawit uŋun do yoyɨŋek yagɨmal, “Bret pudaŋakwan uŋudon kaŋ nandaŋyo amak.”
“Ji Kristo do namɨn dakon monjɨ yaŋ nandaŋ?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Dewit dakon monji.”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek dubagɨsok amɨn da tɨp maba kwaŋ uŋun da arɨpmon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ ŋwakbeŋ aŋek bɨsit aŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Uŋudon gɨn emat amɨn kɨnda Jon dakon busuŋɨ aŋopjak do yabekgɨt. Yabekban uŋun da kɨŋ dam teban yutnon wɨgɨ Jon dakon tegɨ mandaŋ dagagɨt.
Tɨpbaŋ aŋagakwa Stiwen bɨsit yaŋ agɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu, wupno abɨda.”
Pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo yabekbini 12 kabɨ da obɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Kokup amɨni mɨnikon ekwamaŋ, do yoyɨŋbɨ mɨŋat amɨn morapyo kɨŋek kokup monɨŋ monɨŋ ae tɨmɨ dɨgwan kɨŋ jap pakbiyo gat ae dɨpmɨn potpot tamoyo gat wɨsini.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak da kɨŋ aŋmɨlɨp abeŋ.”
Kɨlek taŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nandaki, gak uŋun do amɨn dɨma yoyɨŋek mukwa sogogon kɨŋek gɨptɨmgo yolɨki. Aŋek Moses da yagɨt uŋun da tɨlagon paret aŋaki amɨn da asi kɨlek tal yaŋ gandani.”
“Nak asisi dayɨsat, uŋun bɨsapmon egɨpni amɨn dɨma kɨmagakwa yo morap uŋun kɨsi altaŋ mudokdaŋ.
Yesu uŋun amɨn kabɨ tɨmɨkban ɨleŋon da mɨktɨm kuldukgɨbaŋ kɨndakon pukwa paŋdetni morapmɨ gat kɨsi akgwit. Aŋakwa Judia mɨktɨm dakon amɨn morapmɨ gat, ae Jerusalem kokup papmon amɨn gat, ae tap amɨn Tair ae Saidon kokup da kapmatjok egɨpgwit amɨn uŋun gat kɨsi egɨpgwit.
Kokup kɨndakon amɨn da uwal aŋdaba kaŋ, kokup uŋun yɨpmaŋek pasal kokup kɨndakon kɨni. Nak asi dayɨsat, ji Israel amɨn dakon kokup morapmon pi wasɨp dɨma aŋakwa Amɨn Dakon Monji apdɨsak.
Amɨn kɨnda da mɨktɨm dakon yo morap paŋ egakwan egɨp egɨpni pasɨljak kaŋ, uŋun yo morap da niaŋ aŋek aŋpulugoni? Bo egɨp egɨpni aeni abɨdok do tomni ninaŋ yumjak?
Yɨgakwa oman mɨŋat kɨnda da Pita uŋun kɨndap da teŋteŋɨkon yɨkban kagɨt. Pakyaŋsi kaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “On amɨn Yesu gat kɨsi egɨpgumal.”
Uŋun kɨlɨ kɨmakgɨt, mani abɨsok gak da Piŋkop yo niaŋen kɨnda do bɨsit iyɨŋbɨ uŋun da tagɨ gamjak yaŋ nandɨsat.”
“Nak gagon obɨŋek mɨktɨmon saŋbeŋek dɨma egɨpbeŋ. Mani uŋun amɨn kabɨ da mɨktɨmon sigɨn egɨpdaŋ. Telagɨ Dat, mango tapmɨmɨ toŋsi namgul uŋun naŋ paŋkutnoki. Yaŋ aŋaki nit da kaloŋɨsi ekwamak, uŋun amɨn kabɨ da kaloŋɨsi yaŋ gɨn egɨpni.
Yaŋban paŋdetni nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi aban notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Yaŋ kaŋ namɨn da egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdosak?”
Yaŋ aŋakwa nandaŋek oman monjɨ kɨnda yaŋ ɨban apban iyɨgɨt, ‘Uŋun nibaŋ aŋ?’
Uŋun amɨn da gakdosi amɨn ani do aŋek egɨp egɨpno kaloŋ gak do gamɨsat.
Mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn Anas ae dabɨni dɨwarɨ, ae Kaiapas gat Jon ae Aleksanda gat kɨsi muwukgwit.
Ae 10 tausen danari tɨmɨkgɨt amɨn uŋunyo yaŋ gɨn aŋakwan 10 tausen danari kɨnda gat noman tagɨt.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji wigat gɨtni naŋ pɨgɨni. Amɨn wagɨl tasɨk tokdaŋ dakon kokupmon pɨgɨk dakon wigat gat ae kositni gat uŋun ɨlalogɨsi, do uŋun naŋ yolek pɨgɨk uŋun tagapmɨsi. Amɨn morapmɨsi da wigat uŋun naŋ pɨkwaŋ.
Nin do nandaba wukwan nimɨŋek but galak do yo morapmɨ nimgwit. Ae tap wakga abɨdok do agɨmaŋ bɨsapmon kosit agek naŋ paŋyo aneŋ do yo uŋun tap wakgakon yopgwit.
Yesu uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Judia mɨktɨmon ae Jodan Pakbi terɨ kɨnda uŋudon kɨgɨt. Uŋudon egakwan mɨŋat amɨn madepsi apgwit. Apba Yesu iyɨ aŋ aŋ agɨt uŋudeŋ ae Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt.
Asisi gayɨsat, gak dam tebanon sigɨn egaki wɨgɨ moneŋ niaŋ yopbi do gayɨni uŋun kɨsisi yopmaŋek don waŋga kɨkdɨsal.”
Iyɨŋba Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen uŋun bamɨ yoŋ. Elaija kɨlɨ abɨŋ yo morap paŋmɨlɨp agɨt. Aŋakwan amɨn da galaktokni yolek yo mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ Piŋkop da papiakon gen tosok uŋun da tɨlagon aŋ ɨmgwit. Mani Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda mandabi uŋun yaŋ: ‘Amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji manji ɨmɨŋek yo yokwi madepsi aŋ ɨmdaŋ.’ Uŋun gen mibɨlɨ nido tosok?”
Bo ae Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda mukwa sogok amɨn do yosok uŋun kɨsi dɨma manjɨŋ nandaŋyo awit? Mukwa sogok amɨn Sabat bɨsap morapmon gen teban yapmaŋek pi aŋ, mani dɨwarɨni mɨni ekwaŋ.
Mani amɨn dɨ da yaŋ yawit, “Koŋ dakon mibɨltok amɨn Belsebul da tapmɨmon koŋ yoldak.”
Aŋakwan Galili mɨŋat amɨn morapmɨ gat, ae Dekapolis amɨn gat, ae Jerusalem, ae Judia, ae Jodan Pakbi usugap tet amɨn gat kɨsi da Yesu yolgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban iyɨwit, “Amɨn Tagɨ, pɨndat! Nin emat agak sɨbanin bamorɨ oni.” Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Uŋun arɨpmɨ.”
Gen yosot uŋun pakyaŋsi nandani.”
Uŋun amɨn kabɨ da kalɨp Troas kokup papmon paŋkɨ egek nin do jomjom awit.
Mɨŋat bamorɨ bret sok do plaua wasaŋakwal, kɨnda abɨdaŋek kɨnda yɨpdɨsak.”
Yesu da gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek paŋdetni morapmɨ da yaŋ yawit, “Gen on yosok uŋun jɨgɨsi. Namɨn da arɨpmɨ abɨdosak?”
Aŋek amɨn bamot tɨmɨgek gen pikon yop do nandawit, mani pɨlɨn tok do agɨt do aŋwa don yaŋ nandaŋek dam teban yutnon yopgwit.
Kalɨpsigwan kombɨ amɨn Aisaia da Jon do gen yaŋ mandagɨt: “Mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yosok, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ dakon kosit aŋdɨmdɨm ani, kositni pasɨŋ aŋmɨlɨp ani.’ ”
Amɨn kɨnda iyɨ dakon egɨp egɨp aŋkutnok do nandɨsak kaŋ, egɨp egɨpni pasɨl ɨmdɨsak. Mani amɨn kɨnda egɨp egɨpni paretjak kaŋ, egɨp egɨpni kutnaŋban taŋ ɨmdɨsak.
Nak do pakyaŋsi nandaŋ nameŋ tam, Datnoyo kɨsi tagɨ nandaŋ ɨbam. Abɨsok da wasaŋek uŋun nandaŋ ɨmɨŋek kɨlɨ uŋun koŋ.”
Bɨsap morapmɨ Yesu gat paŋdet kabɨni gat uŋun pigaga muwuk muwuk awit, do uwal da kɨsiron yɨpjak amɨn Judas kɨsi uŋun pigaga kaŋ nandaŋyo agɨt.
Teŋteŋaŋ naban nak mɨktɨmon maŋ pagek nandaŋapbo gen kɨnda altaŋek yaŋ nayɨgɨt, ‘Sol! Sol! Gak nido nak aŋupbal ak do pi asal?’
Nin yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨt do aŋek yo asal uŋun dabɨlno da kɨlɨ uŋun kosot.
Kɨsi arɨpmɨsi naŋba jap dɨwat tawit uŋun paŋdetni da tɨmɨgek yɨk madepsi 7 kabɨ sɨmɨlgwit.
Morapmɨ da yaŋ yawit, “Koŋ kɨnda burɨkon egakwan but upbal asak. Ji nido geni nandaŋ?”
Yaŋ aban Yesu da datni iyɨgɨt, “Bɨsap niaŋ da yaŋ agɨt?” Yaŋban datni da yagɨt, “Ŋakŋagɨkon da altaŋ ɨmgut da tosok.
Yaŋban Pita da yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak abɨsok asisi nandaŋ kɨmokdot, Piŋkop da amɨn morap kɨsi do nandaban arɨpsi asak.
Yesu da tɨlak gen kɨnda gat yoyɨŋek yagɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda da ɨmal kalugɨ kɨnda pudaŋ ɨmal garaŋɨ dagaŋ kwi kɨndakon bupjak kaŋ uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Yaŋ asak kaŋ, ɨmal kalugɨ aŋupbal asak. Ae ɨmal kalugɨ uŋun kalɨpmɨ gat arɨp dɨma.
Aŋakwan gen teban yoyɨŋdet gat Parisi amɨn gat da mɨŋat kɨnda abɨdaŋ aŋapgwit. Amɨn da kaŋakwa uŋun mɨŋat da yumabi agɨt. Aŋabɨŋ amɨn da dabɨlon yɨpba
Yaŋ aŋek gen yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ tosok: ‘Nak dakon yut uŋun mɨŋat amɨnyo da abɨŋ bɨsit aŋnamni do tosok.’ Mani ji da kulabɨk aba ‘kabo noknok dakon pasɨlɨ tamo’ yombem asak.”
Mani gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan Piŋkop da wasok aban kɨmoron da pɨdaŋban aŋalon aŋ yoban amɨn dɨwarɨ da kawit.
nandaŋek yutnon wɨgek Monjɨ gat meŋi Maria gat pɨndakgwit. Pɨndagek ŋwakbeŋ aŋek Monjɨ gawak ɨmgwit. Yaŋ aŋek yɨkni wɨtdalek gol ae yo dɨwarɨ kɨbaŋɨ tagɨsi yumaŋ nogɨ wukwi but galak do ɨmgwit.
Yapyap Bɨlagon amɨn Piŋkop gawak ɨm do Jerusalem egɨpgwit uŋun bɨkbɨkgwan Grik amɨn dɨwarɨ kɨsi egɨpgwit.
Kɨŋ Sekaraia da yutnon wɨgɨ Elisabet gɨldat tagɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt.
Mani Yesu gen kagani sopmaŋek gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma iyɨgɨt. Yaŋ aban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da aeni iyɨgɨt, “Gak Kristo? Gak Piŋkop gawak ɨmamaŋ uŋun dakon Monji bo dɨma?”
Uŋudon egakwan amɨn morapmɨ Yesukon abɨŋ yaŋ yawit, “Jon uŋun geni paŋteban asak do wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ dɨma agɨt, mani gen morap on amɨn do yagɨt uŋun gen bamɨsi gɨn yagɨt.”
Amɨn kɨnda da gen yaŋ gam do aban gen kokwin tamokon kɨk do kosiron kɨnjil bɨsapmon genjil uŋun yaŋ aŋmɨlɨp ak do pi anjil. Yaŋ dɨma aŋek kwal gen kokwin kɨla agak amɨn da obip amɨn da kɨsiron gepban uŋun da dam teban yutnon gepdɨsak.
“Ji kɨŋek yaŋ nandani: Ji sipsip monɨŋ baŋ yaŋ joŋ pɨŋan da bɨkbɨgon yabekdat.
Amɨn kɨŋ ap awit uŋun da yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmɨŋek wunda kwalkwal aŋek yaŋ iyɨwit,
Mani Yesu da yo agɨt dakon geni sigɨn kɨŋ ɨreŋ tagɨt. Aŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da geni nandak do opgwit. Ae sotni paŋmɨlɨp aŋyomjak do opgwit.
Pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda Genesaret mɨktɨmon kɨŋ ɨleŋɨkon wɨgakwan
Yaŋba datni da yaŋ nandagɨt, apma uŋun bɨsapmonsi Yesu da yaŋ nayɨgɨt, “Monjɨgo egɨpdɨsak.” Yaŋ nandaŋek iyɨ gat ae amɨn kabɨni yutnikon egɨpgwit uŋun gat kɨsi nandaŋ gadat awit.
Uŋun yokwi morap amɨn buron da wɨŋ waŋga kwaŋ uŋun da amɨn paŋupbal aŋ.”
Yesu uŋun Parisi amɨn da yo aŋ ɨmdo yawit uŋun kɨlɨ pɨndak mudagɨt, do kokup uŋun yɨpmaŋek kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da yolgwit. Aŋakwa sot amɨn kɨsisi paŋmɨlɨp aŋek
O Amɨn Tagɨ, uwalnin da yo yokwi aŋnim do yoŋ, do paŋpulugaŋaki oman amɨn kabɨgo nin da pasol pasolɨ mɨni teban taŋek gengo yaŋ teŋteŋoneŋ.
Kokup uŋun kɨk do agɨmal uŋun aŋkapmat aŋakwa Yesu da saŋbeŋek kɨk do yaŋ agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋba nandaŋek gen kokwin amɨn da japmɨsi nandaŋek yabekbi kabɨ dapba kɨmotni do nandawit.
Amɨn uŋun kokup yɨp do aŋek oman monjɨni 10 kabɨ yaŋ yoban apba gol moneŋ tabɨlɨ kɨnda kaloŋ kaloŋ do yomɨŋ yomɨŋ agɨt. Yaŋ aŋek yoyɨgɨt, ‘Ji moneŋ uŋun baŋ moneŋ ɨlɨt pi aŋakwa tobɨl apbeŋ bɨsapmon uŋudon wɨgɨsak.’
Yaŋ kaŋek Pita da Yesu da gen yagɨt uŋun nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, ka! Apma pik kɨndap yokwi tosak do yagɨl abɨsok oni kɨbɨdak!”
Nak naga wigat. Amɨn kɨnda nagon abɨŋek damon pɨgɨsak kaŋ, Piŋkop da yokwikon naŋ abɨdokdɨsak. Aŋakwan uŋun amɨn damon pɨgɨ ae waŋga kɨŋ gɨn aŋek jap do arɨpmɨ dɨma akdɨsak.
Kɨŋ yutnikon wɨgapno Konilias da yaŋ niyɨgɨt, ‘Aŋelo kɨnda da altaŋ namɨŋek yaŋ nayɨgɨt, “Jopa kokup papmon amɨn kɨnda egɨsak mani Saimon, ae mani kɨnda Pita. Uŋun amɨn kɨŋ iyɨŋba opjak do amɨn dɨ yabekbi kɨni.
Don aeni kwa Josep da notni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, ‘Nak naga ji dakon notji Josep.’ Yaŋ aban kɨla amɨn madep Pero da Josep dakon yawi dɨwatni dakon mibɨlɨ nandaŋ pɨndakyo agɨt.
Yoyɨŋba mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat ae kɨla amɨn gat muwugek niaŋ ano kɨlek tosak yaŋ do gen paŋkosit awit. Aŋek obip amɨn do moneŋ madepsi yomɨŋek
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji pik kɨndap kaŋek butji pɨsosak. Kɨlɨŋɨ pakbini toŋ ae tamɨ kaluk yopmaŋdak, uŋun bɨsapmon gɨldat bɨsap kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandaŋ.
“Mɨktɨm saut tetgɨn dakon kɨla amɨn mɨŋat madep uŋun Solomon dakon nandaŋ kokwini tagɨsi iyɨŋakwan nandak do mɨktɨm dubagɨsikon da apgut. Mani amɨn kɨnda oni egɨsak, uŋun da Solomon yapmaŋdak, mani geni dɨma nandaŋ. Do gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon uŋun kɨla amɨn mɨŋat madep da pɨdaŋ agek abɨsok ekwaŋ amɨn kabɨ dakon aŋpak yokwi uŋun do yaŋ teŋteŋokdɨsak.
Iyɨŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jap yet tagɨ yopmaŋdak amɨn uŋun Amɨn Dakon Monji.
Oman monjɨni Dewit da kabɨkon da nin paŋpulugosak do amɨn tebaisi kɨnda aŋnoman agɨt.
Amɨn mibɨltok opgwit uŋun da kɨrɨŋɨk ɨmɨŋek tayaŋgok yɨtjak do tebai iyɨwit. Mani tebai sigɨn yaŋ tɨdaŋek yagɨt, “Dewit Dakon Monji, bupmɨ nandaŋ nam!”
Amɨn muwukgwit uŋun nandaŋ upbal madepsi awit. Yaŋ aŋek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek gen mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ yawit. Ni mibɨlɨ do muwukgamaŋ uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt.
Kaŋakwa Pilip da koŋ morapmɨ yol yomɨŋakwan koŋ da madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek wɨŋ abɨgɨwit. Ae amɨn kɨdarɨ kɨmakbi ae kandapmɨ yokwi uŋun paŋmɨlɨp aŋyo agɨt.
Yesu uŋun Kwen Kokup egek Piŋkop da yo morap paŋkaluk asak uŋun do jomjom asak. Yo morap paŋkaluk abeŋ yaŋ Piŋkop da uŋun do kɨlɨ yaŋ teban tagɨt. Paŋtagap aban telagɨ kombɨ amɨn kabɨni da uŋun do kɨlɨ yawit.
Neri uŋun Melki dakon monji. Melki uŋun Adi dakon monji. Adi uŋun Kosam dakon monji. Kosam uŋun Elmadam dakon monji. Elmadam uŋun Er dakon monji.
Yesu nandaban jɨgɨ madepsi aŋakwan bɨsit tebai sigɨn agɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan kɨŋkɨŋni yawi da yaŋ mɨktɨmon mawit.
Ji ‘asi’ bo ‘dɨma’ yaŋ gɨn yoni kaŋ, uŋun da tagɨ. Gen uŋun da kwenon saŋbeŋek yoŋ uŋun Yokwi Ami da paŋalon asak.”
Amɨn jap nawit uŋun 5 tausen yaŋ da nawit.
Yesu gen yaŋ mudaŋakwan Parisi amɨn kɨnda da yutnikon kwan yɨgek jap nonjil do iyɨgɨt. Iyɨŋban Yesu kɨŋ yutnikon wɨgɨ jap noknok tamokon yɨkgɨt.
Ae uŋun da buŋon yaŋ tosok: ‘Gaga do but dasi niaŋ galak tosol, uŋudeŋ gɨn amɨn do but dasi galak taŋ yobi.’ Uŋun gen teban bamot da gen teban morap yapmaŋ mudomal.”
Yesu da yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek jɨkgo yanjaŋ ɨmgwit. Yaŋ aba yoyɨŋban yomakon pɨgɨ mudaŋakwa, mɨŋatjok dakon meŋi datniyo ae paŋdetni tɨmɨkban mɨŋatjok pakgɨron wɨgɨwit.
Aŋakwa mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep Yesu kaŋek but galak nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn Yesukon kɨŋek “Gɨldat tagɨ!” yaŋ iyɨwit.
Uŋun yut da kosit gwagagon monjɨ bɨlak kɨnda yɨkgɨt mani uŋun Yutikus. Pol da gen saŋbeŋek yaŋakwan monjɨ uŋun yɨk dɨpmɨn pagek uwagat aŋek waŋga mɨktɨmon maŋ aŋakgɨt. Maŋ aŋakban kɨmakgɨt naŋ pɨgɨ abɨdawit. Uŋun yut notni kwen kwen awit dakon kɨdɨŋɨ kapbɨ kwen nani egɨpgwiron da magɨt.
“Gen teban gat ae kombɨ amɨn dakon gen gat yaŋ teŋteŋaŋba Jon da bɨsapmon wugɨt. Mani Jon da bɨsapmon da wasaŋek Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni dakon Gen Bin Tagɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋoŋ. Aŋakwa amɨn uŋungwan pɨgɨk do pi tebaisi aŋ.
Ae jap yet dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm tagɨsikon maŋ kwawit. Uŋun bamɨ 100 taŋ taŋ awit.” Yesu da tɨlak gen uŋun yaŋ mudaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Gen on nandak do galak toŋ amɨn ji pakyaŋsi nandaŋek mibɨlɨ nandaŋ pɨsoni.”
Tɨlak kɨndapmon but pɨso gen kɨnda busuŋni da kwen yaŋ mandawit: ON AMƗN UŊUN JUDA AMƗN DAKON KƗLA AMƗN MADEPNI
Amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut mani Josep. Uŋun Juda dakon kokup pap kɨnda mani Arimatea uŋudon nani. Uŋun amɨn tagɨsi ae aŋpakni kɨlegɨsi. Ae uŋun Piŋkop da amɨn kɨla akdɨsak uŋun do jomjom aŋek egɨpgut. Uŋun Juda amɨn dakon gen kokwin amɨn kabɨkon nani kɨnda, mani gen kokwin amɨn kabɨ notni Yesu do nandak nandak awit ae yo awit uŋun do but kaloŋ dɨma agɨt.
Mani uŋun amɨn iyɨ do Yesu da amɨn kɨlegɨ kɨnda yaŋ kosak do nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak namɨn amɨn baŋ but dasi galak taŋ yobeŋ do yosol?”
Yaŋban Konilias da iyɨgɨt, “Yo kɨnda altaŋ naban egapno gɨldat 4 kabɨ mudak. Yo uŋun yaŋ noman taŋ namgut. Nin abɨsok gɨldat tobɨl do 3 kilok on ekwamaŋ uŋuden bɨsapmon nak yutnokon egek bɨsit pi agɨm. Bɨsit aŋek egapbo uŋudon gɨn amɨn kɨnda ɨŋamnokon akban kagɨm. Ɨmalni uŋun teŋteŋɨni madepsi.
Yesu gen uŋun yaŋek burɨgwan da jɨgɨsi nandaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, jikon da kɨnda da nak uwal da kɨsiron nepdɨsak.”
Amɨn kɨnda mɨktɨm dakon yo morap kɨsi paŋ egakwan egɨp egɨpni pasɨl ɨmjak kaŋ, uŋun yo morap da arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋpulugoni. Egɨp egɨpni uŋun yo kɨnda naŋ arɨpmɨ dɨma yumjak, wagɨlsi pasɨl ɨmjak.
Gak jamba but amɨn. Mibɨltok gaga da dabɨlon kɨndap kwɨk tosok uŋun abɨ kɨŋakwan notgo da dabɨlon jɨmjɨmjok tosok uŋun kaŋbɨ pɨsaŋakwan tagɨ paki.
Aŋakwa Parisi amɨn gat gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat da yaŋba yokwi tok aŋek yaŋ yawit, “On amɨn yokwi pakpak amɨn not aŋyoban yɨgek jap noŋ.”
Amɨn morap nak do nandaŋek yutni, notni, sami, meŋi, datni, mɨŋat monjɨyoni, ae jap pini yopmaŋ detni, uŋun yo morapni kosirɨ 100 yaŋ tɨmɨk tɨmɨk akdaŋ. Yaŋ aŋek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokdaŋ.
Yo amɨn but nandak nandagon da wɨsak uŋun yaŋ: nandak nandak yokwi, yumabi aŋpak mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ, yo kabo, amɨn dapdap,
Kɨŋ altaŋek wain gat ae pakbi ɨsɨpmɨ kɨnda gat ɨktagɨlek ɨmɨŋba naŋ nandat aŋek nok do kurak tagɨt.
Kokup ŋwakŋwarɨkon da apbo yutjikon dɨma aŋkɨ nepgwit, ae ɨmalno mɨni egapbo ɨmal dɨma namgwit, ae sot agɨm ae dam teban yutnon yɨkgɨm bɨsapmon kɨlano dɨma awit.’
Nak Daron da mɨktɨmon pɨgɨm. Ae abɨsok mɨktɨm yɨpmaŋek Daron wɨgɨkdɨsat.”
Amɨn agɨpgwit gat akwaŋ bo yaŋ nandaŋek agakwal gɨldat kɨnda mudagɨt. Don dɨwatni ae notni agɨpgwit da bɨkbɨknikon wusɨgɨmal.
“Ae 10 tausen danari tɨmɨkgɨt amɨn uŋun da abɨŋ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Amɨn tagɨ, gak da 10 tausen danari kɨla akeŋ do namgul uŋun pini ako 10 tausen danari kɨnda gat oni noman tak.’
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Uŋun amɨn dukwan egɨsak?” Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Nak dɨma nandɨsat.”
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨsok kɨnda dɨmasi yaŋakwan Pailat da Yesu do nandaban ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Yaŋ nandaŋek Yesu do gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin dɨma nandamaŋ.” Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nakyo kɨsi namɨn da pi uŋun abeŋ do yaŋ mudaŋ namgut uŋun dɨma dayɨkeŋ.”
Uŋun da tɨlak ji abɨsok but yokwi aŋ. Mani aeno dandakeŋ bɨsapmon kɨsɨk kɨsɨk akdaŋ. Ae amɨn kɨnda da kɨsɨk kɨsɨkji arɨpmɨ dɨma gwayesak.
Yɨgakwa Yesu da tɨlak gen morapmɨ yoyɨŋek kɨnda yaŋ yagɨt,
Amɨn kɨnda Amɨn Dakon Monji do yaŋba yokwi tok asak kaŋ, Piŋkop da dɨwarɨni tagɨ wɨrɨrɨk ɨmjak. Mani amɨn kɨnda Telagɨ Wup do yaŋba yokwi tok asak kaŋ, Piŋkop da abɨsok on mɨktɨmon ae don bɨsap madepmon kɨsi dɨwarɨni uŋun dɨma wɨrɨrɨk ɨmdɨsak.”
Datno nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun da iyɨ pi asat uŋun joŋɨgek yaŋ teŋteŋok asak. Ji tekni bɨsap kɨnda dɨma nandawit, bo tomni bɨsap kɨnda dɨma kawit.
Yaŋ iyɨŋakwa amɨn kɨsi yutnikon kɨŋ kɨŋ awit.
Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Gen yaŋ gamaŋ amɨn da abɨŋ altaŋakwa gengo don nandakeŋ.” Yaŋ iyɨŋek obip amɨni yoyɨŋban Pol kɨla amɨn madep Erot da kalɨp yut madep agɨt uŋudon yɨpmaŋek kɨlani ani do yoyɨgɨt.
Don Apolos Akaia mɨktɨmon kɨk do nandak nandak aŋakwan Epesas paŋmuwukbi da burɨ aŋteban awit. Yaŋ aŋek papia kɨnda Akaia paŋmuwukbi da Apolos kwan tagɨsi abɨdoni do mandawit. Aŋakwa Apolos kɨŋ Akaia mɨktɨmon altaŋek amɨn da dabɨlon Juda amɨn dakon top geni pabɨŋ yopgut. Aŋek Piŋkop da papiakon gen toŋ uŋun paŋteŋteŋ aŋek Yesu uŋun asi Kristo yaŋ yoyɨgɨt. Yaŋ aŋek Piŋkop dakon nandaŋ yawotni do aŋek nandaŋ gadat awit amɨn uŋun madepsi paŋpulugagɨt.
Mani emat amɨn kɨnda da Yesu dakon gekgegɨ gwawia naŋ sugagɨt. Sugaŋban uŋudon gɨn pakbi yawiyo da pakgwit.
Yaŋban yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakbɨ kɨmotjak!”
Egek wain naŋ mudaŋba Yesu meŋi da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Wain kɨlɨ mudaŋ.”
Kɨŋ kaŋba tɨp madep tɨp kɨnam sopgut uŋun kɨlɨ aŋtobɨlba kɨgɨt kawit.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da ji tɨmɨgek tepmɨ damɨŋek dɨkba kɨmotdaŋ. Ae ji nak nolgaŋ do aŋek amɨn kɨsi morap da ji do butjap nandaŋ damdaŋ.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu da wasaŋek paŋdetni yoyɨŋ degek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji da tepmɨ madepsi pakdɨsak. Aŋakwan kɨla amɨn, ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat da manji ɨmɨŋek aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Kɨmagek gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Bɨsit aban dagaŋban abɨŋ pɨndakban paŋdetni dɨpmɨn do yokwisi aŋek aeni dɨpmɨn sigɨn pakgwit.
Yopmaŋ kɨŋakwan amɨn monjɨ uŋun abɨdaŋ yutnikon aŋkɨwit. Wagɨl dɨma kɨmakgɨt yaŋ nandaŋek butni yaworɨ tawit.
Yaŋ yaŋek Antiok paŋmuwukbi gat gɨldat morapmɨ egɨpgwit.
“Gen dayɨkdɨsat uŋun pakyaŋsi nandani. Amɨn Dakon Monji amɨn da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ.”
“Nin da nandaŋapno Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak da Piŋkop dakon Telagɨ Yut Madep uŋun tuwɨlek gɨldat kapbɨ da butgwan ae wɨtjɨkeŋ.’ ”
“Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae Parisi amɨn ji jamba but amɨnsi. Awa! Ji kap ɨdapyo dakon manji sugoŋ, mani burɨgwan da kabo ae sukwap nandak nandakyo tugawit da toŋ.
Amɨn da lam koleŋ kwoba baŋ dɨma wɨtjɨŋba toŋ. Kwen tamonikon yopba yut kagagwan amɨn ekwaŋ uŋun kɨsi teŋteŋaŋ yomaŋ.
Pɨdaŋ agakwan kombɨ amɨn Aisaia dakon papia ɨba abɨdaŋ wɨtdalek gen yaŋ naŋ manjɨgɨt:
Do ji abɨsok nido Piŋkop aŋkewalek paŋmuwukbi da kwapmon yo jɨgɨ yopmaŋgaŋ? Kalɨp babɨknin da Moses dakon gen teban uŋun guramɨt do aŋtɨdok awit, ae ninyo kɨsi uŋun guramɨt do aŋtɨdok amaŋ.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon ji dɨsi do kɨla ani. Amɨn da gen pikon depdaŋ ae Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon pawɨgɨ nap kɨrɨŋbaŋ baljokdaŋ. Ji nak nandaŋ namaŋ do amɨn da ji paŋkɨ mɨktɨm dakon kɨla amɨn madep da ɨŋamon depba atdaŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak dakon gen yoyɨni.
Gɨldat morapmɨ jap dɨma naŋek agɨpgwit. Don Pol da binapnikon agek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kabɨ, ji nak dakon gen guramɨkba Krit mɨktɨm tɨmon si egɨpgumaŋ tam, tap wakga dɨma yokwi taŋban, ae yo morap dɨma pasɨlbam.
Aŋek Jon dakon padɨge Jems emat agak sɨba naŋ aŋakban kɨmakgɨt.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo morap altokdɨsak uŋun dakon bɨsap amɨn kɨnda da dɨma nandɨsak. Kwen Kokup aŋeloyo dɨma nandaŋ, ae Monjɨyo kɨsi dɨma nandɨsak. Dat da iyɨ gɨn nandɨsak.
Kɨŋ Siria ae Silisia mɨktɨmon agek Pol da paŋmuwukbi morap yoyɨŋ paŋteban agɨt.
Aŋakwa kwen binap yo masɨ masɨmɨ uŋun dolɨko pɨndatni. Ae mɨktɨmon wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ ako bɨsap madep uŋun dakon tɨlak yaŋ pɨndatni. Yawi ae kɨndap ae mukwa madep altokdaŋ.
Ji gen teban on dayɨsat uŋun guramɨtni kaŋ, ji nak dakon notnoni kabɨ akdaŋ.
Uŋun kokupmon amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut mani Sakius. Sakius uŋun takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn dakon amɨn madep kɨnda egɨpgut. Uŋun yoni morapmɨ amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut.
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Nin niaŋsi aŋek Piŋkop dakon pi aneŋ?”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban Liwai pɨdaŋ yo morapni kɨsi yopmaŋek Yesu yolgɨt.
Wɨgakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat ae Juda amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn gat da Pestuskon kɨŋek Pol gen yaŋ ɨmgwit uŋun do iyɨwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji butji dɨma jɨk toni. Egɨp egɨpji Piŋkopmon tosok yaŋsi nandani, ae egɨp egɨpji nagon tosok yaŋsi nandaŋ namni.
Don Pol Atens yɨpmaŋek Korin kokup papmon kɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek burɨ pɨsawit. Bret dakon yis do dɨma yosok, Parisi gat ae Sadyusi amɨn gat dakon yoyɨŋdetni toptopmɨ do kaŋ kɨmotneŋ do yosok yaŋ nandawit.
Damaskus kokup papmon Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgut amɨn kɨnda egɨpgut mani Ananias. Uŋun amɨn burɨ pɨsaŋakwan dɨpmɨn yombem kɨnda kaŋakwan Amɨn Tagɨ da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Ananias!” Yaŋ iyɨŋban yagɨt, “Amɨn Tagɨ, nak oni.”
“Yaŋban notni yutgwan da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨsak, ‘Jɨgɨ dɨma nabi. Pɨdaŋek arɨpmɨ dɨma gabeŋ. Yoma beŋgan kɨlɨ at, ae gwakno gat kɨlɨ pak mudamaŋ.’
Uŋun do aŋek nin gak do but galaksi nandaŋek ya yaŋsi gayamaŋ.
Bɨsit aŋek abɨŋ pɨndakban paŋdetni dɨpmɨn do yokwisi aŋek aeni dɨpmɨn sigɨn pakgwit. Paŋyolban pɨdaŋ ni gen naŋ iyɨneŋ yaŋ do ɨŋtaŋek ɨsal yɨkgwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da mɨŋat monjɨyoni Yesu da kɨsitni kwenikon wutjɨŋek bɨsit aŋyomjak do paŋopgwit. Paŋopba paŋdetni da dɨma paŋopni do tebai yoyɨwit.
“Wain sop pakpak bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan oman monjɨ kɨnda yabekban wain bamɨ tɨmɨk paŋopjak do kɨgɨt.
Mani Elisabet monjɨ suŋ egɨpgut, do ɨsal egek mɨŋat amɨn pelaŋyo agɨmal.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, nandaŋ gadat asak amɨn uŋun egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do amɨn asak.
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yagɨt, “Moses uŋun but tebanji do aŋek gen teban uŋun mandagɨt.
Mani yo yokwi aŋ yomni amɨn nak da don kobogɨ yokwi aŋ yobeŋ. Yaŋ aŋapbo yawi dɨwatgo da mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋek obɨŋ on mɨktɨmon nak gawak namni.’
Piŋkop da amɨn kɨlegɨ ae yokwiyo kɨsi don kɨmoron baŋ paban pɨdokdaŋ uŋun do nandaŋ teban taŋek egɨsat. On amɨnyo kɨsi yaŋ gɨn nandaŋek ekwaŋ.
Ji da gen tebanon gen yaŋ tosok, Amɨn bamorɨ da gen kaloŋɨ naŋgɨn yaŋkwok amal kaŋ, uŋun da gen bamɨ asak.
Yaŋ yaŋban gen aeni iyɨgɨt, “Yo Piŋkop da paŋmɨlɨp aban yo tagɨsi aŋ uŋun gak da dɨma noknogɨ yaŋ dɨma yoki.”
Yaŋ tɨdaŋakwa uŋudon gɨn Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji si teban taŋek egɨpni. Nak naga abɨsat. Dɨma pasolni.”
Kɨŋ 3 kilok aŋakwan Yesu da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Eloi, eloi lama sabaktani?” Gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ yaŋ: “Piŋkopno, Piŋkopno, nido nepmaŋ dekdal?”
Amɨn bamot Debe kokup papmon Gen Bin Tagɨsi yoyɨŋ teŋteŋaŋakwal amɨn morapmɨsi da Yesu nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit. Aŋek uŋudon da tobɨl Lista ae Ikoniam ae Antiok kɨgɨmal.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, kombɨ amɨn morap kokup kaloŋni da geni dɨma nandaŋ yomaŋ.
Uŋudeŋ gɨn Sunduk da pudaŋ kɨ kabi bamot aŋek iyɨ emat wamjil kaŋ, amɨn kabɨni tebai dɨma egɨpdaŋ. Yaŋ ani kaŋ pasɨl mudokdaŋ.
Paŋdetni gen uŋun nandaŋek mɨktɨmon maŋ pagek madepsi pasal nɨmnɨmɨkgwit.
Jon telagɨ pakbi sogɨt bɨsapmon, Piŋkop da yabekban pi agɨt, bo amɨn da yabekba agɨt? Uŋun do nayɨni.”
Aŋakwan Yesu dakon ɨmalni kwakwagɨsi teŋteŋagɨt. Uŋun mɨktɨm amɨn kɨnda da arɨpmɨ dɨma agagɨ, kwakwagɨsi agɨt.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak gen teban ae kombɨ amɨn dakon gen abo kɨŋ ɨsalɨ asak do dɨma pɨgɨm. Gen teban ae kombɨ amɨn dakon gen bamɨ toŋ aŋmudoni do pɨgɨm.
“Yaŋban yoni morapmɨ amɨn da yagɨt, ‘Abraham dat, uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma. Mani amɨn kɨmakbi kɨnda da kɨŋ altaŋ yomjak kaŋ, padɨk padɨkno da but tobɨl tagɨ ani.’
Jiyo yaŋ gɨn, Piŋkop da oman morap ani do dayɨgɨt uŋun aŋ mudaŋek yaŋ gɨn yoni, ‘Nin oman monjɨ do, ɨsal pinin gɨn amaŋ.’ ”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋba amɨn kɨsi muwut muwut yut yɨpmaŋek yomakon pɨgɨwit. Pɨgakwa Juda amɨn morapmɨ gat ae Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨkon nani morapmɨ Juda amɨnon saŋbeŋek Piŋkop but dasi gawak ɨmgwit amɨn gat kɨsi Pol gat Banabas gat yolgwit. Yolakwa amɨn bamot da Piŋkop dakon nandaŋ yawotni do nandaŋek tebaisi agek egɨ aŋaŋ kɨni do yoyɨŋ paŋteban agɨmal.
Yaŋ abo Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ morap naga do kɨlɨ manjɨgɨm uŋun da Amɨn Tagɨni nak wɨsɨni.” ’ Gen uŋun Amɨn Tagɨ da kalɨpsigwan kɨlɨ yagɨt.”
Amɨn uŋun 12 kabɨ da tɨlak da awit.
Uŋun bɨsapmonsi ni gen baŋ yoyɨni uŋun Telagɨ Wup da dayɨŋ detdɨsak.”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban aŋopba Yesu da koŋ uŋun gen tebaisi iyɨŋban wɨŋ abɨgɨŋakwan uŋun bɨsapmon gɨn monji uŋun kɨlek tagɨt.
Pakbi yɨpmaŋek wɨŋakwal uŋudon gɨn Amɨn Tagɨ dakon Wup da Pilip aŋaŋ kɨgɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn madep uŋun saŋbeŋek Pilip dɨma kagɨt. Mɨni kagɨt mani amɨn uŋun kɨsɨk kɨsɨk aŋek aeni tamonikon pawɨŋ yɨgek kɨgɨt.
Yaŋban Samaria mɨŋat da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Juda amɨn kɨnda, ae nak Samaria mɨŋat kɨnda, do nido pakbi nabɨ noko yaŋ nayɨsal?” (Mɨŋat uŋun mibɨlɨ yaŋ do yagɨt, Juda amɨn da Samaria amɨn gat not dɨma aŋek egɨpgwit.)
Gapman dakon kɨla amɨn madep mibɨltogɨ Erot da Yesu dakon gen bini nandagɨt. Dɨ da Yesu kaŋek Jon kɨmoron da aeni pɨdagɨt yaŋ yawit, do Erot but morap agɨt.
Bamɨ taŋakwa pi ami da bamɨ pasak.”
Yoba tɨmɨk amɨn morap kɨsisi arɨpmɨsi naŋakwa jap nawit dakon dɨwarɨ tawit uŋun paŋdetni da sɨmɨlba yɨgɨ 12 yaŋsi tugawit.
Amɨn morapmɨ da abɨŋ nak dakon man yaŋek yaŋ yokdaŋ, ‘Nak naga Kristo.’ Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn morapmɨ paŋkewaldaŋ.
“Yaŋdo, nak yaŋ dayɨsat: Ji Piŋkop bɨsit iyɨŋba tagɨ damdɨsak, ae wɨsɨŋek bamɨ kokdaŋ, ae yoma domon tɨdaŋba wɨtdal damdɨsak.
Aŋek ɨmal naŋ dabɨlɨ wamaŋ sopmaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Uŋun namɨn da gɨkdak yaŋ do kombɨ gen yaŋ ka!”
Yaŋ yaŋban Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn dakon paŋdetni da abɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin gat ae Parisi amɨn gat Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egapno gak dakon paŋdet kabɨgo nido yaŋ dɨma aŋ?”
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Bɨsap pɨsɨpmɨsok nak saŋbeŋek ae dɨma nandakdaŋ. Ae tɨmɨsok dɨ egek donjok nandakdaŋ.”
“Pi ɨsalni uŋun geni nandaŋek ŋwakbeŋ aŋ ɨmɨŋek bɨsit tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, ‘Butgo yaworɨ taŋakwan egaki don gomango gabeŋ.’
Yesu da saŋbeŋek amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak depmaŋ kɨko ji nak wɨsɨkdaŋ, mani yokwisi taŋ damɨŋakwa kɨmotdaŋ. Nak da kɨkeŋon arɨpmɨ dɨma apni.”
Juda amɨn gen uŋun nandaŋek aeni waseŋ kɨ kabi bamorɨ awit.
